prāha sarva dṛś mad bhavataḥ bhāvam ātmānam ca api śaṃkaraiḥ devāḥ saha ṛṣibhiḥ ca āsan tatra sāhāyya kāriṇaḥ vināśaya āśu tam yajñam varam ekam vṛṇomi aham evam vijñāpitaḥ devyā devaḥ deva varaḥ prabhuḥ sasarja sahasā rudram dakṣa yajña jighāṃsayā sahastra śīrṣa pādam ca sahastra akṣam mahā bhujam sahastra pāṇim durdharṣam yuga anta anala saṃnibham daṃṣṭra karālam duṣprekṣyam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam daṇḍa hastam mahā nādam śārṅgiṇam bhūtibhūṣaṇam sa jāta mātraḥ deveśam upatasthe kṛtāñjaliḥ tam āha dakṣasya makham vināśaya śivoḥ tu iti vinindya mām sa yajate gaṅgādvāre gaṇeśvara vīrabhadreṇa dakṣasya vināśam agamat kratuḥ manyunā ca umayā sṛṣṭā bhadrakālī maheśvarī tayā ca sārdham vṛṣabham samāruhya yayau gaṇaḥ anye sahastraśas rudrāḥ nisṛṣṭāḥ tena dhīmatā roma jāḥ iti vikhyātāḥ tasya sāhāyya kāriṇaḥ śūla śakti gadā hastāḥ ṭaṅka upala karāḥ tathā tad kālāgni rudra saṃkāśāḥ nādayantaḥ diśaḥ daśa sarve vṛṣa āsana ārūḍhāḥ sa bhāryāḥ ca ati bhīṣaṇāḥ samāvṛtya gaṇa śreṣṭham yayuḥ dakṣa makham prati sarve tam deśam gaṅgādvāram iti śrutam dadṛśuḥ yajña deśam tam dakṣasya amita tejasaḥ deva aṅganā sahastra āḍhyam apsaraḥ gīta nāditam vīṇā veṇu nināda āḍhyam veda vāda abhināditam dṛṣṭvā saha ṛṣibhiḥ devaiḥ samāsīnam prajāpatim vayam hi anucarāḥ sarve śarvasya amita tejasaḥ bhāga abhilapsayā prāptāḥ bhāgān yacchadhvam īpsitān tam brūta ājñāpayati yaḥ vetsyāmaḥ hi vayam tatas evam uktā gaṇeśena prajāpati puras sarāḥ mantrāḥ ūcuḥ surān yūyam tama upahata cetasaḥ ye na adhvarasya rājānam pūjayadhvam maheśvaram īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām sarva bhūta tanuḥ haraḥ evam uktāḥ api īśānam māyayā naṣṭa cetasaḥ tatas sa rudraḥ bhagavān sa bhāryaḥ sa gaṇeśvaraḥ spṛśan karābhyām brahmarṣi dadhīcam prāha devatāḥ mantrāḥ pramāṇam na kṛtāḥ yuṣmābhiḥ bala garvitaiḥ iti uktvā yajña śālām tām dadāha gaṇa puṃgavaḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ ca saṃkruddhāḥ yūpān utpāṭya cikṣipuḥ prastotrā saha hotrā ca aśvam ca eva gaṇeśvarāḥ gṛhītvā bhīṣaṇāḥ sarve gaṅgāḥ trotasi cikṣipuḥ vyaṣṭambhayat adīna ātmā tathā anyeṣām divaukasām bhagasya netre ca utpāṭya karaja agreṇa līlayā nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaḥ ca evam apātayat tathā candramasam devam pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā dharṣayāmāsa balavān smayamānaḥ gaṇeśvaraḥ vahneḥ hasta dvayam chittvā jihvām utpāṭya līlayā jaghāna mūrdhani pādena munīn api muni īśvarāḥ tathā viṣṇum saharuḍam samāyāntam mahā balaḥ vivyādha niśā itaiḥ bāṇaiḥ stambhayitvā sudarśanam samālokya mahā bāhuḥ āgatya garuḍaḥ gaṇam jaghāna pakṣaiḥ sahasā nanāda ambunidhiḥ yathā tān dṛṣṭvā garuḍaḥ dhīmān palāyata mahā javaḥ āgatya vārayāmāsa vīrabhadram ca keśavam prasādayāmāsa ca tam gauravāt parameṣṭhinaḥ saṃstūya bhagavant īśaḥ sa ambaḥ tatra agamat svayam vīkṣya deva adhidevam tam sa ambam sarva gaṇaiḥ vṛtam tuṣṭāva bhagavān brahmā dakṣaḥ sarve divaukasaḥ viśeṣāt pārvatīm devīm īśvara ardha śarīriṇīm stotraiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ dakṣaḥ praṇamya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ prasanna mānasā rudram vacaḥ prāha ghṛṇā nidhiḥ tvam eva jagataḥ straṣṭā śāsitā ca eva rakṣakaḥ anugrāhyaḥ bhagavatā dakṣaḥ ca api divaukasaḥ uvāca praṇatān devān prācetasam atho haraḥ saṃpūjyaḥ sarva yajñeṣu na nindyaḥ aham viśeṣataḥ tvam ca api śṛṇu me dakṣa vacanam sarva rakṣaṇam tyaktvā loka eṣaṇām etām mad bhaktaḥ bhava yatnatas bhaviṣyasi gaṇeśānaḥ kalpa ante anugrahān mama tāvat tiṣṭha mama ādeśāt sva adhikāreṣu nirvṛtaḥ evam uktvā sa bhagavān sa patnīkaḥ saha anugaḥ vyājahāra svayam dakṣam aśeṣa jagantaḥ hitam yat ācaṣṭa svayam devaḥ pālaya etat atandritaḥ sarveṣām eva bhūtānām hṛdi eṣa vasati īśvaraḥ paśyanti enam brahma bhūtāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ veda vādinaḥ saḥ ātmā sarva bhūtānām sa bījam paramā gatiḥ tasmāt anādi madhya antam vijñāya parameśvaram karmaṇā manasā vācā samārādhaya yatnatas yatnāt parihara īśasya nindām ātma vināśanīm yaḥ tava eṣa mahā yogī rakṣakaḥ viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ manyante ye jagadyonim vibhinnam viṣṇum īśvarāt mohāt a veda niṣṭha tvāt te yānti narakam narāḥ veda anuvartinaḥ rudram devam nārāyaṇam tathā yaḥ viṣṇuḥ sa svayam rudraḥ yaḥ rudraḥ sa janārdanaḥ sṛjati etat jagat sarvam viṣṇuḥ tat paśyati īśvaraḥ tasmāt tyaktvā hareḥ nindām viṣṇau api samāhitaḥ samāśrayet mahādevam śaraṇyam brahma vādinām upaśrutyā atha vacanam viriñcasya prajāpatiḥ magāma śaraṇam devam gopatim kṛttivāsasam ye anye śāpa agni nirdagdhāḥ dadhīcasya mahā ṛṣayaḥ dviṣantaḥ mohitāḥ devam saṃbabhūvuḥ kaliṣu atha tyaktvā tapaḥ balam kṛtsnam viprāṇām kula saṃbhavāḥ pūrva saṃskāra mahātmyāt brahmanaḥ vacanāt iha mukta śāpāḥ tatas sarve kalpa ante raurava ādiṣu nipātyamānāḥ kālena saṃprāpya āditya varcasam brahmānam jagatām īśam anujñātāḥ svayambhunā samārādhya tapaḥ yogāt īśānam tridaśādhipam bhaviṣyanti yathā pūrvam śaṃkarasya prasādāt etat vaḥ kathitam sarvam dakṣa yajña niṣūdanam śṛṇudhvam dakṣa putrīṇām sarvāsām ca eva saṃtatim iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca prajāḥ sṛja iti vyādiṣṭaḥ pūrvam dakṣaḥ svayambhunā sasarja devān gandharvān ṛṣīn ca eva asura uragān yadā asya sṛjamānasya na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ asiknyām janayāmāsa vīraṇasya prajāpateḥ sutāyām dharma yuktāyām putrāṇām tu sahastrakam teṣu putreṣu naṣṭeṣu māyayā nāradasya saḥ masṛjat kanyāḥ vairaṇyām vai prajāpatiḥ dve ca eva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate arundhatī vasuḥ jāmī lambā bhānuḥ marutvatī saṃkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca bhāminī viśvāyāḥ viśva devāḥ tu sādhyā sādhyān ajījanat marutvantaḥ marutvatyām vasavaḥ aṣṭau vasoḥ sutāḥ bhānvaḥ tu bhānavaḥ ca eva muhūrtāḥ vai muhūrtajāḥ lambāyāḥ ca atha ghoṣaḥ vai nāgavīthī tu jāmī jā pṛthivī viṣayam sarvam arundatyām ajāyata saṃkalpāyāḥ tu saṃkalpaḥ dharma putrāḥ daśa smṛtāḥ mahā apaḥ dhruvaḥ ca somaḥ ca dharaḥ ca eva anilaḥ analaḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭa prakīrtitāḥ mahā apasya putraḥ vaitaṇḍyaḥ śramaḥ śrāntaḥ dhuniḥ tathā kumāraḥ hi analasya āsīt senāpatiḥ iti smṛtaḥ devalaḥ bhagavān yogī pratyūṣasya abhavat sutaḥ viśvakarmā prabhāsasya śilpa kartā prajāpatiḥ aṃśaḥ dhātā bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā mitraḥ atha varuṇaḥ ayamā vivasvant savitā pūṣā hi aṃśumant viṣṇuḥ eva ca tuṣitāḥ nāma te pūrvam cākṣuṣasya antare manoḥ vaivasvate antare proktāḥ ādityāḥ ca adityāḥ sutāḥ hiraṇyakaśipum jyeṣṭham hiraṇyākṣam tathā aparam mārādhya tapasā devam brahmāṇam parameṣṭhinam dṛṣṭvā ālebhe varān divyān stutvā asau vividhaiḥ stavai bādhitāḥ tāḍitāḥ jagmuḥ devadevam pitāmaham śaraṇyam śaraṇam devam śaṃbhum sarva jagat mayam brahmāṇam lokakartāram trātāram puruṣam param kūṭastham jagatām ekam purāṇam puruṣottamam sa yācitaḥ deva varaiḥ munibhiḥ ca muni īśvarāḥ kṣīrodasya uttaram kūlam yatra āste hariḥ īśvaraḥ dṛṣṭvā devam jagadyonim viṣṇum viśva gurum śivam vavande caraṇau mūrdhanā kṛtāñjaliḥ abhāṣata tvam gatiḥ sarva bhūtānām anantaḥ asi akhila ātmakaḥ vyāpī sarva amara vapūḥ mahā yogī sanātanaḥ tvam ātmā sarva bhūtānām pradhānam prakṛtiḥ parā vairāgya aiśvarya nirataḥ rāga atītaḥ nirañjanaḥ trātum arhasi ananta īśa trātā hi parameśvaraḥ ittham sa viṣṇuḥ bhagavant brahmaṇā saṃprabodhitaḥ provāca unnidra padma akṣaḥ pīta vāsā suradviṣaḥ kimartham su mahā vīryāḥ sa prajāpatikāḥ surāḥ imam deśam anuprāptāḥ kim vā kāryam karomi vaḥ ūcuḥ avadhyaḥ sarva bhūtānām tvām ṛte puruṣottama hantum arhasi sarveṣām tvam trātā asi jagat maya śrutvā tat daivataiḥ uktam sa viṣṇuḥ loka bhāvanaḥ meru parvata varṣmāṇam ghora rūpam bhayānakam śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇim tam prāha garuḍadhvajaḥ hatvā tam daitya rājam tvam hiraṇyakaśipum punar imam deśam samāgantum kṣipram arhasi pauruṣāt niśamya vaiṣṇavam vākyam praṇamya puruṣottamam vimuñcan bhairavam nādam śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ bhāruhya garuḍam devaḥ mahā meruḥ iva aparaḥ samācacakṣire nādam tadā daitya pateḥ bhayāt ūcuḥ muñcan bhairavam nādam tam jānīmaḥ amara ardanaiḥ saṃnaddhaiḥ sa āyudhaiḥ putraiḥ prahrāda ādyaiḥ tadā yayau dṛṣṭvā tam garuḍa āsīnam sūrya koṭi sama prabham puruṣam parvata ākāram nārāyaṇam iva aparam dudruvuḥ kecid anyaḥ mamūcuḥ saṃbhrānta locanāḥ ayam sa devaḥ devānām goptā nārāyaṇaḥ ripuḥ nūnam tad sutaḥ vā samāgataḥ iti uktvā śastra varṣāṇi sasṛjuḥ puruṣāya te tāni ca aśeṣatas devaḥ nāśayāmāsa līlayā tadā hiraṇyakaśipoḥ catvāraḥ prathita ojasaḥ putrāḥ nārāyaṇa udbhūtam yuyudhuḥ megha niḥ svanāḥ prahrādaḥ ca api anuhrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ hrādaḥ eva ca prahrādaḥ prāhiṇot brāhmam anuhrādaḥ atha vaiṣṇavam saṃhrādaḥ ca api kaumāram āgneyam hrādaḥ eva ca tāni tam puruṣam prāpya catvāri astrāṇi vaiṣṇavam na śekuḥ bādhitum viṣṇum vāsudevam yathā tathā atha asau caturaḥ putrān mahā bāhuḥ mahā balaḥ pragṛhya pādeṣu karaiḥ saṃcikṣepa nanāda ca pādena tāḍayāmāsa vegena urasi tam balī sa tena pīḍitaḥ atyartham garuḍena tathā āśu gaḥ adṛśyaḥ prayayau tūrṇam yatra nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ gatvā vijñāpayāmāsa pravṛttam akhilam tathā saṃcintya manasā devaḥ sarva jñāna mayaḥ amalaḥ narasya ardha tanum kṛtvā siṃhasya ardha tanum tathā daṃṣṭra karālaḥ yoga ātmā yugānta dahana upamaḥ samāruhya ātmanaḥ śaktim sarva saṃhāra kārakām bhāti nārāyaṇaḥ anantaḥ yathā madhyaṃdine raviḥ dṛṣṭvā prahrādam jyeṣṭha putrakam imam nṛsiṃha vapuṣam pūrvasmāt bahu śaktikam saha eva tu anujaiḥ sarvaiḥ nāśaya āśu mayā īritaḥ tad saṃniyogāt asuraḥ prahrādaḥ viṣṇum avyayam tatas saṃcoditaḥ daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ tadā anujaḥ na hānim akarot astram yathā devasya śūlinaḥ dṛṣṭvā parāhatam tu astram prahrādaḥ bhāgya gauravāt mene sarva ātmakam devam vāsudevam sanātanam tat tat tat tat tat yoginām hṛdayeśayam stutvā nārāyaṇaiḥ stotraiḥ ṛc yajuḥ sāma saṃbhavaiḥ nivārya pitaram bhrātṝn hiraṇyākṣam tadā bravīt ayam nārāyaṇaḥ anantaḥ śāśvataḥ bhagavān ajaḥ purāṇapuruṣaḥ devaḥ mahāyogī jagat mayaḥ ayam dhātā vidhātā ca svayam jyotiḥ nirañjanaḥ īśvaraḥ sarva bhūtānām antaryāmī guṇa atigaḥ provāca putram atyartham mohitaḥ viṣṇu māyayā ayam sarva ātmanā vadhyaḥ nṛsiṃhaḥ alpa parākramaḥ samāgataḥ asmad bhavanam idānīm kāla coditaḥ mā nindasva enam īśānam bhūtānām ekam avyayam katham devaḥ mahādevaḥ śāśvataḥ kāla varjitaḥ kālena hanyate viṣṇuḥ kāla ātmā kāla rūpadhṛk tatas suvarṇakaśipuḥ durātmā vidhi coditaḥ hate hiraṇyakaśipau hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā balaḥ anuhrāda ādayaḥ putrāḥ anye ca śataśas asurāḥ nṛsiṃha deha saṃbhūtaiḥ siṃhaiḥ notāḥ yama ālayam tatas saṃhṛtya tad rūpam hariḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ svam eva paramam rūpam yayau nārāyaṇa āhvayam gate nārāyaṇe daityaḥ prahrādaḥ asura sattamaḥ sa bādhayāmāsa surān raṇe jitvā munīn api labdhvā andhakam mahā putram tapasā ārādhya śaṃkaram devān jitvā sa deva indrān badhvā aca dharaṇīm imām nītvā rasātalam cakre vandīm indīvara prabhām tatas sa brahmakāḥ devāḥ parimlāna mukha śriyaḥ gatvā vijñāpayāmāsuḥ viṣṇave hari mandiram sa cintayitvā viśvātmā tad vadha upāyam avyayaḥ sarvedeva mayam śubhram vārāham vapuḥ ādadhe gatvā hiraṇyanayanam hatvā tam puruṣottamaḥ daṃṣṭrayā uddhārayāmāsa kalpa ādau dharaṇīm imām tyaktvā varāha saṃsthānam saṃsthāpya ca sura dvijān svām eva prakṛtim divyām yayau viṣṇuḥ param padam apālayat svakam rājyam bhāvam tyaktvā tadā asuram iyāja vidhivat devān viṣṇoḥ ārādhane rataḥ niḥ sapatnam tadā rājyam tasya āsīt viṣṇu vaibhavāt tatas kadācid asuraḥ brāhmaṇam gṛham āgatam tāpasam na arcayāmāsa devānām ca eva māyayā śaśāpa asura rājānam krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ yat tat valam samāśritya brāhmaṇān avamanyase sā bhaktiḥ vaiṣṇavā divyā vināśam te gamiṣyati iti uktvā prayayau tūrṇam prahrādasya gṛhāt dvijaḥ mumoha rājya saṃsaktaḥ saḥ api śāpa balāt tatas nārāyaṇasya devasya prahrādasya amara dviṣaḥ kṛtvā tu su mahat yuddham viṣṇunā tena nirjitaḥ saṃjātam tasya vijñānam śaraṇyam śaraṇam yayau nārāyaṇe mahā yogam avāpa puruṣottame mandara sthām umām devīm cakame parvatātmajām īśvara ārādhana arthāya tapaḥ ceruḥ sahastraśas anāvṛṣṭiḥ atīva ugrā hi āsīt bhūta vināśinī yācanta kṣudhā āviṣṭāḥ āhāram prāṇa dhāraṇam sa tebhyaḥ pradadau annam mṛṣṭam bahutaram budhaḥ gate tu dvādaśe varṣe kalpa ante iva śaṅkarī babhūva vṛṣṭiḥ mahatī yathāpūrvam abhūt jagant nivārayāmāsa ca tān kañcid kālam yathāsukham uṣitvā mad gṛhe avaśyam gacchadhvam iti paṇḍitāḥ tatas māyā mayīm sṛṣṭvā kṛśām gām sarve eva te samīpam prāpayāmāsu gautamasya mahātmanaḥ saḥ anuvīkṣya kṛpā āviṣṭaḥ tasyāḥ saṃrakṣaṇa utsukaḥ goṣṭhe tām bandhayāmāsa spṛṣṭa mātrā mamāra sā sa śokena abhisaṃtaptaḥ kārya akāryam mahā muniḥ na paśyati sma sahasā tādṛśam munayaḥ abruvan go vadhyā iyam dvijaśreṣṭha yāvat tava śarīra gā jagmuḥ pāpa vaśam nītāḥ tapaḥ cartum yathā purā sa teṣām māyayā jātām go vadhyām gautamaḥ muniḥ kena api hetunā jñātvā śaśāpa atīva kopanaḥ bhaviṣyanti trayī bāhyāḥ mahāpātakibhiḥ samāḥ babhūvuḥ te tathā śāpāt jāyamānāḥ punar punar sarve saṃprāpya deveśam śaṃkaram viṣṇum avyayam devadevau mahādevau bhaktānām ārti nāśanau kāma vṛttyā mahā yogau pāpāt naḥ trātum arhathaḥ tadā pārśva sthitam viṣṇum saṃprekṣya vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ kim eteṣām bhavet kāryam prāha puṇya eṣiṇām iti tatas sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaraṇyaḥ bhakta vatsalaḥ gopatim prāha vipra indrān ālokya praṇatān hariḥ na veda bāhye puruṣe puṇya leśaḥ api śaṃkara tasmāt vai veda bāhyānām rakṣaṇa arthāya pāpinām bhaviṣyāmaḥ vimohanāya śāstrāṇi kariṣyāmaḥ vṛṣadhvaja evam saṃbodhitaḥ rudraḥ mādhavena murāriṇā cakāra moha śāstrāṇi keśavaḥ api śiva īritaḥ kāpālam nākulam vāmam bhairavam pūrva paścimam pañcarātram pāśupatam tathā anyāni sahastraśas sṛṣṭvā tān ūcatuḥ devau kurvāṇāḥ śāstra coditam jāyantaḥ mānuṣe loke kṣīṇa pāpa cayāḥ tatas īśvara ārādhana balāt gacchadhvam su kṛtām gatim mad prasādena na anyathā niṣkṛtiḥ hi vaḥ evam īśvara viṣṇubhyām coditāḥ te mahā ṛṣayaḥ mad ādeśam pratyapadyanta śirasā asura vidviṣoḥ cakruḥ te anyāni śāstrāṇi tatra tatra ratāḥ punar śiṣyān adhyāpayāmāsuḥ darśayitvā phalāni tu cakāra śaṃkaraḥ bhikṣām hitāya eṣām dvijaiḥ saha kapāla mālā ābharaṇaḥ preta bhasma avaguṇṭhitaḥ vimohayan lokam imam jaṭā maṇḍala maṇḍitaḥ nikṣipya pārvatīm devīm viṣṇau amita tejasi niyojya aṅga bhavam rudram bhairavam duṣṭa nigrahe dattvā nārāyaṇe devīm nandinam kula nandinam strī rūpa dhārī niyatam sevate sma maheśvarīm brahmā hutāśanaḥ śakraḥ yamaḥ anye sura puṃgavāḥ siṣevire mahādevīm strī veśam śobhanam gatāḥ nandīśvaraḥ ca bhagavān śaṃbhoḥ atyanta vallabhaḥ dvāra deśe gaṇādhyakṣaḥ yathāpūrvam atiṣṭhata mandaram saṃprāptam andhakam dṛṣṭvā śaṅkaraḥ kālabhairavaḥ nyaṣedhayat ameya ātmā kāla rūpa dharaḥ haraḥ śūlena urasi tam daityam ājaghāna vṛṣadhvajaḥ tatas sahastraśas daityaḥ sasarja andhaka saṃjñitān sarve andhakam daitya varam saṃprāpya ati bala anvitāḥ bhūla śakti ṛṣṭi giri kūṭa paraśvadhaiḥ bhrāmayitvā atha hastābhyām gṛhīta caraṇa dvayāḥ daitya indreṇa ati balinā kṣiptāḥ te śata yojanam tatas andhaka nisṛṣṭāḥ te śataśas atha sahastraśas kālasūrya pratīkāśāḥ bhairavam tu abhidudruvuḥ mahān babhūva ati bhayaṅkaraḥ yuyodha bhairavaḥ rudraḥ śūlam ādāya bhīṣaṇam dṛṣṭvā andhakānām su balam durjayam tarjitaḥ haraḥ ca gāma śaraṇam devam vāsudevam ajam vibhum saḥ asṛjat bhagavān viṣṇuḥ devīnām śatam uttamam devī pārśva sthitaḥ devaḥ vināśāya amaradviṣām nītam keśava māhātmyāt līlayā eva raṇa ajire dṛṣṭvā parāhatam sainyam andhakaḥ api mahā asuraḥ parāṅmukhaḥ uraṇāt tasmāt palāyata mahā javaḥ tatas krīḍām mahādevaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśa vārṣikīm hitāya loke bhaktānām ājagāma atha mandaram saṃprāptam īśvaram jñātvā sarve eva gaṇeśvarāḥ praviśya bhavanam puṇyam ayuktānām durāsadam dadarśa nandinam devam bhairavam keśavam śivaḥ praṇāma pravaṇam devam saḥ anugṛhya atha nandinam mūrdhani īśānaḥ keśavam pariṣasvaje dṛṣṭvā devī mahādevam prīti visphārita īkṣaṇā śirasā tasya pādayoḥ īśvarasya sā nivedya vijayam tasmai śaṅkarāya atha śaṃkarī bhairavaḥ viṣṇu māhātmyam praṇataḥ pārśva gaḥ avadat śrutvā tad vijayam śaṃbhuḥ vikramam keśavasya ca samāste bhagavant īśaḥ devyā saha varāsane tatas deva gaṇāḥ sarve marīci pramukhāḥ dvijāḥ yena tat vijitam pūrvam devīnām śatam uttamam samāgatam daitya sainyam īś darśana vāñchayā dṛṣṭvā varāsana āsīnam devyā candra vibhūṣaṇam praṇemuḥ ādarāt devyaḥ gāyanti sma ati lālasāḥ praṇemuḥ girijām devīm vāma pārśve pinākinaḥ deva āsana gatam devam nārāyaṇam anāmayam dṛṣṭvā siṃhāsana āsīnam devyā nārāyaṇena ca praṇamya devam īśānam pṛṣṭavatyaḥ vara aṅganāḥ ūcuḥ kaḥ tvam vibhrājase kāntyā kā iyam bāla ravi prabhā kaḥ anu ayam vapuṣā paṅkaja āyata locanaḥ niśamya tāsām vacanam vṛṣa indra vara vāhanaḥ vyājahāra mahā yogī bhūta adhipatiḥ avyayaḥ aham nārāyaṇaḥ gaurī jaganmātā sanātanī vibhajya saṃsthitaḥ devaḥ sva ātmānam bahudhā īśvaraḥ na me viduḥ param tattvam deva ādyāḥ na mahā ṛṣayaḥ ekaḥ ayam veda viśvātmā bhavānī viṣṇuḥ eva ca aham hi niṣkriyaḥ śāntaḥ kevalaḥ niṣparigrahaḥ mām eva keśavam devam āhuḥ devīm atha ambikām eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca kāraṇam kāryam eva ca bhoktā pumān aprameyaḥ saṃhartā kāla rūpadhṛk ha straṣṭā pātā vāsudevaḥ viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ hi akṣaraḥ vyāpī yogī nārāyaṇaḥ svayam tārakaḥ puruṣaḥ hi ātmā kevalam paramam padam sā eṣā māheśvarī gaurī mama śaktiḥ nirañjanā sa antā satyā sat ānandā param padam iti śrutiḥ eṣā eva sarva bhūtānām gatīnām uttamā gatiḥ tayā aham saṃgataḥ devyā kevalaḥ niṣkalaḥ paraḥ tasmāt anādim advaitam viṣṇum ātmānam īśvaram manyante viṣṇum avyaktam ātmānam śraddhayā anvitāḥ ye bhinna dṛṣṭyā api īśānam pūjayantaḥ na mama priyāḥ dviṣanti ye jagat sūtim mohitāḥ raurava ādiṣu rakṣakaḥ viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ śrutvā bhagavataḥ vākyam devyaḥ sarva gaṇeśvarāḥ nemuḥ nārāyaṇam devam devīm ca himaśailajām prārthayāmāsuḥ īśāne bhaktim bhakta jana priye bhavānī pāda yugale nārāyaṇa pada ambuje tatas nārāyaṇam devam gaṇeśāḥ mātaraḥ api ca mohitaḥ girijām devīm āhartum girim āyayau atha ananta vapūḥ śrīmān yogī nārāyaṇaḥ amalaḥ kṛtvā atha pārśve bhagavantam īśo yuddhāya viṣṇum gaṇa deva mukhyaiḥ śilāda putreṇa ca mātṛkābhiḥ triśūlam ādāya kṛśānu kalpam rarāja madhye bhagavān surāṇām vivāhanaḥ vārida varṇa varṇaḥ tadā sumeroḥ śikhara adhirūḍha triloka dṛṣṭiḥ bhagavant iva arkaḥ haraḥ sahastra ākṛtiḥ āvirāsīt triśūla pāṇiḥ gagane su ghoṣaḥ papāta deva upari puṣpa vṛṣṭiḥ samāgatam vīkṣya gaṇeśa rājam samāvṛtam deva ripuḥ gaṇeśaiḥ yuyodha śakreṇa sa mātṛkā abhi vijitya sarvān api bāhu vīryāt vimānam āruhya vihīna sattvaḥ dṛṣṭvā andhakam bhagavant garuḍadhvajaḥ tvām ṛte bhagavant śaktaḥ hantā na anyaḥ asya vidyate tvam hartā sarva lokānām kāla ātmā hi aiśvarī tanuḥ jagāma devatā anīkam gaṇānām harṣam uttamam tvam agniḥ sarva bhūtānām antar carasi nityaśas tvam yatrajñaḥ tvam vaṣaṭkāraḥ tvam dhātā hariḥ avyayaḥ tvam brahmā tvam mahādevaḥ tvam dhāma paramam padam oṃkāra mūrtiḥ yoga ātmā trayī netraḥ trilocanaḥ mahā vibhūtiḥ deveśaḥ jaya aśeṣa jagat pate tatas kālāgni rudraḥ asau gṛhītvā andhakam īśvaraḥ triśūla agreṣu vinyasya prananarta satām gatiḥ dṛṣṭvā andhakam deva gaṇāḥ śūla protam pitāmahaḥ antarikṣe apsaraḥ saṅghāḥ nṛtyantisma manoramāḥ saṃsthāpitaḥ atha śūla agre saḥ andhakaḥ dagdha kilbiṣaḥ utpanna akhila vijñānaḥ tuṣṭāva parameśvaram samāhitāḥ yam viduḥ īśa tattvam purātanam puṇyam ananta rūpam daṃṣṭra karālam divi nṛtyamānam hutāśa vaktram jvalana arka rūpam sahastra pāda akṣi śiraḥ bhiyuktam jaya ādideva amara pūjita aṅghre tvām ekam āhuḥ puruṣam purāṇam āditya varṇam tamasaḥ parastāt tvam paśyasi idam paripāsi ajastram tvam antakaḥ yogi gaṇa abhijuṣṭaḥ ekaḥ antarātmā bahudhā niviṣṭaḥ deheṣu deha ādi viśeṣa hīnaḥ tvam ātma śabdam paramātma tattvam mānanda rūpam praṇava abhidhānam svayam prabho aśeṣa viśeṣa hīnaḥ tvam indra rūpaḥ varuṇa agni rūpaḥ haṃsaḥ prāṇaḥ yajñaḥ nīlagrīvaḥ stūyase veda vidbhiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ tvam jagatām atha ādiḥ sadāśivaḥ tvam parameśvaraḥ asi parātmane pañca pada antarāya tri śakti atītāya nirañjanāya namaḥ lalāṭa arpita locanāya namaḥ janānām hṛdi saṃsthitāya phaṇi indra hārāya namaḥ astu te namaḥ ambikāyāḥ pataye mṛḍāya vedānta vijñāna su niścitāya namaḥ maheśāya namaḥ śivāya evam stuvantam bhagavān śūla agrāt avaropya tam tuṣṭaḥ provāca hastābhyām spṛṣṭvā atha parameśvaraḥ saṃprāpya gāṇapatyam me sannidhāne vasa amaraḥ evam vyāhṛta mātre tu devadevena devatāḥ nīlakaṇṭham jaṭā maulim śūla āsakta mahā karam dṛṣṭvā tam tuṣṭuvuḥ daityam āścaryam paramam gatāḥ sthāne tava mahādeva prabhāvaḥ puruṣaḥ mahān na īkṣate ajñāna jān doṣān gṛhṇāti ca guṇān api sa keśavaḥ saha andhakaḥ jagāma śaṃkara antikam nirīkṣya devam āgatam sa śaṅkaraḥ saha andhakam sa mādhavam sa mātṛkam jagāma nirvṛtim haraḥ pragṛhya pāṇinā īśvaraḥ hiraṇya locana ātmajam jagāma yatra śailajā vimānam īśa vallabhā vilokya sā samāgatam bhavam bhava ārti hāriṇam atha andhakaḥ maheśvarīm dadarśa deva pārśva gām papāta daṇḍa vat kṣitau nanāma pāda padmayoḥ yatas pradhāna pūruṣau nihanti yā akhilam jagat vibhāti yā śiva āsane śivena sākam avyayā namāmi yatra tām umām aśeṣa beda varjitām namāmi yā guṇa atigā girīśa putrikām imām kṣamasva devi śailaje kṛtam mayā vimāhataḥ ittham bhagavatī gaurī bhakti namreṇa pārvatī tatas sa mātṛbhiḥ sārdham bhairavaḥ rudra saṃbhavaḥ parameśvaraḥ yatra sā tāmasī viṣṇoḥ mūrtiḥ saṃhāra kārakā samāste hariḥ avyaktaḥ nṛsiṃha ākṛtiḥ īśvaraḥ tatas ananta ākṛtiḥ śaṃbhuḥ śeṣeṇa api su pūjitaḥ kālāgni rudraḥ bhagavant yuyoja ātmānam ātmani bubhukṣitāḥ mahādevam praṇamya āhuḥ triśūliṇam ūcuḥ bubhukṣitāḥ mahādeva anujñā dīyatām tvayā trailokyam bhakṣayiṣyāmaḥ na anyathā tṛptiḥ astinaḥ etāvat uktvā vacanam mātaraḥ viṣṇu saṃbhavāḥ dadhyau nārāyaṇam devam kṣaṇāt prādurabhūt hariḥ vijñāpayāmāsa ca tam bhakṣayanti iha mātaraḥ nivāraya āśu trailokyam tvadīyāḥ bhagavan iti saṃsmṛtāḥ viṣṇunā devyaḥ nṛsiṃha vapuṣā punar upatasthuḥ mahādevam narasiṃha ākṛtim ca tam saṃprāpya sannidhim viṣṇoḥ sarvāḥ saṃhāra kārakāḥ pradaduḥ śaṃbhave śaktim bhairavāya ati tejase apaśyan tāḥ jagat sūtim nṛsiṃham atha bhairavam tvam āpannam śeṣa ahim ca api mātaraḥ vyājahāra hṛṣīkeśaḥ ye bhaktāḥ śūlapāṇinaḥ ye ca mām saṃsmaranti iha pālanīyāḥ prayatnāt mama eva mūrtiḥ atulā sarva saṃhāra kārakā maheśvara aṃśa saṃbhūtā bhukti mukti pradā tu iyam tāmasā rājasā mūrtiḥ devadevaḥ caturmukhaḥ saḥ ayam devaḥ durādharṣaḥ kālaḥ loka prakālanaḥ yā sā vimohikā mūrtiḥ mama nārāyaṇa āhvayā sa hi viṣṇuḥ param brahma paramātmā parā gatiḥ iti evam bodhitāḥ devyaḥ viṣṇunā viśva mātaraḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca devān jitvā bahūn varṣān mahā asuraḥ pālayāmāsa dharmeṇa trailokyam sacarācaram tasya evam vartamānasya kadācid viṣṇu coditaḥ sanatkumāraḥ bhagavān puram prāpa mahā muniḥ dṛṣṭvā sihāsana gataḥ brahma putram mahā asuraḥ nanāma utthāya śirasā prāñjaliḥ vākyam abravīt brūhi me brahmaṇaḥ putra kim kāryam karavāṇi aham draṣṭum abhyāgataḥ aham vai bhavantam bhāgyavān asi su durlabhā nītiḥ eṣā daityānām daitya sattama triloke dhārmikaḥ nūnam tvādṛśaḥ anyaḥ na vidyate dharmāṇām paramam dharmam brūhi me brahma vittama sa labdhvā paramam jñānam dattvā ca guru dakṣiṇām kṛtvā tena mahat yuddham śakraḥ sarva amaraiḥ vṛtaḥ ca gāma nirjitaḥ viṣṇum devam śaraṇam acyutam daitya indrāṇām vadha arthāya putraḥ mama syāt iti svayam prapannā viṣṇum avyaktam śaraṇyam śaraṇam harim kṛtvā hṛd padma kiñjalke niṣkalam paramam padam prasannaḥ bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharaḥ hariḥ dṛṣṭvā samāgatam viṣṇum aditiḥ bhakti saṃyutā mene kṛtārtham ātmānam toṣayāmāsa keśavam jaya aśeṣa duḥkha ogha nāśa eka heto jaya anādi madhya anta vijñāna mūrte jaya aśeṣa kalpa amala ānanda rūpa namaḥ viṣṇave kāla rūpāya te namaḥ nārasiṃhāya śeṣāya tubhyam namaḥ kālarudrāya saṃhāra kartre namaḥ viśva māyā vidhānāya te namaḥ dharma vijñāna niṣṭhāya tubhyam namaḥ śambhave satya niṣṭhāya te namaḥ yogapīṭha antara sthāya te hi śivāya ekarūpāya bhūyas namaḥ te evam sa bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ devamātryā jagat mayaḥ tvām eva putram devānām hitāya varaye varam dadhāra garbham devānām mātā nārāyaṇam svayam samāviṣṭe hṛṣīkeśe devamātuḥ atha udaram prahlādam asuram vṛddham praṇamya āha pitāmaham pitāmaha mahā prājña jāyante asmad pure adhunā bhavet kāryam naḥ kiṃnimittakāḥ niśamya tasya vacanam ciram dhyātvā mahā asuraḥ namaskṛtya hṛṣīkeśam idam vacanam abravīt uvāca dadhāra asura nāśa artham mātā tam tridivaukasām sa vāsudevaḥ devānām mātuḥ deham samāviśat na yasya devāḥ jānanti sva rūpam paramārthāt sa viṣṇuḥ adityāḥ deham sva icchayā adya samāviśat yasmāt bhavanti bhūtāni yatra saṃyānti saṃkṣayam saḥ avatīrṇaḥ mahā yogī purāṇapuruṣaḥ hariḥ sattā mātra ātma rūpaḥ asau viṣṇuḥ aṃśena jāyate yasya sā jagatām mātā śaktiḥ tad dharma dhāriṇī māyā bhagavatī lakṣmī saḥ avatīrṇaḥ janārdanaḥ yasya sā tāmasī mūrtiḥ śaṃkaraḥ rājasī tanuḥ brahmā saṃjāyate viṣṇuḥ aṃśena ekena sattva bhṛt jagāma śaraṇam viśvam pālayāmāsa dharmāt kāle prāpte mahā viṣṇum devānām harṣa vardhanam asūta kaśyapāt ca enam devamātrī aditiḥ svayam catur bhujam viśāla akṣam śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasam nīla megha pratīkāśam bhrājamānam śriyā āvṛtam upatasthuḥ surāḥ sarve siddhāḥ sādhyāḥ ca cāraṇāḥ kṛta upanayanaḥ vedān adhyaiṣṭa bhagavān hariḥ samācāram bharadvājāt trilokāya pradarśayan yajñaiḥ yajñeśvaram viṣṇum arcayāmāsa sarvagam brāhmaṇān pūjayāmāsa dattvā bahutaram dhanam brahmarṣayaḥ samājagmuḥ yajña vāṭam mahātmanaḥ vijñāya viṣṇuḥ bhagavān bharadvāja pracoditaḥ manam rūpam yajña deśam atha agamat kṛṣṇājina upavīta aṅgaḥ āṣāḍhena virājitaḥ brāhmaṇaḥ jaṭilaḥ vedān udgiran bhasma maṇḍitaḥ saṃprāpya asura rājasya samīpam bhikṣukaḥ hariḥ sva pādaiḥ vimitam deśam ayācata balim tribhiḥ prakṣālya caraṇau viṣṇoḥ baliḥ bhā samanvitaḥ bhṛṅgāram ādāya svarṇa nirmitam prīṇātu devaḥ hariḥ avyaya ākṛtiḥ nipātayāmāsa jalam suśītalam vicakrame pṛthivīm eṣaḥ etā tathā antarikṣam divam ādidevaḥ vyapeta rāgam ditija īśvaram tam prakartu kāmaḥ śaraṇam prapannam ākramya lokatrayam īśa pādaḥ prājāpatyāt brahma lokam jagāma pitāmahāḥ toṣayāmāsa viṣṇum bhittvā tad aṇḍasya kapālam ūrdhvam jagāma divya āvaraṇāni bhūyas atha aṇḍa bhedāt nipapāta śītalam mahā jalam tat puṇya kṛdbhiḥ ca juṣṭam gaṅgā iti uktā brahmaṇā vyoma saṃsthā gatvā mahāntam prakṛtim pradhānam brahmāṇam ekam puruṣam sva bījam atiṣṭhat īśasya padam tat avyayam dṛṣṭvā devāḥ tatra tatra stuvanti ālokya tam puruṣam viśva kāyam nanāma nārāyaṇam ekam avyayam sva cetasā yam praṇamanti devāḥ tam abravīt bhagavant ādikartā bhūtvā punar vāmanaḥ vāsudevaḥ nipātayāmāsa jalam kara agre prahlāda sūnoḥ atha śaṅkhapāṇiḥ pātāla mūlam praviśa iti bhūyas samāsyatām bhavatā tatra nityam bhuktvā bhogān devatānām alabhyān dhyāyasva mām satatam bhakti yogāt uktvā evam daitya siṃham tam viṣṇuḥ satya parākramaḥ saṃstuvanti mahā yogam siddhāḥ devarṣi kinnarāḥ brahmā śakraḥ atha bhagavān rudra āditya marut gaṇāḥ kṛtvā etat adbhutam karma viṣṇuḥ vāmana rūpadhṛk paśyatām eva sarveṣām tatra eva antaradhīyata saḥ api daitya varaḥ śrīmān pātālam prāpa coditaḥ prahlādena asura varaiḥ viṣṇunā viṣṇu tatparaḥ pūjā vidhānam prahlādam tat āha asau cakāra saḥ atha ratha caraṇa asi śaṅkha pāṇim eṣa vaḥ kathitaḥ viprāḥ vāmanasya parākramaḥ sa deva kāryāṇi sadā karoti puruṣottamaḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāya baleḥ putra śatam tu āsīt mahā bala parākramam teṣām pradhānaḥ dyutimān bāṇaḥ nāma mahā balaḥ saḥ atīva śaṃkare bhaktaḥ rājā rājyam apālayat trailokyam vaśam ānīya bādhayāmāsa vāsavam tatas śakra ādayaḥ devāḥ gatvā ūcuḥ kṛttivāsasam tvadīyaḥ bādhate hi asmān bāṇaḥ nāma mahā asuraḥ dadāha bāṇasya puram śareṇa ekena līlayā dahyamāne pure tasmin bāṇaḥ rudram triśūliṇam yayau śaraṇam īśānam gopatim nīlalohitam mūrdhani ādhāya tat liṅgam śāṃbhavam bhīta varjitaḥ nirgatya tu purāt tasmāt tuṣṭāva parameśvaram saṃstutaḥ bhagavant īśaḥ śaṅkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ gāṇapatyena bāṇam tam yojayāmāsa bhāvāt atha abhavan danvaḥ putrāḥ tāra ādyāḥ hi ati bhīṣaṇāḥ tāraḥ tathā śambaraḥ ca kapilaḥ śaṅkaraḥ tathā svarbhānuḥ vṛṣaparvā ca prādhānyena prakīrtitāḥ surasāyāḥ sahastram tu sarpāṇām abhavat dvijāḥ aneka śirasām tadvat khecarāṇām mahātmanām ariṣṭā janayāmāsa gandharvāṇām sahastrakam ananta ādyāḥ mahā nāgāḥ kādraveyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ tāmrā ca janayāmāsa ṣaḍ kanyāḥ dvija puṃgavāḥ śukīm śyenīm ca bhāsīm ca sugrīva aṅgṛdhrikām śucim mahiṣīḥ tathā janayāmāsa surabhiḥ mahiṣīḥ tathā irāḥ vṛkṣa latā vallīḥ tṛṇa jātīḥ ca sarvaśas vai yakṣa rakṣāṃsi muniḥ apsarasaḥ tathā rakṣaḥ gaṇam krodhavaśā janayāmāsa sattamāḥ vinatāyāḥ ca putrau dvau prakhyātau garuḍa aruṇau tayoḥ ca garuḍaḥ dhīmān tapaḥ taptvā su duścaram prasādāt śūnilaḥ prāptaḥ vāhana tvam hareḥ svayam bhagavant tapasā rudram mahdevam tathā aruṇaḥ sārathye kalpitaḥ pūrvam prītena arkasya śaṃbhunā ete kaśyapa dāyādāḥ kīrtitāḥ sthāṇu jaṅgamāḥ mad as pāpa nāśanāḥ saptaviṃśatī sutāḥ proktāḥ soma patnyaḥ ca suvratāḥ ariṣṭanemi patnīnām apatyāni iha ṣoḍaśa tadvat aṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ ṛṣayaḥ brahma satkṛtāḥ kuśāśvasya tu devarṣeḥ deva praharaṇāḥ sutāḥ manvantareṣu niyatam tulyaiḥ kāryaiḥ sva nāmabhiḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca etān utpādya putrān tu prajā saṃtāna kāraṇāt vatsarāt naidhruvaḥ jajñe raibhyaḥ ca su mahā yaśāḥ raibhyasya jajñire raibhyāḥ putrāḥ dyutimatām varāḥ sumedhā janayāmāsa putrān vai kuṇḍapāyinaḥ asitasya ekaparṇāyām brahmiṣṭhaḥ samapadyata nāmnā vai devalaḥ putraḥ yoga ācāryaḥ mahā tapāḥ śāṇḍilyānām paraḥ śrīmān sarva tattva artha vid sudhīḥ prasādāt pārvatīśasya yogam uttamam āptavan śāṇḍilyāḥ vāraibhyāḥ trayaḥ pakṣāḥ tu kāśyapāḥ tṛṇabindoḥ sutā viprāḥ nāmnā tu ilavilā smṛtā pulastyāya sa rājarṣiḥ tām kanyām pratyapādayat ṛṣiḥ tu ailavilaḥ tasyām viśravāḥ samapadyata puṣpotkaṭā ca rākā ca kaikasī devavarṇinī rūpa lāvaṇya saṃpannāḥ tāsām vai śṛṇuta prajāḥ jyeṣṭham vaiśravaṇam tasya suṣuve deva rūpiṇī kaikasī janayat putram rāvaṇam rākṣasa adhipam kumbhakarṇam śūrpaṇakhām tathā eva ca vibhīṣaṇam puṣpotkaṭā vyajanayat putrān viśravasaḥ śubhān mahodaram prahastam ca mahāpārśvam kharam tathā tathā kanyām rākāyām śṛṇuta prajāḥ triśirāḥ dūṣaṇaḥ ca eva vidyujjihvaḥ mahā balaḥ iti ete krūra karmāṇaḥ paulastyāḥ rākṣasāḥ daśa sarve tapas bala utkṛṣṭāḥ rudra bhaktāḥ su bhīṣaṇāḥ pulahasya mṛgāḥ putrāḥ sarve vyālāḥ ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ bhūtāḥ piśācāḥ sarpāḥ ca śūkarāḥ hastinaḥ tathā marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ putraḥ svayam eva prajāpatiḥ atreḥ patnyaḥ abhavan bahvyaḥ sodaryāḥ tāḥ pativratāḥ kṛśāśvasya tu vipra indrāḥ ghṛtācyām iti mama śrutam sa tāsu janayāmāsa svastyātreyān mahā ojasaḥ veda vedāṅga niratān tapasā hata kilbiṣān nāradaḥ tu vasiṣṭhāya dadau devīm arundhatīm ūrdhvaretāḥ tatra muniḥ śāpāt dakṣasya nāradaḥ haryaśveṣu tu naṣṭeṣu māyayā nāradasya tu śaśāpa nāradam dakṣaḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ kṣayam nītāḥ tu aśeṣeṇa nirapatyaḥ bhaviṣyati śakteḥ parāśaraḥ śrīmān sarva jñaḥ tapatām varaḥ mārādhya devadeveśam īśānam tripurāntakam lebhe tu apratimam putram kṛṣṇādvaipāyanam prabhum dvaipāyanāt śrakaḥ jajñe bhagavān eva śaṅkaraḥ aṃśāṃśena avatīrya urvyām svam prāpa paramam padam śukasya api abhavan putrāḥ pañca atyanta tapasvinaḥ bhūriśravāḥ prabhuḥ śaṃbhuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ gauraḥ ca pañcamaḥ yogamātrī ca eva yogamātrī dhṛta vratā ete atra vaṃśyāḥ kathitāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ brahma vādinām atas ūrdhvam nibodhadhvam kaśyapāt rāja saṃtatim iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca aditiḥ suṣuve putram ādityam kaśyapāt prabhum tasya ādityasya bhāryāṇām tu catuṣṭayam saṃjñā rājñī prabhā chāyā putrān tāsām nibodhata saṃjñā tvāṣṭrī ca suṣuve sūryāt manum anuttamam yamam ca yamunām ca eva rājñī raivatam eva ca prabhā prabhātam ādityāt chāyā sāvarṇam ātmajam śanim ca tapatīm ca eva viṣṭim ca eva yathākramam ikṣvākuḥ nabhagaḥ ca eva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātiḥ eva ca nariṣyantaḥ ca nābhāgaḥ hi ariṣṭaḥ kāruṣakaḥ tathā pṛṣadhraḥ ca mahā tejāḥ navā ete śakra sannibhāḥ yadā ilā jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca soma vaṃśa vivṛddhaye pitṝṇām tṛpti kartāram budhāt iti hi naḥ śrutam yad abhavat vīraḥ vikukṣiḥ nāma pārthivaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ putra śatasya api daśa pañca ca tad sutāḥ teṣām jyeṣṭhaḥ kakutsthaḥ abhūt kākutsthaḥ hi suyodhanaḥ suyodhanāt pṛthuḥ śrīmān viśvakaḥ ca pṛthoḥ sutaḥ viśvakāt ārdrakaḥ dhīmān yuvanāśvaḥ tu tad sutaḥ sa gokarṇam anuprāpya yuvanāśvaḥ pratāpavān praṇamya daṇḍa vat bhūmau putra kāmaḥ mahīpatiḥ apṛcchat karmaṇā kena dhārmikam prāpnuyāt sutam ārādhya pūrvapuruṣam nārāyaṇam anāmayam anādinidhanam devam dhārmikam prāpnuyāt sutam yasya putraḥ svayam brahmā pautraḥ syāt nīlalohitaḥ tam ādikṛṣṇam īśānam ārādhya āpnoti sat sutam tam ārādhya hṛṣīkeśam prāpnuyāt dhārmikam sutam sa gautama vacaḥ śrutvā yuvanāśvaḥ mahīpatiḥ mahā yogam vāsudevam sanātanam nirmitā yena śrāvastī gauḍa deśe mahā purī tasmāt ca bṛhadaśvaḥ abhūt tasmāt kuvalayāśvakaḥ dṛḍhāśvaḥ ca eva daṇḍāśvaḥ kapilāśvaḥ tathā eva ca dṛḍhāśvasya pramodaḥ tu haryaśvaḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ kṛśāśvaḥ ca raṇāśvaḥ ca saṃhatāśvasya vai sutau yuvanāśvaḥ raṇāśvasya śakra tulya balaḥ yudhi kṛtvā tu vāruṇīm iṣṭim ṛṣīṇām vai prasādataḥ māndhātāram mahā prājñam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam māndhātuḥ purukutsaḥ abhūt ambarīṣaḥ ca vīryavān mucukundaḥ ca puṇya ātmā sarve śakra samāḥ yudhi ambarīṣasya dāyādaḥ yuvanāśvaḥ aparaḥ smṛtaḥ purukutsasya dāyādaḥ trasadasyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ saḥ atīva dhārmikaḥ rājā kardamasya prajāpateḥ prasādāt dhārmikam putram lebhe sūrya parāyaṇam sa tu sūryam samabhyarcya rājā vasumanāḥ śubham ayajat ca aśvamedhena śatrūn jitvā dvijottamāḥ svādhyāyavān dāna śīlaḥ titikṣuḥ dharma tatparaḥ ṛṣayaḥ tu samājagmuḥ yajña vāṭam mahātmanaḥ vasiṣṭha kaśyapa mukhāḥ devāḥ ca indra purogamāḥ tān praṇamya mahā rājaḥ papraccha vinaya anvitaḥ samāpya vidhivat yajñam vasiṣṭha ādīn dvijottamān uvāca kim svid śeyaskarataram loke asmin brāhmaṇa ṛṣabhāḥ yajñaḥ tapaḥ vā saṃnyāsaḥ brūta me sarva vedinaḥ uvāca iṣṭvā yajñeśvaram yajñaiḥ gaccheda vanam atha ātmavān ārādhya tapasā devam yoginam parameṣṭhinam pravrajet vidhivat yajñaiḥ iṣṭvā pūrvam sura uttamān yam āhuḥ ekam puruṣam purāṇam parameśvaram tam ārādhya sahastrāṃśum tapasā mokṣam āpnuyāt uvāca yaḥ agniḥ sarva ātmakaḥ anantaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ viśvatomukhaḥ yaḥ yajñaiḥ ijyate devaḥ jātavedāḥ sanātanaḥ yatas sarvam idam jātam yasya apatyam prajāpatiḥ tapaḥ su mahat āsthāya pūjyate saḥ maheśvaraḥ sa devadevaḥ tapasā pūjanīyaḥ sanātanaḥ uvāca sahastranayanaḥ devaḥ sākṣī sa tu prajāpatiḥ prasīdati mahā yogī pūjitaḥ tapasā paraḥ na antareṇa tapaḥ kaścid dharmaḥ śāstreṣu dṛśyate iti ākarṇya sa rājarṣiḥ tān praṇamya ati hṛṣṭa dhīḥ ārādhayiṣye tapasā devam ekākṣara āhvayam prāṇam bṛhantam puruṣam āditya antara saṃsthitam cāturvarṇya samāyuktam aśeṣam kṣiti maṇḍalam evam uktvā sa tat rājyam nidhāya ātmabhave nṛpaḥ saṃvatsara śatam sāgram tapaḥ nirdhūta kalmaṣaḥ ha jajāpa manasā devīm sāvitrarim vedamātaram tasya evam japataḥ devaḥ svayaṃbhūḥ parameśvaraḥ dṛṣṭvā devam samāyāntam brahmāṇam viśvatomukham manāma śirasā tasya pādayoḥ nām kīrtayan hirṇya mūrtaye tubhyam sahastrākṣāya vedhase sāṃkhya yoga adhigamyāya namaḥ te jñāna mūrtaye puruṣāya purāṇāya yoginām gurave namaḥ uvāca japeyam devadeveśa gāyatrīm vedamātaram bhūyas varṣa śatam sāgram tāvat āyuḥ bhavet mama bāḍham iti āha viśvātmā samālokya narādhipam spṛṣṭvā karābhyām su prītaḥ tatra eva antaradhīyata saḥ api labdha varaḥ śrīmān jajāpa atiprasanna dhīḥ śāntaḥ triṣavaṇa snāyī kanda mūla phala aśanaḥ tasya pūrṇe varṣa śate bhagavān ugra dīdhitiḥ prādurāsīt mahā yogī bhānoḥ maṇḍala madhyatas tam dṛṣṭvā maṇḍala stham sanātanam svayambhuvam anādyantam brahmānam vismayam gataḥ tuṣṭāva vaidikaiḥ mantraiḥ sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ tasmāt apaśyat puruṣam tam eva parameśvaram candra avayava lakṣamāṇam nara nārī tanum haram bhāsayantam jagat kṛtsnam nīlakaṇṭham sva raśmibhiḥ tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ dṛṣṭvā sadbhāvena pareṇa hi nanāma śirasā rudram sāvitryā anena ca eva hi namaḥ te nīlakaṇṭhāya bhāsvate parameṣṭhine trayī mayāya rudrāya kāla rūpāya hetave tadā prāha mahādevaḥ rājānam prīta mānasaḥ imā mama rahasyāni nāmāni śṛṇu ca anagha sarva vedeṣu gītāni saṃsāra śamanāni tu namaskuruṣva nṛpate ebhiḥ mām satatam śuciḥ adhyāyam śatarudrīyam yajuṣām sāram uddhṛtam brahmacārī mita āhāraḥ bhasma niṣṭhaḥ samāhitaḥ japet āmaraṇāt rudram saḥ yāti paramam padam punar saṃvatsara śatam rājñe hi āyuḥ akalpayat dattvā asmai tat param jñānam vairāgyam parameśvaraḥ rājā api tapasā rudram jajāpa ananya mānasaḥ bhasma channaḥ triṣavaṇam snātvā śāntaḥ samāhitaḥ japataḥ tasya nṛpateḥ pūrṇe varṣa śate punar yoga pravṛttiḥ abhavat kālāt kāla ātmakam param viveśa tat veda sāram sthānam vai parameṣṭhinaḥ bhānoḥ sa maṇḍalam śubhram tatas yātaḥ maheśvaram yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api rājñaḥ caritam uttamam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekonaviśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca bhāryā satyadhanā nāma hariścandram ajījanat vijayasya abhavat putraḥ kārukaḥ nāma vīryavān kārukasya vṛkaḥ putraḥ tasmāt bāhuḥ ajāyata dve bhārye sagarasya api prabhā bhānumatī tathā tābhyām ārādhitaḥ prādāt aurvāgniḥ varam uttamam ekam bhānumatī putram agṛhṇāt asamañjasam prabhā ṣaṣṭi sahastram tu putrāṇām jagṛhe śubhā asamañsasya tanayaḥ hi aṃśumant nāma pārthivaḥ yena bhāgīrathī gaṅgā tapaḥ kṛtvā avatāritā bhagīrathasya tapasā devaḥ prīta manāḥ haraḥ babhāra śirasā gaṅgām soma ante soma bhūṣaṇaḥ bhagīratha sutaḥ ca api śrutaḥ nāma babhūva ha ṛtuparṇasya putraḥ abhūt sudāsaḥ nāma dhārmikāḥ saudāsaḥ tasya tanayaḥ khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādakaḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ tu mahā tejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake aśmakam janayāmasā tam ikṣvāku kula dhvajam aśmakasya utkalāyām tu nakulaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ sa hi rāma bhayāt rājā vanam prāpa su duḥkhitaḥ tasmāt bilibiliḥ śrīmān vṛddhaśarmā acata sutaḥ tasmāt viśvasahaḥ tasmāt khaṭvāṅgaḥ iti viśrutaḥ rāmaḥ dāśarathiḥ voraḥ dharma jñaḥ loka viśrutaḥ bharataḥ lakṣmaṇaḥ ca eva śatrughnaḥ ca mahā balaḥ sarve śakra samāḥ yuddhe viṣṇu śakti samanvitāḥ jajñe rāvaṇa nāśa artham viṣṇuḥ aṃśena viśvakṛt rāmasya subhagā bhāryā janakasya ātmajā śubhā sītā triloka vikhyātā śīla audārya guṇa anvitā tapasā toṣitā devī janakena girīndrajā prāyacchat jānakīm sītām rāmam eva āśritā patim prītaḥ ca bhagavān īśaḥ triśūlī nīlalohitaḥ pradadau śatru nāśa artham janakāya adbhutam dhanuḥ sa rājā janakaḥ vidvān dātu kāmaḥ sutām imām idam dhanuḥ samādātum yaḥ śaknoti jagattraye devaḥ vā dānavaḥ vā api sa sītām labdhum arhati vijñāya rāmaḥ balavān janakasya gṛham prabhuḥ bhañjayāmāsa ca ādāya gatvā asau līlayā eva hi udvavāha ca tām kanyām pārvatīm iva śaṅkaraḥ rāmaḥ parama dharma ātmā senām iva ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ rāmam jyeṣṭham sutam vīram rājānam kartum ārabhat tasya atha patnī subhagā kaikeyī cāru bhāṣiṇī nivārayāmāsa patim prāha saṃbhrānta mānasā mad sutam bharatam vīram rājānam kartum arhasi sa tasyāḥ vacanam śrutvā rājā duḥ khita mānasaḥ bāḍham iti abravīt vākyam tathā rāmaḥ api dharma vid praṇamya atha pituḥ pādau lakṣmaṇena saha acyutaḥ yayau vanam sa patnīkaḥ kṛtvā samayam ātmavān saṃvatsarāṇām catvāri daśa ca eva mahā balaḥ kadācid vasataḥ araṇye rāvaṇaḥ nāma rākṣasaḥ parivrājaka veṣeṇa sītām hṛtvā yayau purīm a dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇaḥ rāmaḥ sītām ākulita indriyau tatas kadācid kapinā sugrīveṇa dvijottamāḥ vānarāṇām abhūt sakhyam rāmasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ sugrīvasya anugaḥ vīraḥ hanumān nma vānaraḥ mahā tejāḥ rāmasya āsīt priyaḥ sadā sa kṛtvā paramam dhairyam rāmāya kṛta niścayaḥ mānayiṣyāmi tām sītām iti uktvā vicacāra ha mahīm sāgara paryantām sītā darśana tatparaḥ gama tatra atha nirjane deśe vṛkṣa mūle śuci smitām apaśyat amalām sītām rākṣasībhiḥ samāvṛtām aśru pūrṇa īkṣaṇām hṛdyām saṃsmarantīm aninditām rāmam indīvara śyāmam lakṣmaṇam ca ātma saṃsthitam nivedayitvā ca ātmānam sītāyai rahasi svayam asaṃśayāya pradadau asyai rāma aṅgulīyakam dṛṣṭvā aṅgulīyakam sītā patyuḥ parama śobhanam mene samāgatam rāmam prīti visphārita īkṣaṇā samāśvāsya tadā sītām dṛṣṭvā rāmasya ca antikam nayiṣye tvām mahā bāhuḥ uktvā rāmam yayau punar nivedayitvā rāmāya sītā darśanam ātmavān tasthau rāmeṇa puratas lakṣmaṇena ca pūjitaḥ tatas sa rāmaḥ balavān sārdham hanumantā svayam kṛtvā atha vānara śataiḥ laṅkā mārgam mahodadheḥ setum parama dharma ātmā rāvaṇam hatavan prabhuḥ sa patnīkam ca sa sutam sa bhrātṛkam aridamaḥ ha ānayāmāsa tām sītām vāyuputra sahāyavān setu madhye mahādevam īśānam kṛttivāsasam sthāpayāmāsa liṅga stham pūjayāmāsa rāghavaḥ tasya devaḥ mahādevaḥ pārvatyā saha śaṅkaraḥ yat tvayā sthāpitam liṅgam drakṣyanti iha dvijātayaḥ mahāpātaka saṃyuktāḥ teṣām pāpam vinaśyatu darśanāt eva liṅgasalya nāśam yānti na saṃśayaḥ yāvat sthāsyanti girayaḥ yāvat eṣā ca medinī snānam dānam japaḥ śrāddham bhaviṣyati akṣyam kṛtam smaraṇāt eva liṅgasya dina pāpam praṇaśyati iti uktvā bhagavant śaṃbhuḥ pariṣvajya tu rāghavam rāmaḥ api pālayāmāsa rājyam dharma parāyaṇaḥ brāhmaṇān sarvān pūjayāmasaca īśvaram yajñena yajñahantāram aśvamedhena śaṃkaram lavaḥ ca su mahābhāgaḥ sarva tattva artha vid sudhīḥ nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīka ākhyaḥ kṣemadhanvā ca tad sutaḥ tasya putraḥ abhavat vīraḥ devānīkaḥ pratāpavān tasmāt candrāvalokaḥ tu tārāpīḍaḥ tu tad sutaḥ śrutāyuḥ abhavat tasmāt ete ikṣvāku vaṃśa jāḥ sarve prādhānyataḥ proktāḥ samāsena dvijottamāḥ yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt nityam ikṣvākoḥ vaṃśam uttamam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge viśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ailaḥ purūravāḥ ca atha rājā rājyam apālayat āyuḥ māyuḥ amāvāyuḥ viśvāyuḥ ca eva vīryavān śatāyuḥ ca śrutāyuḥ ca divyāḥ ca eva urvaśī sutāḥ āyuṣaḥ tanayāḥ vīrāḥ pañca eva āsan mahā ojasaḥ svarbhānu tanayāyām vai prabhāyām iti naḥ śrutam nahuṣaḥ prathamaḥ teṣām dharma jñaḥ loka viśrutaḥ nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaṭ indra upama tejasaḥ utpannāḥ pitṛ kanyāyām virajāyām mahā balāḥ saṃyātiḥ āyātiḥ pañcakaḥ aśvakaḥ teṣām yayātiḥ pañcānām mahā bala parākramaḥ devayānī mukhanasaḥ sutām bhāryām avāpa saḥ śarmiṣṭhām āsurīm ca eva tanayām vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ druhyum ca anum ca pūrum ca śarmiṣṭhā ca api ajījanat diśi turvasum putram ādiśat dakṣiṇā parayoḥ rājā yadum jyeṣṭham nyayojayat pratīcyām uttārāyām ca druhyum ca anum akalpayat taiḥ iyam pṛthivī sarvā dharmataḥ paripālitā rājā api dāra sahitaḥ navam prāpa mahā yaśāḥ sahastrajit tathā ajyeṣṭhaḥ kroṣaṭuḥ nālaḥ ajita uraghuḥ sutāḥ śatajitaḥ api āsan trayaḥ parama dhārmikāḥ haihayaḥ ca hayaḥ ca eva rājā veṇuhayaḥ paraḥ mahiṣmān saṃjitasya abhūt bhadraśreṇyaḥ tad anvayaḥ bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādaḥ durdamaḥ nāma pārthivaḥ dhanakasya tu dāyādāḥ catvāraḥ loka sammatāḥ kṛtavīryaḥ kṛtāgniḥ ca kṛtavarmā tathā eva ca tasya putra śatāni āsan pañca tatra mahā rathāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ balinaḥ śūrāḥ dharma ātmānaḥ namasvinaḥ śūraḥ ca śūrasenaḥ ca dhṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ tathā eva ca jayadhvajaḥ ca balavān nārāyaṇa paraḥ nṛpaḥ śūrasena ādayaḥ sarve catvāraḥ prathita ojasaḥ rudra bhaktāḥ mahātmānaḥ pūjayanti sma śaṃkaram jayadhvajaḥ tu matimān devam nārāyaṇam harim jagāma śaraṇam viṣṇum daivatam dharma tatparaḥ īśvara ārādhana rataḥ pitā naḥ abhūt iti tān abravīt mahā tejāḥ eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ mama viṣṇoḥ aṃśena saṃbhūtāḥ rājānaḥ yat mahī tale rājyam pālayata avaśyam bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ pūjanīyaḥ yatas viṣṇuḥ pālakaḥ jagantaḥ hariḥ sāttvikā rājasā ca eva tāmasā ca svayaṃbhuvaḥ tistraḥ tu mūrtayaḥ proktāḥ sṛṣṭi sthiti anta hetavaḥ sattva ātmā bhagavān viṣṇuḥ saṃsthāpayati sarvadā sṛjet brahmā rajomūrtiḥ saṃharet tāmasaḥ haraḥ tasmāt mahīpatīnām tu rājyam pālayatām ayam mad ārādhyaḥ bhagavant viṣṇuḥ keśavaḥ keśi mardanaḥ procuḥ saṃhāra kṛt rudraḥ pūjanīyaḥ mumukṣubhiḥ ayam hi bhagavān rudraḥ sarvam jagat idam śivaḥ tamaḥ guṇam samāśritya kalpa ante saṃharet prabhuḥ yā sā ghoratarā mūrtiḥ asya tejā mayī parā saṃharet vidyayā sarvam saṃsāram śūlabhṛt tayā tathā ca vaiṣṇavī śaktiḥ nṛpāṇām devatā sadā tam abravīt rāja putraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ matimatām varaḥ evam vivāde vitate śūrasenaḥ abravīt vacaḥ tatas te rāja śārdūlāḥ papracchuḥ brahma vādinaḥ gatvā sarve su saṃrabdhāḥ saptarṣīṇām tadā āśramam tān abruvan te munayaḥ vasiṣṭha ādyāḥ yathārthāt yā yasya abhimatā puṃsaḥ sā hi tasya eva devatā kintu kārya viśeṣeṇa pūjitāḥ ca iṣṭa dāḥ nṛṇām sarvadā na ayam niyamaḥ hi anyathā nṛpāḥ nṛpāṇām daivatam viṣṇuḥ tathā eva ca purandaraḥ viprāṇām agniḥ ādityaḥ brahmā ca eva pinākadhṛk devānām daivatam viṣṇuḥ dānavānām triśūlabhṛt gandharvāṇām tathā somaḥ yakṣāṇām api kathyate vidyādharāṇām vāgdevī sādhyānām bhagavān raviḥ rakṣasām śaṃkaraḥ rudraḥ kiṃnarāṇām ca pārvatī ṛṣīṇām daivatam brahmā mahādevaḥ ca śūlabhṛt manūnām syāt umā devī tathā viṣṇuḥ sa bhāskaraḥ gṛhasthānām ca sarve syuḥ brahmā vai brahmacāriṇām vaikhānasānām arkaḥ syāt yatīnām ca maheśvaraḥ bhūtānām bhagavān rudraḥ kūṣmāṇḍānām vināyakaḥ sarveṣām bhagavān brahmā devadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ tasmāt jayadhvajaḥ nūnam viṣṇu ārādhanam arhati tān praṇamya atha te jagmuḥ purīm parama śobhanām pālayāñcakrire pṛthvīm jitvā sarva ripūn raṇe tatas kadācid vipra indrāḥ videhaḥ nāma dānavaḥ bhīṣaṇaḥ sarva sattvānām purīm teṣām samāyayau daṃṣṭra karālaḥ dīpta ātmā yugānta dahana upamaḥ śūlam ādāya sūrya ābham nādayan vai diśaḥ daśa tatas sarve su saṃyattāḥ kārtavīrya ātmajāḥ tadā yuyudhuḥ dānavam śakti giri kūṭa asi mudgaraiḥ tān sarvān dānavaḥ viprāḥ śūlena prahasan iva māsa ghora ātmā kalpa ante bhairavaḥ yathā śūrasena ādayaḥ pañca rājānaḥ tu mahā balāḥ śūraḥ astram prāhiṇot raudram śūrasenaḥ tu vāruṇam prājāpatyam tathā kṛṣṇaḥ vāyavyam dhṛṣṇaḥ eva ca bhañjayāmāsa śūlena tāni astrāṇi sa dānavaḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ mahā vīryaḥ gadām ādāya bhīṣaṇām spṛṣṭvā mantreṇa tarasā cikṣepa na nanāda ca saṃprāpya sā gādā asya uraḥ videhasya śilā upamam na dānavam cālayitum śaśāka antaka saṃnibham dudruvuḥ te bhaya grastāḥ dṛṣṭvā tasya atipauruṣam viṣṇum grasiṣṇum loka ādim aprameyam anāmayam trātāram puruṣam pūrvam śrīpatim pītavāsasam bhakta anugraha kāraṇāt jagrāha jagatām yonim smṛtvā nārāyaṇam nṛpaḥ prāhiṇot vai videhāya dānavebhyaḥ yathā hariḥ pṛthivyām pātayāmāsa śiraḥ adri śikhara ākṛti tasmin hate deva ripau śīra ādyāḥ bhrātaraḥ nṛpāḥ samāyayuḥ purīm ramyām bhrātaram ca api apūjayan kārtavīrya sutam draṣṭum viśvāmitraḥ mahā muniḥ tam āgatam atho dṛṣṭvā rājā saṃbhrānta mānasaḥ samāveśya āsane ramye pūjayāmāsa bhāvāt uvāca bhagavān ghoraḥ prasādāt bhavataḥ asuraḥ nipātitaḥ mayā saṃkhye videhaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ tvad vākyāt chinna saṃdehaḥ viṣṇum satya parākramam prapannaḥ śaraṇam tena prasādaḥ mama kṛtaḥ śubhaḥ yakṣyāmi parameśānam viṣṇum padma dala īkṣaṇam katham kena vidhānena saṃpūjyaḥ hariḥ īśvaraḥ kaḥ ayam nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ kiṃprabhāvaḥ ca suvrata uvāca yatas pravṛttiḥ bhūtānām yasmin sarvam idam jagat sa viṣṇuḥ sarva bhūta ātmā tam āśritya vimucyate sva varṇa āśrama dharmeṇa pūjyaḥ ayam puruṣottamaḥ a kāma hata bhāvena samārādhyaḥ na ca anyathā etāvat uktvā viśvāmitraḥ mahā muniḥ śūra ādyaiḥ pūjitaḥ viprāḥ jagāma atha svam ālayam yajñena yajña gamyam tam niṣkāmāḥ rudram avyayam tān vasiṣṭhaḥ tu bhagavān yājayāmāsa sarva vid yājayāmāsa bhūtādim ādidevam janārdanam tasya yajñe mahā yogī sākṣāt devaḥ svayam hariḥ yaḥ imam śṛṇuyāt nityam jayadhvaja parākramam sarva pāpa vimukta ātmā viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekaviśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śata putrāḥ tu tasya āsan tālajaṅghāḥ prakīrtitāḥ teṣām jyeṣṭhaḥ mahā vīryaḥ vītihotraḥ abhavat nṛpaḥ vṛṣa prabhṛtayaḥ ca anye yādavāḥ puṇya karmiṇaḥ vṛṣaḥ vaṃśa karaḥ teṣām tasya putraḥ abhavat madhuḥ madhoḥ putra śatam tu āsīt vṛṣaṇaḥ tasya vaṃśa bhāj tasya bhāryā rūpavatī guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ alaṅkṛtā sa kadācid mahābhāgaḥ kālindī tīra saṃsthitām paśyat urvaśīm devīm gāyatīm madhura svanām provāca suciram kālam devi rantum mayā ar'hasi sā devī nṛpatim dṛṣṭvā rūpa lāvaṇya saṃyutam kālāt prabuddhaḥ rājā tām urvaśīm prāha śobhanām gamiṣyāmi purīm ramyām hasatī sā bravīt vacaḥ prītiḥ saṃjāyate mahyam sthātavyam vatsaram punar tām abravīt sa matimān gatvā śīghrataram purīm āgamiṣyāmi bhūyas atra tat me anujñātum arhasi tam abravīt sā subhagā tathā kuru viśām pate na anyayā apsarasā tāvat rantavyam bhavat punar om iti uktvā yayau tūrṇam purīm parama śobhanām gatvā pativratām patnīm dṛṣṭvā bītaḥ abhavat nṛpaḥ saṃprekṣya sā guṇavatī bhāryā tasya pativratā bhītam prasannayā prāha vācā pīna payodharā tat brūhi me yathā tattvam na rājñām kīrtaye tu idam sa tasyāḥ vākyam ākarṇya lajjā avanata cetanaḥ na uvāca kiṃcid nṛpatiḥ jñāna dṛṣṭyā viveda sā na bhetavyam tvayā svāmin kāryam pāpa viśodhanam bhīte tvayi mahā rāja rāṣṭram te nāśam eṣyati tadā sa rājā dyutimān nirgatya tu purāt tatas gatvā kaṇva āśramam puṇyam dṛṣṭvā tatra mahā munim niśamya kaṇva vadanāt prāyaścitta vidhim śubham jagāma himavat pṛṣṭham samuddiśya mahā balaḥ bhrājamānam śriyā vyomni bhūṣitam divya mālayā vīkṣya mālām amitra ghnaḥ sasmāra apsarasām varām urvaśīm tām manaḥ cakre tasyāḥ eva iyam arhati saḥ atīva kāmukaḥ rājā gandharveṇa atha tena hi cakāra su mahat yuddham mālām ādātum udyataḥ vijitya samare mālām gṛhītvā durjayaḥ dvijāḥ jagāma tām apsarasam kālindīm draṣṭum ādarāt a dṛṣṭvā apsarasam tatra kāma bāṇa abhipīḍitaḥ babhrāma sakalām pṛthvīm sapta dvīpa samanvitām ākramya himavat pārśvam urvaśī darśana utsukaḥ iti tatra tatra apsaraḥ varyāḥ dṛṣṭvā tam siṃha vikramam kāmam saṃdadhire ghoram bhūṣitam citra mālayā saṃsmaran urvaśī vākyam tasyām saṃsakta mānasaḥ na paśyati smatāḥ sarvāḥ giri śṛṅgāṇi jagmivān tatra api apsarasam divyām a dṛṣṭvā kāma pīḍitaḥ bheje śṛṅgāṇi atikramya sva bāhu bala bhāvitaḥ sa tasya tīre subhagām carantīm ati lālasām dṛṣṭavān anavadya aṅgām tasyai mālām dadau punar sa mālayā tadā devīm bhūṣitām prekṣya mohitaḥ reme kṛtārtham ātmānam jānānaḥ su ciram tayā atha urvaśī rāja varyam rata ante vākyam abravīt kim kṛtam bhavatā pūrvam purīm gatvā vṛthak nṛpa mālā apaharaṇam tathā śrutvā etat vyāhṛtam tena gaccha iti āha hita eṣiṇī śāpam dāsyati te kaṇvaḥ mama api bhavataḥ priyā tayā asakṛt mahā rājaḥ proktaḥ api mada mohitaḥ na tatyaja atha tad pārśvam tatra saṃnyasta mānasaḥ tatas urvaśī kāmarūpā rājñe svam rūpam utkaṭam su romaśam piṅgala akṣam darśayāmāsa sarvadā tasyām virakta cetaskaḥ smṛtvā kaṇva abhibhāṣitam saṃvatsara dvādaśakam kanda mūla phala aśanaḥ bhūyas eva dvādaśakam vāyubhakṣaḥ abhavat nṛpaḥ gatvā kaṇva āśramam bhītyā tasmai sarvam nyavedayat vīkṣya tam rāja śārdūlam prasannaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ gaccha vārāṇasīm divyām īśvara adhyuṣitām purīm snātvā saṃtarpya vidhivat gaṅgāyān devatāḥ pitṝn dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaram liṅgam kilbiṣāt mokṣyase akhilāt praṇamya śirasā kaṇvam anujñāpya ca durjayaḥ mārāṇasyām haram dṛṣṭvā pāpāt muktaḥ abhavat tatas jagāma sva purīm śubhrām pālayāmāsa medinīm yājayāmāsa tam kaṇvaḥ yācitaḥ ghṛṇayā muniḥ babhūva jāta mātram tam rājānam upatasthire urvaśyām ca mahā vīryāḥ sapta deva suta upamāḥ kanyāḥ jagṛhire sarvāḥ jandharva dayitāḥ dvijāḥ vaṃśaḥ pāpa haraḥ nṛṇām kroṣṭoḥ api nibodhata iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge dvāviśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca kroṣṭoḥ ekaḥ abhavat putraḥ vṛjinīvant iti śrutiḥ tasya putraḥ pṛthuyaśāḥ rājā abhūt dharma tatparaḥ pṛthuśravāḥ tasya putraḥ tasya āsīt pṛthusattamaḥ tasya abhūt rukmakavacaḥ parāvṛt tasya sattamāḥ parāvṛtaḥ sutaḥ jajñe jyāmaghaḥ loka viśrutaḥ romapādaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu babhruḥ tasya ātmajaḥ nṛpaḥ tasya putraḥ mahā vīryaḥ prajāvān kauśikaḥ tatas kaiśikasya sutaḥ cediḥ caidyāḥ tasya abhavan sutāḥ teṣām pradhānaḥ jyotiṣmant vapuṣmant tad sutaḥ abhavat krathasya api abhavat kuntī vṛṣṇī tasya abhavat sutaḥ vṛṣṇeḥ nivṛttiḥ utpannaḥ daśārhaḥ tasya tu dvijāḥ jaimūtiḥ abhavat vīraḥ vikṛtiḥ para vīra hā dāna dharma rataḥ nityam samyak śīla parāyaṇaḥ kadācid mṛgayām yātaḥ dṛṣṭvā rākṣasam ūrjitam dudrāva mahā taviṣṭaḥ bhayena muni puṃgavāḥ anvadhāvata saṃkruddhaḥ rākṣasaḥ tam mahā balaḥ duryodhanaḥ agni saṃkāśaḥ śūla āsakta mahā karaḥ rājā navarathaḥ bhītyā na ati dūrāt anuttamam sa tat vegena mahatā saṃprāpya matimān nṛpaḥ vavande śirasā dṛṣṭvā sākṣāt devīm sarasvatīm tuṣṭāva vāgbhiḥ iṣṭābhiḥ baddhāñjaliḥ amitra jit papāta daṇḍa vat bhūmau tvām aham śaraṇam gataḥ namasyāmi mahādevīm sākṣāt devīm sarasvatīm vāgdevatām anādyantām īśvarām brahmacāriṇīm namasye jagatām yonim yoginīm paramām kalām hiraṇyagarbha mahiṣīm tri netrām candra śekharām namasye parama ānandām cit kalām brahma rūpiṇīm pāhi mām parameśāni bhītam śaraṇam āgatam etasmin antare kruddhaḥ rājānam rākṣaseśvaraḥ hantum samāgataḥ sthānam yatra devī sarasvatī samudyamya tadā śūlam praveṣṭum bala darpitaḥ triloka mātuḥ tat sthānam śaśāṅka āditya saṃnibham śūlena urasi nirbhidya pātayāmāsa tam bhuvi gaccha iti āha mahā rāja na sthātavyam tvayā punar idānīm nirbhayaḥ tūrṇam sthāne asmin rākṣasaḥ hataḥ tatas praṇamya hṛṣṭa ātmā rājā navarathaḥ parām purīm jagāma vipra indrāḥ puraṃdara pura upamām sthāpayāmāsa deveśīm tatra bhakti samanvitaḥ tasya ca āsīt daśarathaḥ putraḥ parama dhārmikaḥ devyāḥ bhaktaḥ mahā tejāḥ śakuniḥ tasya ca ātmajaḥ sa ca aśvamedhena devakṣatraḥ ca tad sutaḥ atha aṃśoḥ sattvatas nāma viṣṇu bhaktaḥ pratāpavān mahātmā dāna nirataḥ dhanurveda vidām varaḥ māstram pravartayāmāsa kuṇḍa gola ādibhiḥ śrutam tasya nāmnā tu vikhyātam sāttvatam nāma śobhanam pravartate mahā śāstram kuṇḍa ādīnām hita āvaham sāttvataḥ tasya putraḥ abhūt sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ sāttvataḥ sattva saṃpannaḥ kauśalyām suṣuve sutān andhakam vai mahābhojam vṛṣṇim devāvṛdham nṛpam jyeṣṭham ca bhajamāna ākhyam dhanurveda vidām varam teṣām devāvṛdhaḥ rājā cacāra paramam tapaḥ dhārmikaḥ rūpa saṃpannaḥ tattva jñāna rataḥ sadā bhajamānasya sṛñjayyām bhajamānāḥ vijajñire teṣām pradhānau vikhyātau nimiḥ kṛkaṇaḥ eva ca mahābhoja kule jātāḥ bhojāḥ vaimārtikāḥ tathā vṛṣṇeḥ sumitraḥ balavān anamitraḥ śinaḥ tathā prasenaḥ tu mahābhāgaḥ satrājit nāma ca uttamaḥ anamitrāt śiniḥ jajñe kaniṣṭhāt vṛṣṇi nandanāt mādrayā vṛṣṇeḥ sutaḥ jajñe pṛśniḥ vai yadu nandanaḥ jajñāte tanayau pṛśneḥ śvaphalkaḥ citrakaḥ ca ha śvaphalkaḥ kāśi rājasya sutām bhāryām avindata upamaṅguḥ tathā maṅguḥ anye ca bahavaḥ sutāḥ akrūrasya smṛtaḥ putraḥ devavant iti viśrutaḥ upadevaḥ ca puṇya ātmā tayoḥ viśva pramāthinaḥ aśvagrīvaḥ subāhuḥ ca supārśvaka gaveṣaṇau andhakāt kāśya duhitā lebhe ca caturaḥ sutān kukuram bhajamānam ca śucim kambalabarhiṣam kukurasya sutaḥ vṛṣṇiḥ vṛṣṇeḥ tu tanayaḥ abhavat vaṃśasya ca akṣayām kīrti gāna yogam anuttamam sa labdhvā varam avyagraḥ vareṇyam vṛṣavāhanam pūjayāmāsa gānena sthāṇum tridaśa pūjitam aśikṣayat amitra ghnaḥ priyām tām bhrānta locanām tasyām utpādayāmāsa subhujam nāma śobhanam rūpa lāvaṇya saṃpannām hrīmatīm api kanyakām śikṣayāmāsa vidhivat gāna vidyām ca kanyakām udvavāha ātmajām kanyām gandharvāṇām tu mānasīm tasyām utpādayāmāsa pañca putrān anuttamān vīṇā vādana tattva jñān gāna śāstra viśāradān putraiḥ pautraiḥ sa patnīkaḥ rājā gāna viśāradaḥ pūjayāmāsa gānena devam tripura nāśanam hrīmatī ca api yā kanyā śrīḥ iva āyata locanā subāhuḥ nāma gandharvaḥ tām ādāya yayau purīm suṣeṇa vīra sugrīva subhoja naravāhanāḥ punarvasuḥ ca abhijitaḥ saṃbabhūva āhukaḥ sutaḥ devakasya sutāḥ vīrāḥ jajñire tridaśa upamāḥ teṣām svasāraḥ sapta āsan vasudevāya tāḥ dadau vṛkadevā upadevā ca tathā anyā devarakṣitā māntidevā ca sahadevā sahadevā ca suvratā devakī ca api tāsām tu variṣṭhā abhūt sumadhyamā subhūmiḥ rāṣṭrapālaḥ ca tuṣṭimant śaṅkuḥ eva ca bhajamānāt abūt putraḥ prakhyātaḥ asau vidūrathaḥ svayaṃbhojaḥ tatas tasmāt hṛdikaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ rohiṇī ca mahābhāgā vasudevasya śobhanā patnī saṃkarṣam rāmam jyeṣṭham halāyudham halāyudhaḥ svayam sākṣāt śeṣaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ bhṛgu śāpa chalena eva mānayan mānuṣīm tanum babhūta tasyām devakyām rohiṇyām api mādhavaḥ umā deha samudbhūtā yoga nidrā ca kauśīkī niyogāt vāsudevasya yaśodā tanayā hi abhūt ye ca anye vasudevasya vāsudeva agrajāḥ sutāḥ prāk eva kaṃsaḥ tān sarvān jaghāna muni puṃgavāḥ suṣeṇaḥ ca tathā udāyī bhadrasenaḥ mahā balaḥ api hateṣu eteṣu sarveṣu rohiṇī vasudevataḥ asūta rāmam loka īśam balabhadram halāyudham jāte atha rāme devānām ādim ātmānam acyutam asūta devakī kṛṣṇam śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasam revatī nāma rāmasya bhāryā āsīt su guṇa anvitā ṣoḍaśa strī sahastrāṇi kṛṣṇasya akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ babhūvuḥ ātmajāḥ tāsu śataśas atha sahastraśas cārudeṣṇaḥ sucāruḥ ca cāruveṣaḥ yaśodharaḥ cāruśravāḥ cāruyaśāḥ pradyumnaḥ śaṅkhaḥ eva ca mahā bala parākramāḥ viśiṣṭāḥ sarva putrāṇām saṃbabhūvuḥ im sutāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā tanayān vīrān raukmiṇeyān janārdanam jāmbavatī abravīt kṛṣṇam bhāryā tasya śuci smitā mama tvam puṇḍarīkākṣa viśiṣṭam guṇavattamam sureśa sadṛśam putram dehi dānava sūdanaiḥ jātbavatyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā jagannāthaḥ svayam hariḥ tat śṛṇudhvam muni śreṣṭhāḥ yathā asau devakī sutaḥ dṛṣṭvā lebhe sutam rudram taptvā tīvram mahat tapaḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atha devaḥ hṛṣīkeśaḥ bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ tatāpa ghoram putra artham nidānam tapasaḥ tapaḥ sva icchayā api avatīrṇaḥ asau kṛtakṛtyaḥ api viśvadhṛk jagāma yogibhiḥ juṣṭam nānā pakṣi samākulam muni indrasya mahātmanaḥ tapat tri rājam ārūḍhaḥ suparṇam ati tejasam śaṅkha cakra gadā pāṇiḥ śrīvatsa kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ nānā druma latā ākīrṇam nānā puṣpa upaśobhitam ṛṣīṇām āśramaiḥ juṣṭam veda ghoṣa nināditam siṃha ṛkṣa śarabha ākīrṇam śārdūla gaja saṃyutam ārāmaiḥ vividhaiḥ juṣṭam devatāyatanaiḥ śubhaiḥ mahā muni gaṇaiḥ tathā upetam sarvatas puṇyam jñānibhiḥ tattva darśibhiḥ nadībhiḥ abhitas juṣṭam jāpakaiḥ brahma vādibhiḥ sevitam tāpasaiḥ puṇyaiḥ īśa ārādhana tatparaiḥ bhasma avadāta sarva aṅgaiḥ rudra jāpya parāyaṇaiḥ muṇḍitaiḥ jaṭilaiḥ śuddhaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ ca śikhājaṭaiḥ tatra āśrama vare ramye siddha āśrama vibhūṣite gaṅgā bhagavatī nityam vahati eva agha nāśinī sa tān anviṣya viśvātmā tāpasān vīta kalmaṣān praṇāmena atha vacasā pūjayāmāsa mādhavaḥ te te dṛṣṭvā jagadyonim śaṅkha cakra gadā dharam ayam sa bhagavān ekaḥ sākṣāt nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ agacchati adhunā devaḥ purāṇapuruṣaḥ svayam ayam eva avyayaḥ straṣṭā saṃhartā ca eva rakṣakaḥ amūrtaḥ mūrtimān bhūtvā munīn draṣṭum iha āgataḥ eṣa dhātā vidhātā ca samāgacchati sarva gaḥ anādiḥ akṣayaḥ anantaḥ mahābhūtaḥ maheśvaraḥ śrutvā śrutvā hariḥ teṣām vacāṃsi vacana atigaḥ yayau sa tūrṇam govindaḥ sthānam tasya mahātmanaḥ upaspṛśya atha bhāvena tīrthe tīrthe sa yādavaḥ cakāra devakī sūnuḥ deva ṛṣi pitṛ tarpaṇam nadīnām tīra saṃsthāni sthāpitāni muni īśvaraiḥ liṅgāni pūjayāmāsa śambhoḥ amita tejasaḥ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā samāyāntam yatra yatra janārdanam pūjayāñcakrire puṣpaiḥ akṣataiḥ tatra vāsinaḥ samīkṣya vāsudevam tam śārṅga śaṅkha asi dhāriṇam tasthire niścalāḥ sarve śubha aṅgam tad nivāsinaḥ yāni tatra ārurukṣūṇām mānasāni janārdanam dṛṣṭvā samīhitāni āsan niṣkrāmanti purā ahiram atha avagāhya gaṅgāyām kṛtvā deva ādi tarpaṇam ādāya puṣpa varyāṇi muni indrasya āviśat gṛham dṛṣṭvā tam yoginām śreṣṭham bhasma uddhūlita vigraham jaṭā cīra dharam śāntam nanāma śirasā munim ālokya kṛṣṇam āyāntam pūjayāmāsa tattva vid mahā āsane ca āsayāmāsa yoginām prathama atithim uvāca vacasām yonim jānīmaḥ paramam padam viṣṇum avyakta saṃsthānam śiṣya bhāvena saṃsthitam svāgatam te hṛṣīkeśa sa phalāni tapāṃsi naḥ yat sākṣāt eva viśvātmā mad geham viṣṇuḥ āgataḥ tādṛśasya atha bhavataḥ kim āgamana kāraṇam vyājahāra mahā yogī vacanam praṇipatya tam śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca bhagavan draṣṭum icchāmi girīśam kṛttivāsasam saṃprāptaḥ bhavataḥ sthānam bhagavat darśana utsukaḥ katham sa bhagavān īśaḥ dṛśyaḥ yoga vidām varaḥ mayā acireṇa kutra aham drakṣyāmi tam umāpatim iti āha bhagavān uktaḥ dṛśyate parameśvaraḥ iha īśvaram devadevam muni indrāḥ brahma vādinaḥ dhyāyantaḥ atra āsate devam jāpinaḥ tāpasāḥ ca ye iha devaḥ sa patnīkaḥ bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ iha āśrame purā rudrāt tapaḥ taptvā su dāruṇam lebhe maheśvarāt yogam vasiṣṭhaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ iha eva bhagavān vyasaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ dṛṣṭvā tam paramam jñānam labdhavan īśvara īśvaram iha eva devatāḥ pūrvam kālāt bhītāḥ maheśvaram dṛṣṭavantaḥ haram śrīman nirbhayāḥ nirvṛtim yayuḥ iha ārādhya mahādevam sāvarṇiḥ tapatām varaḥ pravartayāmāsa śubhām kṛtvā vai saṃhitām dvijaḥ paurāṇikām su puṇya arthām sat śiṣyeṣu dvijātiṣu iha eva saṃhitām dṛṣṭvā kāpeyaḥ śāṃśapāyanaḥ mahādevam cakāra imām paurāṇīm tad niyogataḥ dvādaśa eva sahastrāṇi ślokānām puruṣottama iha pravartitā puṇyā dvi aṣṭa sāhastrikā uttarā vāyavīyottaram nāma purāṇam veda saṃmitam iha eva khyāpitam śiṣyaiḥ śāṃśapāyana bhāṣitam yājñavalkyaḥ mahā yogī dṛṣṭvā atra tapasā haram iha eva bhṛguṇā pūrvam taptvā vai paramam tapaḥ śukraḥ maheśvarāt putraḥ labdhaḥ yoga vidām varaḥ draṣṭum arhasi viśveśam ugram bhīmam kapardinam bratam pāśupatam yogam kṛṣṇāya akliṣṭa karmaṇe bhasma uddhūlita sarva aṅgaḥ muṇḍaḥ valkala saṃyutaḥ jajāpa rudram aniśam śiva eka āhita mānasaḥ tatas bahutithe kāle sa umaḥ soma ardha bhūṣaṇaḥ adṛśyata mahādevaḥ vyomni devyāḥ maheśvaraḥ kirīṭinam gadinam citra mālam pinākinam śūlinam devadevam hārdūla carma ambara saṃvṛta aṅgam nṛsiṃha carma āvṛta sarva gātram samudgirantam praṇavam bṛhantam prabhum purāṇam puruṣam purastāt sanātanam yoginam īśitāram aṇoḥ aṇīyāṃsam anantaśaktim prāṇeśvaram śaṃbhum asau dadarśa tadā anvapaśyat giriśasya vāme śaṅkha asi cakra arpita hastam ādyam kṛtāñjalim dakṣiṇatas sureśam haṃsa adhirūḍham puruṣam dadarśa stuvānam īśasya param prabhāvam nandīśvara ādīn amita prabhāvān kumāram agni patimam sa śākham parāśaram tad paratas vasiṣṭham svāyaṃbhuvam ca api manum dadarśa tuṣṭāva mantraiḥ amara pradhānam baddhāñjaliḥ viṣṇuḥ udāra buddhiḥ praṇamya devyā giriśam sa bhaktyā śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca brahma adhipam tvām ṛṣayaḥ vadanti saṃhartā dinakara maṇḍala adhivāsaḥ prāṇaḥ tvam hutavaha vāsava ādi bheda sa tvām ekam śaraṇam upaimi devam īśam sāṃkhyāḥ tvām viguṇam atha āhuḥ eka rūpam yogāḥ tvām satatam upāsate hṛdistham tvām ekam śaraṇam upaimi devam īśam sarva agham praṇudati siddha yogi juṣṭam smṛtvā te pada yugalam bhavat prasādāt yasya aśeṣa vibhāga hīnam amalam hṛdi antara avasthitam sthānam prāhuḥ an ādi madhya nidhanam yasmāt idam jāyate om namaḥ nīlakaṇṭhāya trinetrāya ca raṃhase mahādevāya te nityam īśānāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ pinākine tubhyam namaḥ muṇḍāya daṇḍine namaḥ bhairava nādāya kāla rūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe namaḥ astu te girīśāya svāhākārāya te namaḥ namaḥ mukta aṭṭahāsāya bhīmāya ca namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ te kāma nāśāya namaḥ kāla pramāthine namaḥ bhairava veṣāya harāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe namaḥ ambikā adhipataye paśūnām pataye namaḥ nara nārī śarīrāya sāṃkhyayoga pravartine namaḥ haṃsāya viśvāya mohanāya namaḥ namaḥ namaḥ te prāṇa pālāya ghaṇṭā nāda priyāya ca kapāline namaḥ tubhyam jyotiṣām pataye namaḥ evam hi bhaktyā deveśam abhiṣṭūya sa mādhavaḥ papāta pādayoḥ viprāḥ deva devyoḥ sa daṇḍa vat utthāpya bhagavān sa umaḥ kṛṣṇam keśiniṣūdanam babhāṣe madhuram vākyam megha gambhīra niḥ svanaḥ kimartham puṇḍarīkākṣa tapaḥ taptam tvayā avyaya tvam eva dātā sarveṣām kāmānām kāminām iha tvam hi sā paramā mūrtiḥ mama nārāyaṇa āhvayā na anavāptam tvayā tāta vidyate puruṣottama mā vettha nārāyaṇa anantam ātmānam parameśvaram śrutvā tad vacanam kṛṣṇaḥ prahasan vai vṛṣadhvajam uvāca vīkṣya viśveśam devīm ca himaśailajām jñātam hi bhavatā sarvam svena yogena śaṃkara icchāmi ātma samam putram tvad bhaktam dehi śaṃkaraiḥ tathā astu iti āha viśvātmā prahṛṣṭa manasā haraḥ devīm ālokya girijām keśavam pariṣasvaje tatas sā jagatām mātā śaṅkara ardha śarīriṇī vyājahāra hṛṣīkeśam devī himagirīndrajā vatsa jāne tava anantām niścalām sarvadā acyuta tvam hi nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣāt sarva ātmā puruṣottamaḥ prārthitaḥ daivataiḥ pūrvam saṃjātaḥ daivakī sutaḥ paśya tvam ātmanā ātmānam ātmīyam amalam padam imān imān varān iṣṭān mattaḥ gṛhṇīṣva keśava sarvajña tvam tathā aiśvaryam jñānam tat pārameśvaram īśvare niścalām bhaktim ātmani api param balam evam uktaḥ tayā kṛṣṇaḥ mahādevyā janārdanaḥ maheśvaraḥ pragṛhya kṛṣṇam bhagavant atha īśaḥ munibhiḥ r jagāma kailāsa girim girīśaḥ iti śrī kūrmapūrāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge caturviśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca rarāma bhagavān sa umaḥ keśavena maheśvaraḥ apaśyan tam mahātmānam kailāsa giri vāsinaḥ pūjayāñcakrire kṛṣṇam devadevam atha acyutam catur bāhum udāra aṅgam kāla megha sama prabham kirīṭinam śārṅgapāṇi śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasam dīrgha bāhum viśāla akṣam pītavāsasam acyutam dadhānam urasā mālām vaijayantīm anuttamām bhrājamānam śriyā divyam yuvānam ati komalam bhrājamānaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ cacāra giri kandare gandharva apsarasām mukhyāḥ nāga kanyāḥ ca kṛtsnaśas dṛṣṭvā āścaryam param gatvā harṣāt utphulla ucanāḥ mumucuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi tasya mūrdhani mahātmanaḥ dṛṣṭvā cakamire kṛṣṇam strasta vastra vibhūṣaṇāḥ kāścid gāyanti vividhām gītim gīta viśāradāḥ saṃprekṣya devakī sūnum sundaryaḥ kāma mohitāḥ kāścid vilāsa bahulāḥ nṛtyanti sma tad agratas saṃprekṣya saṃsthitāḥ kāścid papuḥ tad vadana amṛtam kāścid bhūṣaṇa varyāṇi sva aṅgāt ādāya sa ādaram bhūṣayāñcakrire kṛṣṇam kāminyaḥ loka bhūṣaṇam kāścid bhūṣaṇa varyāṇi samādāya tad aṅgataḥ sva ātmānam būṣayāmāsuḥ sva ātma gaiḥ api mādhavam kāścid āgatya kṛṣṇasya samīpam kāma mohitāḥ cucumbuḥ vadana ambhojam hareḥ mugdha mṛga īkṣaṇāḥ prāpayāmāsuḥ loka ādim māyayā tasya mohitāḥ tāsām sa bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ kāmān kamala locanaḥ bahūni kṛtvā rūpāṇi pūrayāmāsa līlayā reme nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān māyayā mohayan jagant gate bahutithe kāle dvāravatyām nivāsinaḥ babhūvuḥ vihvalāḥ bhītāḥ govinda virahe janāḥ kṛṣṇena mārgamāṇaḥ tam himavantam yayau girim a dṛṣṭvā tatra govindam praṇamya śirasā munim ājagāma upamanyum tam purīm dvāravatīm punar tad antare mahā daityāḥ rākṣasāḥ ca ati bhīṣaṇāḥ mājagmuḥ dvārakām śubhrām bhīṣayantaḥ sahastraśas sa tān suparṇaḥ balavān kṛṣṇa tulya parākramaḥ hatvā yuddhena mahatā rakṣati sma purīm śubhām etasmin eva kāle tu nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ dṛṣṭvā kailāsa śikhare kṛṣṇam dvāravatīm gataḥ tam dṛṣṭvā nāradam ṛṣim sarve tatra nivāsinaḥ procuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ nāthaḥ kutra āste bhagavant hariḥ ramate adya mahā yogīm tam dṛṣṭvā aham iha āgataḥ tasya upaśrutya vacanam suparṇaḥ patatām varaḥ jagāma ākāśa gaḥ viprāḥ kailāsam girim uttamam dadarśa devakī sūnum bhavane ratna maṇḍite praṇamya daṇḍa vat bhūmau suparṇaḥ śaṅkaram śivam nivedayāmāsa hareḥ pravṛttim dvārake pure tatas praṇamya śirasā śaṅkaram nīlalohitam bhājagāma purīm kṛṣṇaḥ saḥ anujñātaḥ hareṇa tu āruhya kaśyapa sutam strī gaṇaiḥ abhipūjitaḥ vacobhiḥ amṛta āsvādaiḥ mānitaḥ madhusūdanaḥ vīkṣya yāntam amitra ghnam gandharva apsarasām varāḥ visarjayitvā viśvātmā sarvāḥ eva aṅganāḥ hariḥ yayau sa tūrṇam govindaḥ divyām dvāravatīm purīm śrutvā paura janāḥ tūrṇam kṛṣṇa āgamanam uttamam maṇḍayāñcakrire divyām purīm dvāravatīm śubhām patākābhiḥ viśālābhiḥ dhvajaiḥ ratna pariṣkṛtaiḥ lāja ādibhiḥ purīm ramyām bhūṣayāñcakrire tadā haṅkhān sahastraśas dadhmuḥ voṇāvādān vitenire praviṣṭa mātre govinde purīm dvāravatīm śubhām agāyat madhuram gānam striyaḥ yauvana śālinaḥ dṛṣṭvā nanṛtuḥ īśānam sthitāḥ prāsāda mūrdhasu praviśya bhavanam kṛṣṇaḥ āśīrvāda abhivardhitaḥ mahā yogī bhāti devībhiḥ anvitaḥ su ramye maṇḍape śubhre śaṅkha ādyaiḥ parivāritaḥ bhitas mukhyaiḥ strī sahastraiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ bhrājate mālayā devaḥ yathā devyā samanvitaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ pūrva jātāḥ mārkaṇḍeya ādayaḥ dvijāḥ tatas sa bhagavān kṛṣṇaḥ mārkaṇḍeyam samāgatam nanāma utthāya śirasā sva āsanam ca dadau hariḥ saṃpūjya tān ṛṣi gaṇān praṇāmena mahā bhujaḥ hariḥ dattvā tad abhivāñchitān snātvā śukla ambaraḥ bhānum upatiṣṭhat kṛtāñjaliḥ jajāpa jāpyam vidhivat prekṣamāṇaḥ divākaram tarpayāmāsa deveśaḥ deveśaḥ devān muni gaṇān pitṝn pūjayāmāsa liṅga stham bhūteśam bhūtibhūṣaṇam samāpya niyamam sarvam niyantā asau nṛṇām svayam bhojayitvā muni varam brāhmaṇān abhipūjya ca kṛtvā ātma yogam vipra indrāḥ mārkaṇḍeyena ca acyutaḥ paurāṇikīḥ puṇyāḥ cakre putra ādibhiḥ vṛtaḥ atha etat sarvam akhilam dṛṣṭvā karma mahā muniḥ mārkaṇḍeyaḥ hasan kṛṣṇam babhāṣe madhuram vacaḥ uvāca kaḥ samārādhyate devaḥ bhavatā karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ bhāra avataraṇa arthāya jātaḥ vṛṣṇi kule prabhuḥ tam abravīt mahā bāhuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ brahma vidām varaḥ śṛṇvatām eva putrāṇām sarveṣām prahasan iva śrī bhagavant uvāca tathā api devam īśānam pūjayāmi sanātanam pūjayāmi tathā api īśam jānan na etat param śivam na vai paśyanti tam devam māyayā mohitāḥ janāḥ tatas aham sva ātmanaḥ mūlam jñāpayan pūjayāmi tam na ca liṅga arcanāt puṇyam loke ismin bhīti nāśanam tathā liṅge hitāya eṣām lokānām pūjayet śivam yaḥ aham tat liṅgam iti āhuḥ veda vāda vidaḥ janāḥ tatas aham ātmam īśānam pūjayāmi ātmanā eva tu tasya eva paramā mūrtiḥ tad mayaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ eṣa devaḥ mahādevaḥ sadā saṃsāra bhīrubhiḥ dhyeyaḥ pūjyaḥ ca vandyaḥ ca jñeyaḥ liṅge maheśvaraḥ uvāca kim tat liṅgam suraśreṣṭha liṅge saṃpūjyate ca kaḥ brūhi kṛṣṇa viśāla akṣa gahanam hi etat uttamam purā ca ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame prabodha artham brahmaṇaḥ mama prādurbhūtaḥ svayam śivaḥ tasmāt kālāt samārabhya brahmā ca aham sadā eva hi pūjayāvaḥ mahādevam lokānām hita kāmyayā uvāca katham liṅgam abhūt pūrvam aiśvaram paramam padam prabodha artham svayam kṛṣṇa vaktum arhasi sāṃpratam śrī bhagavant uvāca mayam sahastra śīrṣā bhūtvā aham sahastra akṣaḥ sahastrapād sahastra bāhuḥ yukta ātmā śayitaḥ aham sanātanaḥ koṭi sūrya pratīkāśam bhrājamānam śriyā āvṛtam mahā yogam puruṣam kāñcana prabham kṛṣṇa ajira dharam devam ṛc yajuḥ sāmbhiḥ stutam nimeṣa mātreṇa sa mām prāptaḥ yoga vidām varaḥ vyājahāra svayam brahmā smayamānaḥ mahā dyutiḥ aham kartā hi lokānām svayaṃbhūḥ prapitāmahaḥ aham kartāsmi lokānām saṃhartā ca punar punar evam vivāde vitate māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ prabodha artham param liṅgam prādurbhūtam śiva ātmakam kāla anala sama prakhyam jvālā mālā samākulam tadā āśu samayam kṛtvā gatau ūrdhvam adhas ca dvau pitāmahaḥ api aham na antam jñātavantau samāḥ śatam proccārantau mahā nādam oṅkāram paramam padam prahva añjali puṭa upetau śaṃbhum tuṣṭuvatuḥ param brahma viṣṇū ūcatuḥ anādi mala saṃsāra roga vaidyāya śaṃbhave namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye jvālā mālā vṛta aṅgāya jvalana stambha rūpiṇe namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye ādi madhya anta hīnāya sva bāva amala dīptaye namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye pradhānapuruṣa īśāya vyoma rūpāya vedhase namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye namaḥ śivāya śāntāya brahmaṇe liṅga mūrtaye evam saṃstūyamānaḥ tu vyaktaḥ bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ bhāti devaḥ mahā yogī sūrya koṭi sama prabhaḥ pinākapāṇiḥ bhagavān kṛttivāsāḥ triśūlabhṛt paśyetam mām mahādevam bhayam sarvam pramucyatām yuvām prasūtau gātrebhyaḥ mama pūrvam sanātanau ayam me dakṣiṇe pārśve brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ vāma pārśve ca mama viṣṇuḥ pālakaḥ hṛdaye haraḥ evam uktvā atha mām devaḥ mahādevaḥ svayam śivaḥ āliṅgya devam brahmānam prasāda abhimukhaḥ abhavat tatas prahṛṣṭa manasau praṇipatya maheśvaram ūcatuḥ prekṣya tad vaktram nārāyaṇa pitāmahau tatas sa bhagavant īśaḥ prahasan parameśvaraḥ uvāca mām mahādevaḥ prītaḥ prītena cetasā pralaya sthiti sargāṇām kartā tvam dharaṇī pate tridhā bhinnaḥ asmi aham viṣṇo brahma viṣṇu hara ākhyayā sarga rakṣā laya guṇaiḥ nirguṇaḥ api nirañjanaḥ saṃmoham tyaja bho viṣṇo pālaya enam pitāmaham bhaviṣyati eṣa bhagavān tava putraḥ sanātanaḥ śūlapāṇiḥ bhaviṣyāmi krodha jaḥ te putrakaḥ tatas prabhṛti lokeṣu liṅga arcā su pratiṣṭhitā etat liṅgasya māhātmyam bhāṣitam te mayā anagha etat budhyanti yoga jñāḥ na devāḥ na ca dānavāḥ etat hi paramam jñānam avyaktam śiva saṃjñitam yena sūkṣmam acintyam tat paśyanti jñāna vakṣuṣaḥ namaḥ veda rahasyāya nīlakaṇṭhāya vai namaḥ vibhīṣaṇāya śāntāya sthāṇave hetave namaḥ śaṃkarāya maheśāya girīśāya śivāya ca saṃsāra sāgarāt asmāt acirāt uttariṣyasi evam sa vāsudevena vyāhṛtaḥ muni puṃgavaḥ manasā devam īśānam viśvatomukham praṇamya śirasā kṛṣṇam anujñātaḥ mahā muniḥ jagāma ca īpsitam deśam devadevasya śūlinaḥ yaḥ imam śrāvayet nityam liṅga adhyāyam anuttamam śṛṇuyāt vā paṭhet vā api sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate vāsudevasya vipra indrāḥ pāpam muñciti mānavaḥ evam āha mahā yogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas labdha varaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ jāmbavatyām maheśvarāt ajījanat mahātmānam sāmbam ātmajam uttamam tau ubhau guṇa saṃpannau kṛṣṇasya eva apare tanū hatvā ca kaṃsam narakam anyān ca śataśas asurān vijitya līlayā śakram jitvā bāṇam mahā asuram sthāpayitvā jagat kṛtsnam loke dharmān ca śāśvatān cakre nārāyaṇaḥ gantum sva sthānam buddhim uttamām etasmin antare viprāḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ kṛṣṇam īśvaram ājagmuḥ dvārakām draṣṭum kṛta kāryam sanātanam sa tān uvāca viśvātmā praṇipatya abhipūjya ca na upaviṣṭān vai saha rāmeṇa dhīmatā gamiṣye tat param sthānam svakīyam viṣṇu saṃjñitam kṛtāni sarva kāryāṇi prasīdadhvam muni īśvarāḥ idam kali yugam ghoram saṃprāptam adhunā aśubham mad jñānam brāhmaṇānām hita āvaham teṣām naśyatu tat pāpam bhaktānām puruṣottame yeḥ acayiṣyanti imām bhaktyā nityam kali yuge dvijāḥ bhānāḥ veda dṛṣṭena te gamiṣyanti tat padam ye brāhmaṇāḥ vaṃśa jātāḥ yuṣmākam vai sahastraśas teṣām nārāyaṇe bhaktiḥ bhaviṣyati kalau yuge parāt parataram yānti nārāyaṇa parāyaṇāḥ dhyānam homam tapaḥ taptam jñānam yajña ādikaḥ vidhiḥ teṣām vinaśyati kṣipram ye nindanti pinākinam yaḥ mām samāśrayet nityam ekāntam bhāvam āśritaḥ vinindya devam īśānam saḥ yāti naraka ayutam tasmāt sā parihartavyā nindā paśupatau dvijāḥ manasā manasā vācā tad bhakteṣu api yatnatas ye tu dakṣa adhvare śaptāḥ dadhīyena dvijottamāḥ dviṣantaḥ devam īśānam yuṣmākam vaṃśa saṃbhavāḥ śaptāḥ ca gautamena urvyām na saṃbhāṣyāḥ dvijottamaiḥ iti evam uktāḥ kṛṣṇena sarve eva mahā ṛṣayaḥ om iti uktvā yayuḥ tūrṇam svāni sthānāni sattamāḥ tatas nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ līlayā eva jagat mayaḥ iti eṣa vaḥ samāsena rājñām vaṃśaḥ anukīrtitaḥ na śakyaḥ vistarāt vaktum kim bhūyas śrotum icchatha yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api vaṃśānām kathanam śubham iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca iti caturyugam eṣām svabhāvam sūtaiḥ adya kathayasva samāsatas uvāca gate nārāyaṇe kṛṣṇe svam eva paramam padam pārthaḥ parama dharma ātmā pāṇḍavaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ kṛtvā ca iva uttara vidhim śokena mahatā āvṛtaḥ apaśyat pathini gacchantam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam munim śiṣyaiḥ praśiṣyaiḥ abhitas saṃvṛtam brahma vādinam papāta daṇḍa vat bhūmau tyaktvā śokam tadā arjunaḥ uvāca parama prītaḥ kasmāt deśāt mahā mune idānīm gacchasi kṣipram kam vā deśam prati prabho saṃdarśanāt vai bhavataḥ śokaḥ mama vipulaḥ gataḥ idānīm mama yat kāryam brūhi padma dala īkṣaṇa tam uvāca mahā yogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ svayam upaviśya śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ muniḥ idam kali yugam ghoram saṃprāptam pāṇḍu nandana tatas gacchāmi devasya vārāṇasīm mahā purīm bhaviṣyanti mahā pāpāḥ varṇa āśrama vivarjitāḥ na anyat paśyāmi jantūnām muktvā vārāṇasīm purīm sarva pāpa praśamanam prāyaścittam kalau yuge kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca sarveṣu eteṣu vai narāḥ bhaviṣyanti mahātmānaḥ dhārmikāḥ satya vādinaḥ tvam hi lokeṣu vikhyātaḥ dhṛtimān jana vatsalaḥ pālaya adya param dharmam svakīyam mucyase bhayāt pṛṣṭavan praṇipatya asau yuga dharmān dvijottamāḥ praṇamya devam īśānam yuga dharmān sanātanān na śakyate mayā pārtha vistareṇa abhibhāṣitum ādyam kṛta yugam proktam tatas tretā yugam budhaiḥ tṛtīyam dvāparam pārthaiḥ caturtham kaliḥ ucyate dhyānam param kṛta yuge tretāyām jñānam ucyate brahmā kṛta yuge devaḥ tretāyām bhagavān raviḥ dvāpare daivatam viṣṇuḥ kalau rudraḥ maheśvaraḥ brahmā viṣṇuḥ tathā sūryaḥ sarve eva kaliṣu api ādye kṛta yuge dharmaḥ catuṣpādaḥ sanātanaḥ tretā yuge tri pādaḥ syāt dvi pādaḥ dvāpare sthitaḥ tri pāda hīnaḥ tiṣye tu sattā mātreṇa tiṣṭhati tu mithuna utpattiḥ vṛttiḥ sākṣāt rasa ullasā prajāḥ tṛptāḥ sadā sarvāḥ sat ānandāḥ ca bhoginaḥ adhama uttama tvam na asti āsām nirviśeṣāḥ purañjaya tulyam āyuḥ sukham rūpam tāsām tasmin kṛte yuge viśokāḥ sattva bahulāḥ ekānta bahulāḥ tathā dhyāna niṣṭhāḥ tapas niṣṭhāḥ mahādeva parāyaṇāḥ tāḥ vai niṣkāma cāriṇyaḥ nityam mudita mānasāḥ rasollāsā kāla yogāt tretā ākhye naśyate tatas tasyām siddhau praṇaṣṭāyām anyā siddhiḥ avartata apām saukṣmye pratihate tadā megha ātmanā tu vai sakṛt eva tayā vṛṣṭyā saṃyukte pṛthivī tale prādurāsan tadā tāsām vṛkṣāḥ vai gṛha saṃjñitāḥ tatas kālena mahatā tāsām eva viparyayeṇa tāsām tu tena tad kāla bhāvinā praṇaśyanti tatas sarve vṛkṣāḥ te gṛha saṃjñitāḥ tatas teṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāntāḥ maithuna udbhavāḥ abhidhyāyanti tām siddhim satya abhidhyāyinaḥ tadā prādurbabhūvuḥ tāsām tu vṛkṣāḥ te gṛha saṃjñitāḥ vastrāṇi te prasūyante phalāni ābharaṇāni ca teṣu eva jāyate tāsām gandha varṇa rasa anvitam amākṣikam mahā vīryam puṭake puṭake madhu hṛṣṭa puṣṭāḥ tayā siddhyā sarvāḥ vai vigata jvarāḥ tatas kāla antareṇa eva punar lobha āvṛtāḥ tadā vṛkṣān tān paryagṛhṇanta madhu ca amākṣikam balāt tāsām tena apacāreṇa punar lobha kṛtena vai praṇaṣṭām adhunā sārdham kalpavṛkṣāḥ kvacid kvacid śīta varṣa ātapaiḥ tīvraiḥ tatas tāḥ duḥkhitāḥ bhṛśam dvandvaiḥ saṃpīḍyamānāḥ tu cakruḥ āvaraṇāni ca kṛtvā dvandva pratīghātān vārttā upāyam acintayan naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdham kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā tatas prādur babhau tāsām siddhiḥ tretā yuge punar hi tāsām vṛṣṭi udakāni iha yāni nimnaiḥ gatāni tu avahan vṛṣṭi saṃtatyā strotaḥ sthānāni nimnagāḥ ye punar tat apām stokāḥ āpannāḥ pṛthivī tale pām bhūṇeḥ ca saṃyogāt oṣadhyaḥ tāḥ tadā abhavan a phāla kṛṣṭāḥ ca anuptāḥ grāmya āraṇyāḥ caturdaśa ṛtu puṣpa phalaiḥ ca eva vṛkṣa gulmāḥ ca jajñire tatas prādurabhūt tāsām rāgaḥ lobhaḥ ca sarvaśas avaśyam bhāvinā ar'the na tretā yuga vaśena vai tatas tāḥ paryagṛhṇanta nadī kṣetrāṇi parvatān viparyayeṇa tāsām tāḥ oṣadhyaḥ viviśuḥ mahīm pitāmaha niyogena dudoha pṛthivīm pṛthuḥ tatas tāḥ jagṛhuḥ sarvāḥ anyonyam krodha mūrchitāḥ vasu dāra dhana ādyān tu balāt kāla balena tu maryādāyāḥ pratiṣṭhā artham jñātvā etat bhagavān ajaḥ sasarja kṣatriyān brahmā brāhmaṇānām hitāya ca varṇa āśrama vyavasthām ca tretāyām kṛtavān prabhuḥ dvāpareṣu atha vidyante mati bhedāḥ sadā nṛṇām rāgaḥ lobhaḥ tathā yuddham tattvānām aviniścayaḥ vedavyāsaiḥ caturdhā tu vyasyate dvāpara ādiṣu ṛṣi putraiḥ punar bhedāt bhidyante dṛṣṭi vibhramaiḥ saṃhitāḥ ṛk yajuḥ sāmnām saṃhanyante śruta ṛṣibhiḥ sāmānyāt vaikṛtāt ca eva dṛṣṭi bhedaiḥ kvacid kvacid brāhmaṇam kalpasūtrāṇi mantra pravacanāni ca itihāsa purāṇāni dharma śāstrāṇi suvrata avṛṣṭiḥ maraṇam ca eva tathā eva vāyādhi upadravāḥ vāc manaḥ kāya jaiḥ duḥkhaiḥ nirvedaḥ jāyate nṛṇām nirvedāt jāyate teṣām duḥkha mokṣa vicāraṇā vicāraṇāt ca vairāgyam vairāgyāt doṣa darśanam doṣāṇām darśanāt ca eva dvāpare jñāna saṃbhavaḥ eṣā rajas tamaḥ yuktā vṛttiḥ vai dvāpare smṛtā dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tiṣye māyām asūyām ca vadham ca eva tapasvinām sādhayanti narāḥ nityam tamasā vyākulīkṛtāḥ anāvṛṣṭi bhayam ghoram deśānām ca viparyayaḥ adhārmikāḥ anācārāḥ mahā kopa alpa cetasaḥ anṛtam vadanti te lubdhāḥ tiṣye jātāḥ su dus prajāḥ duriṣṭaiḥ duradhītaiḥ ca durācāraiḥ durāgamaiḥ viprāṇām karma doṣaiḥ ca prajānām jāyate bhayam śūdrāṇām mantra yaunaiḥ ca saṃbandhaḥ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha rājānaḥ sūdra bhūyiṣṭhāḥ brāhmaṇān bādhayanti ca bhrūṇa hatyā vīra hatyā prajāyete nareśvara snānam homam japam dānam devatānām tathā ar'canam vinindanti mahādevam brāhmaṇān puruṣottamam āmnāya dharma śāstrāṇi purāṇāni kalau yuge kurvanti a veda dṛṣṭāni karmāṇi vividhāni tu kuśīla caryāḥ pāṣaṇḍaiḥ vṛthak rūpaiḥ samāvṛtāḥ aṭṭa śūlāḥ janapadāḥ śiva śūlāḥ catuṣpathāḥ pramadāḥ keśa śūlinyaḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge śukla danta ajina ākhyāḥ ca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāya vāsasaḥ śasya caurāḥ bhaviṣyanti tathā caila abhimarṣiṇaḥ duḥ kha pracura tā alpa āyuḥ deha utsādaḥ sa roga tā kāṣāyiṇaḥ atha nirgranthāḥ tathā kāpālikāḥ ca ye veda vikrayiṇaḥ ca anye tīrtha vikrayiṇaḥ pare dṛṣṭvā na calanti tāḍayanti dvijendrān ca śūdrāḥ rāja upajīvinaḥ jñātvā na hiṃsate rājā kalau kāla balena tu śūdrān abhyarcayanti alpa śruta bhagya bala anvitāḥ na prekṣante arcitān ca api śūdrāḥ dvijavarān nṛpa sevā avasaram ālokya dvāri tiṣṭhanti ca dvijāḥ vāhana sthān samāvṛtya śūdrān śūdra upajīvinaḥ adhyāpayanti vai vedān śūdrān śūdra upajīvinaḥ paṭhanti vaidikān mantrān nāstikyam ghoram āśritāḥ tapaḥ yajña phalānām ca vikretāraḥ dvijottamāḥ yatayaḥ ca bhaviṣyanti śataśas atha sahastraśas nāśayanti hi adhītāni na adhigacchanti ca anagha vāma pāśupata ācārāḥ tathā vai pāñcarātrikāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau tasmin brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ tathā jñāna karmaṇi uparate loke niṣkriya tām gate kīṭa mūṣaka sarpāḥ ca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān kurvānti ca avatārāṇi brāhmaṇānām kuleṣu vai dadhīca śāpa nirdagdhāḥ purā dakṣa adhvare dvijāḥ nindanti ca mahādevam tamasā āviṣṭa cetasaḥ ye ca anye śāpa nirdagdhāḥ gautamasya mahātmanaḥ sarve te ca bhaviṣyanti brāhmaṇa ādyāḥ sva jātiṣu vinindanti hṛṣīkeśam brāhmaṇān brahma vādinaḥ bāhya vrata ācārāḥ durācārāḥ vṛthak śramāḥ tamasā āviṣṭa manasaḥ vaiḍāla vṛttikā adhamāḥ kalau rudraḥ mahādevaḥ lokānām īśvaraḥ paraḥ na devatā bhavet nṛṇām devatānām ca daivatam kariṣyati avatārāṇi śaṅkaraḥ nīlalohitaḥ śrauta smārta pratiṣṭhā artham bhaktānām hita kāmyayā upadekṣyati tad jñānam śiṣyāṇām brahma saṃjñitam sarva vedānta sāram hi dharmān veda nidarśitān anāyāsena su mahat puṇyam āpnoti mānavaḥ aneka doṣa duṣṭasya kaleḥ eṣa mahān guṇaḥ vrajet ye namanti virūpākṣam īśānam kṛttivāsasam evaṃvidhe kali yuge doṣāṇām eka śodhanam mahādeva namaskāraḥ dhyānam dānam iti śrutiḥ tasmāt anīśvarān anyān tyaktvā devam maheśvaram samāśrayet virūpākṣam yadi icchet paramam padam na arcayanti iha ye rudram śivam tridaśa vanditam teṣām dānam tapaḥ yajñaḥ vṛthak jīvitam eva ca śaṃbhave sthāṇave nityam śivāya parameṣṭhine namaḥ śomāya rudrāya mahāgrāsāya hetave prapadye aham virūpākṣam śaraṇyam brahmacāriṇam mahādevam mahā yogam īśānam ca ambikāpatim yoginām yoga dātāram yoga māyā samāvṛtam yoginām kurum ācāryam yogi gamyam pinākinam saṃsāra tāraṇam rudram brahmāṇam brahmaṇaḥ adhipam śāśvatam sarvagam brahmaṇyam brāhmaṇapriyam nīlakaṇṭham viśvamūrti vyāpinam viśvaretasam kālāgnim kāla dahanam kāma dam kāma nāśanam namasye giriśam devam candra avayava bhūṣaṇam
