vilohitam lelihāna māhityam parameṣṭhinam ugram paśupatim bhīmam bhāskaram tamasaḥ param iti etat lakṣaṇam proktam yugānām vai samāsatas atīta anāgatānām vai yāvat manvantara kṣayaḥ manvantareṇa ca ekena sarvāṇi eva antarāṇi vai manvantareṣu sarveṣu atīta anāgateṣu vai evam uktaḥ bhagavatā kirīṭī śvetavāhanaḥ babhāra paramām bhaktim īśāne avyabhicāriṇīm namaścakāra tam ṛṣim kṛṣṇadvaipāyanam prabhum sarvajñam sarva kartāram viṣṇum vyavasthitam tam uvāca punar vyāsaḥ pātham parapuraṃjayam karābhyām su śubhābhyām ca saṃspṛśya praṇatam muniḥ dṛṣṭavān asi tam devam viśvākṣam viśvatomukham tat aiśvaram divyam yathāvat viditam tvayā svayam eva hṛṣīkeśaḥ prītyā uvāca sanātanaḥ majasva parayā bhaktyā śaraṇyam śaraṇam śivam evam uktvā sa bhagavān anugṛhya arjunam prabhuḥ jagāma śaṃkara purīm samārādhayitum bhavam pāṇḍaveyaḥ api tat vākyāt saṃprāpya śaraṇam śivam na arjunena samaḥ śaṃbhoḥ bhaktyā bhūtaḥ bhaviṣyati muktvā satyavatī sūnum kṛṣṇam vā devakī sutam pārāśaryāya munaye vyāsāya amita tejase kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ sākṣāt viṣṇuḥ eva sanātanaḥ namaḥ kurudhvam tam ṛṣim kṛṣṇam satyavatī sutam pārāśaryam mahātmānam yoginam viṣṇum avyayam preṇemuḥ tam mahātmānam vyāsam satyavatī sutam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ prāpya vārāṇasīm divyām kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ kim akārṣot mahābuddhiḥ śrotum kautūhalam hi naḥ uvāca prāpya vārāṇasī divyām upaspṛśya mahā muniḥ pūjayāmāsa jāhnavyām devam viśveśvaram śivam tam āgatam punim dṛṣṭvā tatra ye nivasanti vai pūjayāñcakrire vyāsam munayaḥ muni puṃgavam papracchuḥ praṇatāḥ sarve kathāḥ pāpa vināśanīḥ mahādeva āśrayāḥ puṇyāḥ mokṣa dharmān sanātanān sa ca api kathayāmāsa sarvajñaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ teṣām madhye muni indrāṇām vyāsa śiṣyaḥ mahā muniḥ pṛṣṭavan jaiminiḥ vyāsam gūḍham artham sanātanam kecid dhyānam praśaṃsanti dharmam eva apare janāḥ anye sāṃkhyam tathā yogam tapaḥ tu anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ ahiṃsām satyam api anye saṃnyāsam apare viduḥ kecid dayām praśaṃsanti dānam adhyayanam tathā kim eteṣām bhavet jyāyaḥ prabrūhi muni puṃgava śrutvā sa jaimineḥ vākyam kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ prāha gambhīrayā vācā praṇamya vṛṣaketanam sādhu sādhu mahābhāga yat pṛṣṭam bhavatā mune vakṣye guhyatamāt guhyam śruṇvantu anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ īśvareṇa purā proktam jñānam etat sanātanam gūḍham aprājña vidviṣṭam sevitam sūkṣma darśibhiḥ na aśraddadhāne dātavyam na abhakte parameṣṭhinaḥ na veda vidviṣu śubham jñāna nānām jñānam uttamam meru śṛṅge purā devam īśānam tripura dviṣam devadeva mahādeva bhaktānām ārti nāśana katham tvām puruṣaḥ devam acirāt eva paśyati āyāsa bahulā loke yāni ca anyāni śaṃkaraiḥ yena vibrānta cittānām yoginām karmiṇām api dṛśyaḥ hi bhagavān sūkṣmaḥ sarveṣām atha dehinām etat guhyatamam jñānam gūḍham brahma ādi sevitama hitāya sarva bhaktānām brūhi kāma aṅga nāśana uvāca avācyam etat vijñānam jñānam ajñaiḥ bahiṣkṛtam param guhyatamam kṣetram mama vārāṇasī purī sarveṣām eva bhūtānām saṃsāra arṇava tāriṇī tatra bhaktāḥ mahādevi madīyam vratam āsthitāḥ nivasanti mahātmānaḥ param niyamam āsthitāḥ uttamam sarva tīrthānām sthānānām uttamam ca tat jñānānām uttamam jñānam avimuktam param mama sthāna antaram pavitrāṇi tīrthāni āyatanāni ca śmaśāna saṃsthitāni eva divya bhūmi gatāni ca ayuktāḥ tat na paśyanti yuktāḥ paśyanti cetasā pālaḥ bhūtvā jagant idam saṃharāmi atra sundari devi idam sarva guhyānām sthānam priyatamam mama dattam japtam hutam ca iṣṭam tapaḥ taptam kṛtam ca yat dhyānam adhyayanam jñānam sarvam tatra akṣayam bhavet brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ye varṇa saṃkarāḥ striyaḥ mlecchāḥ ca ye ca anye saṃkīrṇāḥ pāpa yonayaḥ koṭāḥ pipīlikāḥ ca eva ye ca anye mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ candra ardha maulayaḥ tri akṣāḥ mahā vṛṣabha vāhanāḥ na avimukte mṛtaḥ kaścid narakam yāti kilbiṣī īśvara anugṛhītāḥ hi sarve yānti parām gatim mokṣam su durlabham matvā saṃsāram ca ati bhīṣaṇam aśmanā caraṇau hatvā vārāṇasyām vaset naraḥ yatra tatra vipannasya gatiḥ saṃsāra mokṣaṇā aprabuddhāḥ na paśyanti mama māyā vimohitāḥ avimuktam na sevanti mūḍhāḥ ye tamasā āvṛtāḥ viṣ mūtra retasām madhye te vasanti punar punar sa yāti paramam sthānam yatra gatvā na śocati janma mṛtyu jarā muktam param yāti śiva ālayam apunar maraṇānām hi sā gatiḥ mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām tām prāpya kṛtakṛtyaḥ syāt iti manyanti paṇḍatāḥ prāpyate gatiḥ utkṛṣṭā yā avimukte tu labhyate nānā varṇāḥ vivarṇāḥ ca caṇḍāla ādyāḥ jugupsitāḥ pūrṇa dehāḥ ye viśiṣṭaiḥ pātakaiḥ tathā bheṣajam paramam teṣām avimuktam viduḥ budhāḥ avimuktam param jñānam avimuktam param padam kṛtvā vai naiṣṭhikīm dīkṣām avimukte vasanti ye teṣām tat paramam jñānam dadāmi ante param padam prāyāgam naimiṣam puṇyam śrīśailaḥ atha mahā layaḥ bhadrakarṇam ca gayā puṣkaram eva ca śāligrāmam ca kubjāmram kokāmukham anuttamam prabhāsam vijayeśānam gokarṇam bhadrakarṇakam etāni puṇya sthānāni trailokye viśrutāni ha na yāsyanti param mokṣam vārāṇasyām yathā mṛtāḥ vārāṇasyām viśeṣeṇa gaṅgā tripathagāminī praviṣṭā nāśayet pāpam janma antara śataiḥ kṛtam anyatra sulabhā gaṅgā śrāddham dānam tapaḥ japaḥ vāyubhakṣaḥ ca satatam vārāṇasyām stitaḥ naraḥ yadi pāpaḥ yadi śaṭhaḥ yadi vā adhārmikaḥ naraḥ asīm samāsādya punāti sakalam naraḥ yeḥ acayanti stuvanti vai sarva pāpa vinirmuktāḥ te vijñeyāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ anyatra yoga jñānābhyām saṃnyāsāt athavā anyatas ye bhaktāḥ devadeveśe vārāṇasyām vasanti vai jñāna ajñāna abhiniṣṭhānām paramānandam icchatām yāni ca eva avimuktasya dehe tu uktāni kṛtsnaśas purī vārāṇasī tebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ hi adhikā aśubhā yatra sākṣāt mahādevaḥ dehānte svayam īśvaraḥ ekena janmanā devi vārāṇasyām tat āpnuyāt yathā avimukta āditye vārāṇasyām vyavasthitam madhye vārāṇasī purī mad param sthānam na bhūtam na bhaviṣyati yatra nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ mahādevaḥ divā īśvaraḥ tatra devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ upāsate mām satatam devadevam pitāmaham mahāpātakinaḥ ye ca ye tebhyaḥ pāpa kṛttamāḥ ha vārāṇasīm samāsādya te yānti paramām gatim vimucyate etat rahasyam vedānām purāṇānām ca suvratāḥ avimukta āśrayam jñānam na kaścid vetti tattvāt devatānām ṛṣīṇām ca śṛṇvatām parameṣṭhinām yathā nārāyaṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ devānām puruṣottamaḥ yathā īśvarāṇām giriśaḥ sthānānām ca etat uttamam kali kalmaṣa saṃbhūtā yeṣām upahatā matiḥ na teṣām veditum śakyam sthānam tat parameṣṭhinaḥ teṣām vinaśyati kṣipram iha amutra ca pātakam yāni ca iha prakurvanti pātakāni kṛta ālayāḥ nāśayet tāni sarvāṇi devaḥ kāla tanuḥ śivaḥ āgacchatām idam sthānam sevitum mokṣa kāṅkṣiṇām mṛtānām ca punar janam na bhūyas bhava sāgare tasmāt sarva prayatnena vārāṇasyām vaset naraḥ yogī vā api athavā ayogī pāpī vā puṇya kṛttamaḥ uvāca iti evam uktvā bhagavān vyāsaḥ veda vidām varaḥ saha eva śiṣya pravaraiḥ vārāṇasyām cacāra ha iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrvam vibhāge ekonatriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca sa śiṣyaiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ dhīmān guruḥ dvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ jagāma vipulam liṅgam oṃkāram mukti dāyakam tatra abhyarcya mahādevam śiṣyaiḥ saha mahā muniḥ provāca tasya māhātmyam munīnām bhāvitātmanām idam tat vimalam liṅgam oṅkāram nāma śobhanam sevitam sūribhiḥ nityam vārāṇasyām vimokṣa dam atra sākṣāt mahādevaḥ pañca āyatana vigrahaḥ yat tat pāśupatam jñānam pañcārtham iti śabdyate śānti atītā tathā śāntiḥ vidyā ca eva parā kalā pratiṣṭhā ca nivṛttiḥ ca pañca artham liṅgam aiśvaram pañcānām api devānām brahma ādīnām sat āśrayam oṃkāra bodhakam liṅgam pañcāyatanam ucyate saṃsmaret aiśvaram liṅgam pañcāyatanam avyayam dehānte tat param jyotiḥ ānandam viśate budhaḥ atra devarṣayaḥ pūrvam siddhāḥ brahmarṣayaḥ tathā upāsya devam īśānam prāptavantaḥ param padam matsyodaryāḥ taṭe puṇyam sthānam guhyatamam śubham kṛttivāseśvaram liṅgaḥ madhyameśvaram uttamam maheśvaram tathā uṅkāram kapardeśvaram eva ca etāni guhya liṅgāni vārāṇasyām dvijottamāḥ na kaścid iha jānāti vinā śambhoḥ anugrahāt evam uktvā yayau kṛṣṇaḥ pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ tivāsa īśvaram liṅgam draṣṭum devasya śūlinaḥ samabhyarcya tathā śiṣyaiḥ māhātmyam kṛttivāsasaḥ brāhmaṇān hantum āyātaḥ ye atra nityam upāsate teṣām liṅgāt mahādevaḥ prādurāsīt trilocanaḥ rakṣaṇa artham dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ bhaktānām bhakta vatsalaḥ hatvā gaja ākṛtim daityam śūlena avajñayā haraḥ vasaḥ tasya akarot kṛttim kṛttivāsa īśvaraḥ tatas atra siddhim parām prāptāḥ munayaḥ muni puṃgavāḥ tena eva ca śarīreṇa prāptāḥ tat paramam padam vidyāḥ vidyeśvarāḥ rudrāḥ ca prakīrtitāḥ tat kṛttivāsa īśvaram liṅgam nityam āvṛtya saṃsthitāḥ jñātvā kali yugam ghoram adharma bahulam janāḥ kṛtti vāsam na muñcanti kṛtārthāḥ te na saṃśayaḥ ālayaḥ sarva siddhānām etat sthānam vadanti hi yuge yuge hi atra dāntāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāra āgāḥ dhyāyanti hṛdaye devam sthāṇum sarva antaram śivam gāyanti siddhāḥ kila gītakāni ye vārāṇasyām nivasanti viprāḥ ye kṛttivāsam śaraṇam prapannāḥ saṃprāpya loke jagatām abhīṣṭam rārādhayanti prabhum īśitāram indrāḥ yajanti yajñaiḥ abhisaṃdhi hīnāḥ sthāṇum prapadye giriśam purāṇam smarāmi rudram hṛdaye niviṣṭam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge triṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca samābhāṣya munīn dhīmān devadevasya śūlinaḥ jagāma liṅgam tat draṣṭum kapardeśvaram avyayam snātvā tatra vidhānena tarpayitvā pitṝn dvijāḥ piśācamocane tīrthe pūjayāmāsa śūlinam tatra āścaryam apaśyan te munayaḥ guruṇā saha menire kṣetra māhātmyam praṇemuḥ giriśam haram kaścid abhyājagāma idam śārdūlaḥ ghora rūpadhṛk mṛgīm ekām bhakṣayitum kapardeśvaram uttamam tatra sā bhīta hṛdayā kṛtvā kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam dhāvamānā su saṃbhrāntā vyāghrasya vaśam āgatā tām vidārya nakhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śārdūlaḥ su mahā balaḥ jagāma ca anyam vijanam deśam dṛṣṭvā muni īśvarān mṛta mātrā ca sā bālā kapardeśa agratas mṛgī adṛśyata mahā jvālā vyomni sūrya sama prabhā tri netrā nīla kaṇṭhā ca śaśāṅka aṅkita mūrdhajā vṛṣa adhirūḍhā puruṣaiḥ tādṛśaiḥ eva saṃvṛtā puṣpa vṛṣṭim khecarāḥ tasya mūrdhani gaṇeśvaraḥ svayam bhūtvā na dṛṣṭaḥ tad kṣaṇāt tatas dṛṣṭvā etat āścarya varam jaimini pramukhāḥ dvijāḥ teṣām provāca bhagavān deva agre ca upaviśya saḥ kapardeśasya māhātmyam praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam smṛtvā eva aśeṣa pāpa ogham kṣipram asya vimuñcati kāma krodha ādayaḥ doṣāḥ vārāṇasī nivāsinām dhyāyatām atra niyatam yoginām śānta cetasām yoga saṃsiddhiḥ sā ṣaṣ māse na saṃśayaḥ brahmahatyā ādayaḥ pāpāḥ vinaśyanti asya pūjanāt piśācamocane kuṇḍe snātasya atra samīpatas asmin kṣetre purā viprāḥ tapasvī śaṃsita vrataḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ iti khyātaḥ pūjayāmāsa śaṃkaram jajāpa rudram aniśam praṇavam brahma rūpiṇam puṣpa dhūpa ādibhiḥ stotraiḥ namaskāraiḥ pradakṣiṇaiḥ uvāsa tatra yoga ātmā kṛtvā dīkṣām tu naiṣṭhikām kadācid āgatam pretam paśyati sma kṣudhā anvitam asthi carma pinaddha aṅgam niḥ śvasantam muhur muhur tam dṛṣṭvā sa muni śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpayā parayā yutaḥ provāca kaḥ bhavān kasmāt deśāt deśam imam śritaḥ tasmai piśācaḥ kṣudhayā pīḍyamānaḥ abravīt vacaḥ na pūjitāḥ mayā devāḥ gāvaḥ api atithayaḥ tathā na kadācid kṛtam puṇyam alpam vā su alpam eva vā ekadā bhagavān devaḥ govṛṣa īśvara vāhanaḥ mad īśvaraḥ vārāṇasyām dṛṣṭaḥ spṛṣṭe namaskṛtaḥ tadā acireṇa kālena pañcatvam aham āgataḥ na dṛṣṭam na na mayā ghoram yamasya vadanam mune īdṛśīm yonim āpannaḥ paiśācīm kṣudhayā anvitaḥ pipāsayā adhunā ākrāntaḥ na jānāmi hita ahitam kuruṣva tam namaḥ tubhyam tvām aham śaraṇam gataḥ iti uktaḥ śaṅkukarṇaḥ atha piśācam idam abravīt tvādṛśaḥ na hi loke asmin vidyate puṇya kṛttamaḥ yat tvayā bhagavān pūrvam dṛṣṭaḥ viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ saṃspṛṣṭaḥ vanditaḥ bhūyas kaḥ anyaḥ tvad sadṛśaḥ bhuvi snānam kuruṣva śīghram tvam asmin kuṇḍe samāhitaḥ yena imām kutsitām yonim kṣipram eva prahāsyasi smṛtvā kapardeśvaram īśitāram tadā avagāḍhaḥ muni saṃnidhāne mamāra divya ābharaṇa upapannaḥ adṛśyata arka pratime vimāne śaśāṅka cihna aṅkita cāru mauliḥ yathā udaye bhānuḥ aśeṣa devaḥ nṛtyanti divya apsarasaḥ abhirāmāḥ muñcanti vṛṣṭim kusuma ambu miśrām gandharva vidyādhara kiṃnara ādyāḥ saṃstūyamānaḥ atha muni indra saṅghaiḥ bodham bhagavant prasādāt samāviśat maṇḍalam etat agryam dṛṣṭvā vimuktam sa piśāca bhūtam muniḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ manasā maheśam praṇamya tuṣṭāva kapardinam tam uvāca kapardinam tvām paratas parastāt goptāram ekam puruṣam purāṇam vrajāmi yogeśvaram īśitāra mā ādityam agnim kapilā adhirūḍham tvām brahmapāram hṛdi sanniviṣṭam vrajāmi rudram śaraṇam diva stham sahastra pāda akṣi śiraḥ abhiyuktam tvām brahām apāram praṇamāmi śambhum yatas prasūtiḥ jagantaḥ yena āvṛtam sarvam idam śivena tam brahmapāram bhagavantam īśam praṇamya nityam śaraṇam prapadye aliṅgam āloka vihīna rūpam tam brahmapāram parameśvaram tvā labdhvā samādhim parama artha bhūtāḥ tam brahmapāram bhavataḥ sva rūpam na yatra nāma ādi viśeṣa kḷpti na saṃdṛśe tiṣṭhati yat sva rūpam tam brahmapāram praṇataḥ asmi nityam svayaṃbhuvam tvām śaraṇam prapadye yat veda vāda abhiratāḥ videham paśyanti anekam bhavataḥ sva rūpam yatas pradhānam puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ namāmi tam jyotiṣi saṃniviṣṭam bṛhantam bhavataḥ sva rūpam vrajāmi nityam śaraṇam guheśam sthāṇum prapadye giriśam purārim pinākinam tvām śaraṇam vrajāmi tad kṣaṇāt paramam liṅgam prādurbhūtam śiva ātmakam jñānam ānandam advaitam koṭi kālāgni sannibham śaṅkukarṇaḥ atha mukta ātmā tad ātmā sarvagaḥ amalaḥ etat rahasyam ākhyātam māhātmyam vaḥ kapardinaḥ yaḥ imām śṛṇuyāt nityam kathām pāpa praṇāśinīm bhaktaḥ pāpa viśuddha ātmā rudra sāmīpyam āpnuyāt drakṣyāmaḥ satatam devam pūjayāmaḥ atha śūlinam iti uktvā bhagavān vyāsaḥ śiṣyaiḥ saha mahā muniḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekatriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca uṣitvā tatra bhagavān kapardeśa antike punar draṣṭum yayau madhyameśam bahu varṣa gaṇān prabhuḥ tatra mandākinīm puṇyām ṛṣi saṅga niṣevitām nadīm vimala pānīyām dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭaḥ abhavat muniḥ sa tām anvīkṣya munibhiḥ saha dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ cakāra bhāva pūta ātmā snānam snāna vidhāna vid saṃtarpya vidhivat devān ṛṣīn pitṛ gaṇān tathā pūjayāmāsa lokādim puṣpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ bhavam praviśya śiṣya pravaraiḥ sārdham satyavatī sutaḥ madhyameśvaram īśānam arcayāmāsa śūlinam tatas pāśupatāḥ śāntāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ draṣṭum samāgatāḥ rudram madhyameśvaram īśvaram oṃkāra āsakta manasaḥ veda adhyayana tatparāḥ jaṭilāḥ muṇḍitāḥ ca api śukla yajña upavītinaḥ kaupīna vasanāḥ kecid apare ca api avāsasaḥ brahmacarya ratāḥ śāntāḥ vedānta jñāna tatparāḥ dṛṣṭvā dvaipāyanam viprāḥ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtam munim kaḥ bhavān kutas āyātaḥ saha śiṣyaiḥ mahā mune procuḥ paila ādayaḥ śiṣyāḥ tān ṛṣīn brahma bhāvitān ayam satyavatī sūnuḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ svayam yasya devaḥ mahādevaḥ sākṣāt eva pinākadhṛk aṃśāṃśena abhavat putraḥ nāmnā śukaḥ iti prabhuḥ yaḥ sa sākṣāt mahādevam sarva bhāvena śaṅkaram tatas pāśupatāḥ sarve hṛṣṭa sarva tanūruhāḥ bhagavan bhavatā jñātam vijñānam parameṣṭhinaḥ kṣipram paśyema tam devam śrutvā bhagavataḥ mukhāt visarjayitvā tān śiṣyān sumantu pramukhān tatas tad kṣaṇāt eva vimalam saṃbhūtam jyotiḥ uttamam līnāḥ tatra eva te viprāḥ kṣaṇāt antaradhīyata tatas śiṣyān samāhūya bhagavān brahma vittamaḥ provāca madhyameśasya māhātmyam paila pūrvakān atra pūrvam hṛṣīkeśaḥ viśvātmā devakī sutaḥ uvāsa vatsaram kṛṣṇaḥ sadā pāśupataiḥ vṛtaḥ ārādhayan hariḥ śaṃbhum kṛtvā pāśupatam vratam tasya te bahavaḥ śiṣyāḥ brahmacarya parāyaṇāḥ labdhvā tad vacanāt jñānam dṛṣṭavantaḥ maheśvaram tasya devaḥ mahādevaḥ pratyakṣam nīlalohitaḥ teṣām tat aiśvaram jñānam utpatsyati jagat maya ye atra drakṣyanti deveśam snātvā rudram pinākinam brahmahatyā ādikam pāpam teṣām āśu vinaśyati prāṇān tyajanti ye martyāḥ pāpa karma ratāḥ api te yānti tat param sthānam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā dhanyāḥ tu khalu te viprāḥ mandākinyām kṛta udakāḥ snānam dānam tapaḥ śrāddham piṇḍa nirvapaṇam tu iha ekaikaśas kṛtam viprāḥ punāti āsaptamam kulam saṃnihatyām upaspṛśya rāhu graste divākare evam uktvā mahā yogī madhyameśa anti ke prabhuḥ uvāsa su ciram kālam pūjayan vai maheśvaram iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge dvātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tatas sarvāṇi guhyāni tīrthāni āyatanāni ca prayāgam paramam tīrtham prayāgāt adhikam śubham hi viśvarūpam tathā tīrtham tālatīrtham anuttamam mahā ākhyam mahā tīrtham tīrtham ca eva ārṣabham param prājāpatyam tathā tīrtham svargadvāram tathā eva ca gayā tīrtham mahā tīrtham tīrtham ca eva mahānadī nārāyaṇam param tīrtham vāyutīrtham anuttamam jñānatīrtham param guhyam vārāham tīrtham uttamam yamatīrtham mahā puṇyam tīrtham saṃvartakam śubham agnitīrtham dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ kalaśeśvaram uttamam nāgatīrtham somatīrtham sūryatīrtham tathā eva ca ghaṭotkacam tīrtha varam śrītīrtham ca pitāmaham gaṅgātīrtham tu deveśam yayāteḥ tīrtham uttamam atra liṅgam purā ānīya brahmā snātum yadā gataḥ tadānīm sthāpayāmāsa viṣṇuḥ tat liṅgam aiśvaram tatas snātvā samāgatya brahmā provāca tam harim mayā ānītam idam liṅgam kasmāt sthāpitavan asi tasmāt pratiṣṭhitam liṅgam nāmnā tava bhaviṣyati bhūteśvaram tathā tīrtham tīrtham dharma samudbhavam daurvāsikam vyomatīrtham candratīrtham dvijottamāḥ citrāṅgadeśvaram puṇyam puṇyam vidyādhareśvaram sārasvatam prabhāsam ca bhadrakarṇam hradam śubham laukika ākhyam mahā tīrtham tīrtham ca eva vṛṣadhvajam hiraṇyagarbham goprekṣyam tīrtham ca eva vṛṣadhvajam upaśāntam śivam ca eva vyāghreśvaram anuttamam trilocanam mahā tīrtham lolārkam ca uttara āhvayam kapālamocanam tīrtham brahmahatyā vināśanam śukreśvaram mahā puṇyam ānandapuram uttamam evamādīni tīrthāni prādhānyāt kathitāni tu na śakyam vistarāt vaktum tīrtha saṃkhyāḥ dvijāttamāḥ teṣu sarveṣu tīrtheṣu snātvā abhyarcya pinākinam upoṣya tatra tatra asau pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ tarpayitvā pitṝn devān kṛtvā punar eva api yatra viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ snātvā abhyarcya param liṅgam śiṣyaiḥ saha mahā muniḥ uvāca śiṣyān dharma ātmā svān deśān gantum arhathā te praṇamya mahātmānam jagmuḥ paila ādayaḥ dvijāḥ vāsam ca tatra niyataḥ vārāṇasyām cakāra saḥ śāntaḥ dāntaḥ triṣavaṇam snātvā abhyarcya pinākinam bhaikṣa āhāraḥ viśuddha ātmā brahmacarya parāyaṇaḥ bhramamāṇena bhikṣā tu na eva labdhā dvijottamāḥ tatas krodha āvṛta tanuḥ narāṇām iha vāsinām vighnam sṛjāmi sarveṣām yena siddhiḥ vihīyate tad kṣaṇe sā mahādevī śaṃkara ardha śarīriṇī prādurāsīt svayam prītyā veṣam kṛtvā tu mānuṣam gṛhāṇa bhikṣām mattaḥ tvam uktvā evam pradadau śivā uvāca ca mahādevī krodhanaḥ tvam bhavān yatas evam uktaḥ sa bhagavān dhyānāt jñātvā parām śivām uvāca praṇataḥ bhūtvā stutvā ca pravaraiḥ stavaiḥ caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām praveśam dehi śāṅkari evam sa bhagavān vyāsaḥ mahā yogī purātanaḥ jñātvā kṣetra guṇān sarvān sthitaḥ tasya atha pārśvatas evam vyāsam sthitam jñātvā kṣetram sevanti paṇḍitāḥ tasmāt sarva prayatnena vārāṇasyām vaset naraḥ uvāca yaḥ paṭhet avimuktasya māhātmyam śṛṇuyāt api śrāvayet vā dvijān śāntān saḥ apiyāti parām gatim śrāddhe vā daivike kārye rātrau ahani vā dvijāḥ nadīnām ca eva tīreṣu devatāyataneṣu ca snātvā samāhita manāḥ dambha mātsarya varjitaḥ japet īśam namaskṛtya saḥ yāti paramām gatim iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge trayastriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ idānīm tu prayāgasya māhātmyam brūhi suvrata yāni tīrthāni tatra eva viśrutāni mahānti vai idānīm kathaya naḥ sūta sarva artha vid bhavān uvāca śṛṇudhvam ṛṣayaḥ sarve vistareṇa bravīmi vaḥ prayāgasya ca māhātmyam yatra devaḥ pitāmahaḥ mārkaṇḍeyena kathitam kaunteyāya mahātmane nihatya kauravāna sarvān bhrātṛbhiḥ saha pārthivaḥ śokena mahā tā āviṣṭā mumoha sa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ acireṇa atha kālena mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahā tapāḥ saṃprāptaḥ hāstinapuram rājadvāre sa tiṣṭhati dvārapālaḥ api tam dṛṣṭvā rājñaḥ kathitavān drutam mārkaṇḍeyaḥ draṣṭum icchan tvām āste dvāri asau muniḥ svāgatam te mahā prājña svāgatam te mahā mune adya mama pitaraḥ tuṣṭāḥ tvayi tuṣṭe mahā mune siṃhāsanam upasthāpya pāda śauca arcana ādibhiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahātmā iti pūjayāmāsa tam munim mārkaṇḍeyaḥ tatas tuṣṭaḥ provāca sa yudhiṣṭhiram kimartham muhyase vidvas sarvam jñātvā aham āgataḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā praṇamya āha mahā munim asmābhiḥ kauravaiḥ sārdham prasaṅgāt muni puṃgava yena hiṃsā samudbhūtāt janma antara kṛtāt api uvāca śṛṇu rājan mahābhāga yat mām pṛcchasi bhārat prayāga gamanam śreṣṭham narāṇām pāpa nāśanam uvāca mṛtānām kā gatiḥ tatra snātānām api kim phalam ye vasanti prayāge tu brūhi teṣām tu kim phalam uvāca kathayiṣyāmi te vatsa yā ceṣṭā yat ca tad phalam purā mahā ṛṣibhiḥ samyak kathyamānam mayā śrutam etat prajāpati kṣetram triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam atra snātvā divam yānti ye mṛtāḥ te apunarbhavāḥ tatra brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ rakṣām kurvanti saṃgatāḥ bahūni anyāni tīrthāni sarva pāpa apahāni tu saṃkṣepeṇa pravakṣyāmi prayāgasya iha kīrtanam ṣaṣṭiḥ dhanuḥ sahastrāṇi yāni rakṣanti jāhnavīm yamunām rakṣati sadā savitā sapta vāhanaḥ prayāge tu viśeṣeṇa svayam vasati vāsavaḥ nyagrodham rakṣate nityam śūlapāṇiḥ maheśvaraḥ sthānam rakṣanti vai devāḥ sarva pāpa haram śubham prayāgam smaramāṇasya sarvam āyāti saṃkṣayam darśanāt tasya tīrthasya nāma saṃkīrtanāt api muttikā ālambhanāt vā api naraḥ pāpāt pramucyate pañca kuṇḍāni rāja indra yeṣām madhye tu jāhnavī prayāgam viśataḥ puṃsaḥ pāpam naśyati tad kṣaṇāt yojanānām sahastreṣu gaṅgām yaḥ smarate naraḥ kīrtanāt mucyate pāpāt dṛṣṭvā bhadrāṇi paśyati vyādhitaḥ yadi vā dīnaḥ krūddhaḥ vā api bhavet naraḥ tyajet dīpta kāñcana varṇa ābhaiḥ vimānaiḥ bhānu varṇibhiḥ īpsitān labhate kāmān vadanti muni puṃgavāḥ vara aṅganā samākīrṇaiḥ modate śubha lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt svargāt paribhraṣṭaḥ kṣīṇa karmā narottama hiraṇya ratna saṃpūrṇe samṛddhe jāyate kule deśa sthaḥ yadi vā araṇye videśe yadi vā gṛhe prayāgam smaramāṇaḥ tu yaḥ tu prāṇān parityajet sarva kāma phalāḥ vṛkṣāḥ mahī yatra hiraṇmayī modate munibhiḥ sārdham sva kṛtena iha karmaṇā tatas śubhāni karmāṇi cintayānaḥ punar punar guṇavān vitta saṃpannaḥ bhavati iha na saṃśayaḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā satya dharma pratiṣṭhitaḥ suvarṇam atha muktām vā tathā eva anyān pratigrahān sva kārye pitṛ kārye vā devatā abhyarcane api vā atas tīrthe na gṛhṇīyāt puṇyeṣu āyataneṣu ca kapilām pāṭalā varṇām yaḥ tu dhenum prayacchati svarṇa śṛṅgīm raupya khurām caila kaṇṭhām payasvinīm yāvat romāṇi tasyāḥ vai santi gātreṣu sattama iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge catustriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca bhārṣeṇa tu vidhānena yathā dṛṣṭam yathā śrutam prayāga tīrtha yātrā arthaḥ yaḥ prayāti naraḥ kvacid balīvardam samārūḍhaḥ śṛṇu tasya api yat phalam yaḥ tu putrān tathā bālān snāpayet pāyayet tathā yathā ātmanā tathā sarvān dānam vipreṣu dāpayet niṣphalam tasya tat tīrtham vivarjayet na sa paśyati tam ghoram narakam tena karmaṇā baṭa mūlam samāśritya yaḥ tu prāṇān parityajet tatra brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ diśaḥ ca sa digīśvarāḥ lokapālāḥ ca siddhāḥ ca pitaraḥ loka saṃmatāḥ nāgāḥ supārṇāḥ siddhāḥ ca tathā nityam samāsate hariḥ ca bhagavān āste prajāpati puraskṛtaḥ prayāgam rāja śārdūla triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam tatra abhiṣekam yaḥ kuryāt saṃgame saṃśita vrataḥ tulyam rājasūya aśvamedhayoḥ na mātṛ vacanāt tāta na loka vacanāt api matiḥ utkramaṇīyā te prayāga gāmanam prati daśa tīrtha sahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭi koṭayaḥ tathā apare teṣām sāṃnidhyam atra eva tīrthānām kuru nandana sā gatiḥ tyajataḥ prāṇān gaṅgā yamunā saṃgame ye prayāgam na saṃprāptāḥ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam evam dṛṣṭvā tu tat tīrtham prayāgam paramam padam mucyate sarva pāpebhyaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ iva rāhuṇā kambala aśvatarau nāgau yamunā dakṣiṇe taṭe tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca mucyate sarva pātakaiḥ tatra gatvā naraḥ sthānam mahādevasya dhīmataḥ ātmānam tārayet pūrvam daśa atītān daśa aparān kṛtvā abhiṣekam tu naraḥ saḥ aśvamedha phalam labhet pūrva pārśve tu gaṅgāyāḥ trailokya khyātimān nṛpa avacaḥ sarva sāmudraḥ pratiṣṭhānam ca viśrutam uttareṇa pratiṣṭhānam bhāgīrathyāḥ tu savyatas aśvamedha phalam tatra smṛta mātrāt tu jāyate urvaśī puline ramye vipule haṃsa pāṇḍure parityajati yaḥ prāṇān śṛṇu tasya api yat phalam ṣaṣṭi varṣa sahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭi varṣa śatāni ca bhāste sa pitṛbhiḥ sārdham svarga loke narādhipa saṃdhyāvaṭe ramye brahmacārī jita indriyaḥ naraḥ śuciḥ upāsīta brahma lokam avāpnuyāt koṭitīrtham samāśritya yaḥ tu prāṇān parityajet yatra gaṅgā mahābhāgā bahu tīrtha tapaḥ vanā siddha kṣetram hi tat jñeyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā tārayate martyān nāgān tārayate api adhas divi tārayate devān tena tripathagā smṛtā yāvat asthīni gaṅgāyām tiṣṭhanti puruṣasya tu tīrthānām paramam tīrtham nadīnām paramā nadī mokṣa dā sarva bhūtānām mahāpātakinām api sarvatra sulabhā gaṅgā triṣu sthāneṣu durlabhā gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca gaṅgāsāgara saṃgame sarveṣām ame bhūtānām pāpa upahata cetasām gatim anveṣamāṇānām na asti gaṅgā samā gatiḥ pavitrāṇām pavitram ca maṅgalānām ca maṅgalam māheśvarāt paribhraṣṭā sarva pāpa harā śubhā kṛte yuge tu tīrthāni tretāyām puṣkaram param dvāpare tu kurukṣetram kalau gaṅgām viśiṣyate gaṅgām eva niṣeveta prayāge tu viśeṣataḥ na anyat kali yuga udbhūtam malam hantum su duṣkṛtam akāmaḥ vā sa kāmaḥ vā gaṅgāyām yaḥ vipadyate iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge pañcatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ṣaṣṭiḥ tīrtha sahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭiḥ tīrtha śatāni ca māgha māse gamiṣyanti gaṅgā yamunā saṃgamam gaṅgā yamunayoḥ madhye kārṣa agnim yaḥ tu sādhayet ahīna aṅgaḥ api arogaḥ ca pañca indriya samanvitaḥ yāvanti romakūpāṇi tasya gātreṣu mānada sa bhuktvā vipulān bhogān tat tīrtham bhajate punar jala praveśam yaḥ kuryāt saṃgame loka viśrute ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahastrāṇi ṣaṣṭim varṣa śatāni ca adhas sirāḥ tu ayaḥ dhārām ūrdhva pādaḥ pibet naraḥ śatam varṣa sahastrāṇi svarga loke mahīyate bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogān tat tīrtham bhajate punar śatam varṣa sahastrāṇi soma loke mahīyate tatas tasmāt paribhraṣṭaḥ rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ guṇavān rūpa saṃpannaḥ vidvān su priya vākyavān bhuktvā tu vipulān bhogān tata tīrtham bhajate punar ṛṇapramocanam nāma tīrtham tu paramam smṛtam eka rātra uṣitaḥ snātvā ṛṇaiḥ tatra pramucyate sūrya lokam avāpnoti anṛṇaḥ ca sadā bhavet iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ṣaṭtriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca tapanasya sutā devī triṣu lokeṣu viśrutā samāgatā mahābhāgā yamunā yatra nimnagā yena eva niḥ sṛtā gaṅgā tena eva yamunā gatā yojanānām sahastreṣu kīrtanāt pāpa nāśanā tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca yamunāyām yudhiṣṭhira prāṇān tyajati yaḥ tatra sa yāti paramām gatim agnitīrtham iti khyātam yamunā dakṣiṇa taṭe tatra snātvā divam yānti ye mṛtāḥ te apunarbhavāḥ kṛṣṇa pakṣe caturdaśyām snātvā saṃtarpayet śuciḥ dharmarājam mahā pāpaiḥ mucyate na atra saṃśayaḥ daśa tīrtha sahastrāṇi triṃśat koṭayaḥ tathā aparāḥ prayāge saṃsthitāni syuḥ evam āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ tistraḥ koṭyoḥ ca tīrthānām vāyuḥ abravīt divi bhūmi antarikṣe ca tat sarvam jāhnavī smṛtā yatra gaṅgā mahābhāgā sa deśaḥ tat tapaḥ vanam siddhikṣetram tu tat jñeyam gaṅgā tīra samāśritam idam satyam dvijātīnām sādhūnām ātmajasya ca suhṛdām ca japet karṇe śiṣyasya anugatasya tu mahā ṛṣīṇām idam guhyam sarva pāpa pramocanam yaḥ ca idam śṛṇuyāt nityam tīrtham puṇyam sadā śuciḥ jātismari tvam labhate nāka pṛṣṭhe ca modate prāpyante tāni tīrthāni sadbhiḥ śiṣṭa anudarśibhiḥ evam uktvā sa bhagavān mārkaṇḍeyaḥ mahā muniḥ tīrtāni kathayāmāsa pṛthivyām yāni kānicid bhū samudra ādi saṃsthānam pramāṇam jyotiṣām sthitam pṛṣṭaḥ provāca sakalam uktvā atha prayayaḥ muniḥ yaḥ idam kalyam utthāya paṭhate atha śṛṇoti vā iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām purva vibhāge saptatriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ūcuḥ kathitaḥ bhavatā sūta sargaḥ svayambhuvaḥ śubhaḥ idānīm śrotum icchāmaḥ trilokasya asya maṇḍalam yāvantaḥ sāgarāḥ dvīpāḥ tathā varṣāṇi parvatāḥ vanāni saritaḥ sūrya grahānām sthitiḥ eva ca yad ādhāram idam kṛtsnam yeṣām pṛthvī purā tu iyam nṛpāṇām tat samāsena sūta vaktum iha arhasi uvāca vakṣye deva ādidevāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave namaskṛtvā aprameyāya yat uktam tena dhīmatā putraḥ tasya abhavan putrāḥ prajāpati samāḥ daśa agnīdhraḥ ca agnibāhuḥ ca vapuṣmant dyutimant tathā jyotiṣmant daśamaḥ teṣām mahā bala parākramaḥ dhārmikaḥ dāna nirataḥ sarva bhūta anukampakaḥ medha agnibāhu putrāḥ tu trayaḥ yoga parāyaṇāḥ jātismarāḥ mahābhāgāḥ na rājye dadhire matim plakṣdvīpa īśvaraḥ ca eva tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ śālmala īśam vapuṣmantam narendram abhiṣiktavan jyotiṣmantam kuśadvīpe rājānam kṛtavān prabhuḥ dyutimantam ca rājānam krauñcadvīpe samādiśat śākadvīpa īśvaram ca api havyam cakre priyavrataḥ puṣkara adhipatim cakre savanam ca prajāpatiḥ mahāvītam smṛtam varṣam tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ nāmnā tu dhātakeḥ ca api dhātakīkhaṇḍam ucyate śākadvīpa īśvarasya atha havyasya api abhavan sutāḥ jaladaḥ ca kumāraḥ ca sukumāraḥ maṇīcakaḥ kumārasya tu kaumāram tṛtīyam sukumārakam maṇīcakam caturtham tu pañcamam kusumottaram modākam ṣaṣṭham iti uktam saptamam tu mahādrumam kuśalaḥ prathamaḥ teṣām dvitīyaḥ tu manoharaḥ uṣṇaḥ tṛtīyaḥ saṃproktaḥ caturthaḥ pravaraḥ smṛtaḥ teṣām sva nāmabhiḥ deśāḥ krauñcadvīpa āśrayāḥ śubhāḥ udbhedaḥ veṇumant ca eva aśvarathaḥ lambanaḥ dhṛtiḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākāraḥ ca api saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ sva nāma cihnitān yatra tathā varṣāṇi suvratāḥ jñeyāni sapta tāni eṣu dvīpeṣu evam na yaḥ mataḥ śālmala dvīpa nāthasya sutāḥ ca āsan vapuṣmataḥ śvetaḥ ca haritaḥ ca eva jīmūtaḥ rohitaḥ tathā plakṣadvīpa īśvarasya api sapta medhātitheḥ sutāḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayaḥ teṣām śiśiraḥ ca sukhodayaḥ bhānandaḥ ca śivaḥ ca eva kṣemakaḥ ca dhruvaḥ tathā plakṣadvīpa ādiṣu jñeyaḥ śākadvīpa antikeṣu vai jambudvīpa īśvarasya api putrāḥ tu āsan mahā balāḥ agnīdhrasya dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ tad nāmāni nibodhata nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaḥ ca eva tathā hariḥ ilāvṛtaḥ ramyaḥ hiraṇvant ca kuruḥ bhadrāśvaḥ ketumāhalakaḥ jambudvīpa īśvaraḥ rājā sa ca agnīdhraḥ mahāmatiḥ nābheḥ tu dakṣiṇam varṣam himāhvam pradadau punar hemakūṭam tatas varṣam dadau kiṃpuruṣāya tu tṛtīyam naiṣadham varṣam haraye dattavān pitā nīla acala āśritam varṣam ramyāya pradadau pitā śvetam yat uttaram varṣam pitrā dattam hiraṇvate yat uttaram śṛṅgavataḥ varṣam tat kuruve dadau meroḥ pūrveṇa yat varṣam bhadrāśvāya nyavedayat gandhamādana varṣam tu ketumālāya dattavān varṣeṣu eteṣu tān putrān abhiṣicya narādhipaḥ saṃsāra kaṣṭa tām jñātvā tapaḥ tepe vanam gataḥ himāhvayam tu yasya etat nābheḥ āsīt mahātmanaḥ ṛṣabhāt bharataḥ jajñe vīraḥ putra śata agrajaḥ saḥ abhiṣicya ṛṣabhaḥ putram bharatam pṛthivīpatiḥ tapasā karṣitaḥ atyartham kṛśaḥ dhamani saṃtataḥ jñāna yoga rataḥ bhūtvā mahā pāśupataḥ abhavat parameṣṭhī sutaḥ tasmāt pratīhāraḥ tad anvayaḥ tasya putraḥ mahā vīryaḥ dhīmant tasmāt ajāyata tvaṣṭā tvaṣṭuḥ ca virajaḥ rajaḥ tasya api abhūt sutaḥ śatajit rajasaḥ tasya jajñe putra śatam dvijāḥ teṣām pradhānaḥ balavān viśvajyotīḥ iti smṛtaḥ ārādhya devam brahmāṇam kṣemakam nāma pārthivam asūta putram dharma jñam mahā bāhum ariṃdamam ete purastāt rājānaḥ mahāsattvāḥ mahā ojasaḥ eṣām vaṃśa prasūtaiḥ ca bhuktā iyam pṛthivī purā iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge aṣṭātriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca atas param pravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa dvijottamāḥ janaḥ tapaḥ ca satyam ca lokāḥ tu aṇḍa udbhavāḥ matāḥ tāvat bhūrlokaḥ ākhyātaḥ purāṇe dvija puṃgavāḥ yāvat pramāṇaḥ bhūrlokaḥ vistarāt parimaṇḍalāt bhuvarlokaḥ api tāvān syāt maṇḍalāt bhāskarasya tu ūrdhvam yat maṇḍalāt vyoma dhruvaḥ yāvat vyavasthitaḥ pravahaḥ ca eva tathā eva anuvahaḥ paraḥ saṃvahaḥ vivahaḥ ca atha tad ūrdhvam syāt parāvahaḥ lakṣe divākarasya api maṇḍalam śaśinaḥ smṛtam nakṣatra maṇḍalam kṛtsnam tad lakṣeṇa prakāśate tāvat pramāṇa bhāge tu budhasya api uśanāḥ sthitaḥ aṅgārakaḥ api śukrasya tad pramāṇaḥ vyavasthitaḥ sauriḥ dvi lakṣeṇa guroḥ grahānām atha maṇḍalam saptarṣi maṇḍalam tasmāt lakṣa mātre prikāśate ṛṣīṇām maṇḍalāt ūrdhvam lakṣa mātre sthitaḥ dhruvaḥ tatra dharmaḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ triguṇaḥ tasya vistāraḥ maṇḍalasya pramāṇāt dviguṇaḥ tasya vistārāt vistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ pṛthivī chāyām nirmitaḥ maṇḍala ākṛtiḥ svarbhānoḥ tu vṛhat sthānam tṛtīyam yat tamaḥ mayam candrasya ṣoḍaśaḥ bhāgaḥ bhārgavasya vidhīyate bhārgavāt pāda hīnaḥ tu vijñeyaḥ vai bṛhaspatiḥ vistārāt maṇḍalāt ca eva pāda hīnaḥ tayoḥ budhaḥ tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi vapuṣmanti iha yāni vai budhena tāni tulyāni vistārāt maṇḍalāt tathā tārā nakṣatra rūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparāt śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve ca eva yojane sarva avara nikṛṣṭāni tārakā maṇḍalāni tu upariṣṭāt trayaḥ teṣām grahāḥ ye dūra sarpiṇaḥ sauraḥ aṅgirāḥ ca vakraḥ ca jñeyāḥ manda vicāriṇaḥ sūryaḥ saumaḥ budhaḥ ca eva bhārgavaḥ ca eva śīghragāḥ dakṣiṇāyana mārga sthaḥ yadā carati raśmimān tadā sarva grahāṇām sa sūryaḥ adhastāt prasarpati vistīrṇam maṇḍalam kṛtvā tasya ūrdhvam carate śaśī nakṣatra maṇḍalam kṛtsnam somāt ūrdhvam prasarpati nakṣatrebhyaḥ budhaḥ ca ūrdhvam budhāt ūrdhvam tu bhārgavaḥ vakraḥ tu bhārgavāt ūrdhvam vakrāt ūrdhvam bṛhaspatiḥ tasmāt śanaiścaraḥ tasmāt saptarṣi maṇḍalam ṛṣīṇām ca eva vaḥ ca ūrdhvam vyavasthitaḥ yojanānām sahastrāṇi bhāskarasya rathaḥ nava īṣā daṇḍaḥ tathā eva syāt dviguṇaḥ dvijasattamāḥ yojanānām tu tasya akṣaḥ tatra cakram pratiṣṭhitam tri nābhimati pañca are kṛtsnam kālacakram pratiṣṭhitam catkāriṃśat sahastrāṇi dvitīyaḥ akṣaḥ vivasvataḥ pañca anyāni tu sa ardhāni syandanasya dvijottamāḥ akṣa pramāṇam ubhayoḥ pramāṇam tat yuga ardhayoḥ dvitīye akṣe tu tat cakram saṃsthitam mānasa acale hayāḥ ca sapta chandāṃsi tad nāmāni nibodhata gāyatrī ca bṛhatī uṣṇih jagatī paṅktiḥ eva ca anaṣṭubh triṣṭubh iti uktāḥ chandāṃsi harayaḥ hareḥ mānasa upari māhendrī prācyām diśi mahā purī amarāvatī saṃyamanī sukhā ca eva vibhā kramāt kāṣṭhām gataḥ dakṣiṇatas kṣipta iṣuḥ iva sarpati jyotiṣām cakram ādāya devadevaḥ prajāpatiḥ aśeṣāsu diśāsu eva tathā eva vidiśāsu ca karoti ahar tathā rātrim vimuñcan medinīm dvijāḥ trailokyam kathitam sadbhiḥ lokānām muni puṃgavāḥ āditya mūlam akhilam trilokam na atra saṃśayaḥ rudra indra upendra candrāṇām vipra indrāṇām divaukasām sarva ātmā sarva loka īśaḥ mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ dvādaśa anye tathā ādityāḥ devāḥ te ye adhikāriṇaḥ nirvahanti padam tasya tad aṃśāḥ viṣṇu mūrtayaḥ chandaḥ mayam brahma mayam purāṇam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitā āryā pūrva vibhāge ekonacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca gandharvaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca grāmaṇī sarpa rākṣasaiḥ mitraḥ ca varuṇaḥ śakraḥ eva ca vivasvān atha pūṣā ca parjanyaḥ ca aṃśuḥ eva ca bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā ca viṣṇuḥ ca dvādaśā ete divākarāḥ āpyāyanti vai bhānum vasanta ādiṣu vai kramāt pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ ca atriḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ bhṛguḥ rathasvanaḥ atha varuṇaḥ suṣeṇaḥ senajit tathā tārkṣyaḥ ca ariṣṭanemiḥ ca rathajit satyajit tathā rākṣasa pravarāḥ hi ete prayānti puratas kramāt vāsukiḥ kaṅkanīraḥ ca takṣakaḥ sarpa puṃgavaḥ elāpattraḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ tathā airāvata saṃjñitaḥ dhanañjayaḥ mahāpadmaḥ tathā karkoṭakaḥ dvijāḥ tumburuḥ nāradaḥ hāhā hūhūḥ viśvāvasuḥ tathā citrasenaḥ tathā ūrṇāyuḥ dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ dvijottamāḥ sūryavarcāḥ dvādaśā ete gandharvāḥ gāyatām varāḥ gāyanti vividhaiḥ gānaiḥ bhānum ṣaḍja ādibhiḥ kramāt anumlocā ghṛtīcī ca viśvācī ca urvaśī tathā anyā ca pūrvacittiḥ syāt anyā ca eva tilottamā tāṇḍavaiḥ vividhaiḥ enam vasanta ādiṣu vai kramāt toṣayanti mahādevam bhānum ātmānam avyayam sūryam āpyāyayanti ete tejasā tejasām nidhim kurvate abhīṣu saṃgraham sarpāḥ vahanti deveśam yātudhānāḥ prayānti ca bhūtānām aśubham karma vyapohanti iha kīrtitāḥ varṣantaḥ ca tapantaḥ ca hlādayantaḥ ca vai prajāḥ gopayanti iha bhūtāni sarvāṇi iha ayuga kṣayāt eteṣām eva devānām yathāvīryam yathā tapaḥ yathāyogam yathāsattvam saḥ eṣa tapati prabhuḥ ahar rātra vyavasthāna kāraṇam sa prajāpatiḥ pitṛ deva manuṣya ādīn sa sadā āpyāyet raviḥ tatra devaḥ mahādevaḥ bhāsvān sākṣāt maheśvaraḥ bhāsate veda viduṣām nīlagrīvaḥ sanātanaḥ saḥ eṣa devaḥ bhagavān parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge catvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca evam eṣa mahādevaḥ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ karoti niyatam kālam kāla ātmā hi aiśvarā tanuḥ tasya ye raśmayaḥ viprāḥ sarva loka pradīpakāḥ teṣām śreṣṭhāḥ punar sapta raśmayaḥ graha yonayaḥ viśvavyacāḥ punar ca anyaḥ saṃyadvasuḥ atas paraḥ arvāvasuḥ iti khyātaḥ svarāj anyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ supumnaḥ sūrya raśmiḥ tu puṣṇāti śiśiradyutim viśvakarmā tathā raśmiḥ budham puṣṇāti sarvadā viśvavyacāḥ tu yaḥ raśmiḥ śukram puṣṇāti nityadā saṃyadvasuḥ iti khyātaḥ sa puṣṇāti ca lohitam vṛhaspatim prapuṣṇāti raśmiḥ arvāvasuḥ prabhoḥ śanaiścaram prapuṣṇāti saptamaḥ tu surāj tathā evam sūrya prabhāvena sarvāḥ nakṣatra tārakāḥ divyānām pārthivānām ca naiśānām ca eva sarvaśas mādānāt nityam ādityaḥ tejasām tamasām prabhuḥ ādatte sa tu nāḍīnām sahastreṇa samantataḥ nādeyān ca eva sāmudrān kūpyān ca eva sahastradṛś sthāvarān jaṅgamān ca eva yat ca kulyā ādikam payaḥ tāsām catuḥ śatam nāḍyaḥ varṣante citra mūrtayaḥ vandanāḥ ca eva yājyāḥ ca ketanāḥ bhūtanāḥ tathā amṛtāḥ nāma tāḥ sarvāḥ raśmayaḥ vṛṣṭi sarjanāḥ hima udvāhāḥ ca tāḥ nāḍyaḥ raśmayaḥ tri śatam punar raśmyaḥ meṣyaḥ ca pauṣyaḥ ca hlādinyaḥ hima sarjanāḥ candrāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ pīta ābhāḥ syuḥ gabhastayaḥ śukrāḥ ca kakubhaḥ ca eva gāvaḥ viśva bhṛtaḥ tathā śukrāḥ tāḥ nāmataḥ sarvāḥ trividhāḥ gharma sarjanāḥ samam bibharti tābhiḥ sa manuṣya pitṛ devatāḥ varuṇaḥ māgha māse tu sūryaḥ pūṣā tu phalgune caitre māsi bhavet aṃśaḥ dhātā vaiśākha tāpanaḥ bhavet indraḥ āṣāḍhe savitā raviḥ vivasvān śrāvaṇe māsi prauṣṭhapadyām bhagaḥ smṛtaḥ parjanyaḥ aśvayuji tvaṣṭā kārttike māsi bhāskaraḥ mārgaśīrṣa bhavet mitraḥ pauṣe viṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ pañca raśmi sahastrāṇi varuṇasya arka karmaṇi ṣaḍbhiḥ sahastraiḥ pūṣā tu deva oṃśaḥ saptabhiḥ tathā dhātā aṣṭabhiḥ sahastraiḥ tu navabhiḥ tu śatakratuḥ vivasvān daśabhiḥ pāti pāti ekādaśabhiḥ bhagaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ raśmi sahastraiḥ tu viṣṇuḥ tapati viśvasṛj vasante kapilaḥ sūryaḥ grīṣme kāñcana saprabhaḥ śvetaḥ varṣāsu varṇena pāṇḍuraḥ śaradi prabhuḥ hemante tāmra varṇaḥ syāt śiśire lohitaḥ raviḥ oṣadhīṣu balam dhatte svadhām api pitṛṣu atha anye ca aṣṭau grahāḥ jñeyāḥ sūryeṇa adhiṣṭhitāḥ dvijāḥ candramāḥ soma putraḥ ca śukraḥ ca eva bṛhaspatiḥ bhaumaḥ mandaḥ tathā rāhuḥ ketumant api ca aṣṭamaḥ bhrāmyamāṇāḥ yathāyogam bhramanti anu divākaram alāta cakra vat yānti vāta cakra īritāḥ dvijāḥ yasmāt vahati tān vāyuḥ pravahaḥ tena saḥ smṛtaḥ vāma dakṣiṇāt yuktāḥ daśa tena niśākaraḥ vīthi āśrayāṇi carati nakṣatrāṇi raviḥ yathā hrāsa vṛddhī ca vipra indrāḥ dhruva ādhārāṇi sarvadā āpūryate parasya antar satatam divasa kramāt suraiḥ somam āpyāyati nityadā ekena raśminā viprāḥ suṣumna ākhyena bhāskaraḥ eṣā sūryasya vīryeṇa somasya āpyāyitā tanuḥ paurṇamāsyām sa dṛśyeta saṃpūrṇe divasa kramāt saṃpūrṇam ardha māsena tam somam amṛta ātmakam tatas pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcid śiṣṭe kalā ātmake aparāhṇe pitṛ gaṇāḥ jaghanyam paryupāsate pibanti dvi kalam kālam śiṣṭā tasya kalā sudhā amṛta mayīm puṇyām tām andoḥ amṛta ātmakām niḥ sṛtam tat amāvāsyām gabhastibhyaḥ svadhā amṛtam māsa tṛptim apa api agryām pitaraḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ na somasya vināśaḥ syāt sudhā devaiḥ tu pīyate evam sūrya nimittasya kṣayaḥ vṛddhiḥ ca sattamāḥ somaputrasya ca aṣṭabhiḥ vājibhiḥ vāyu vegibhiḥ śukrasya bhūmi jaiḥ aśvaiḥ syandanaḥ daśabhiḥ vṛtaḥ aṣṭabiḥ ca atha bhaumasya rathaḥ haimaḥ su śobhanaḥ bṛhaspateḥ atha aṣṭa aśvaḥ syandanaḥ hema nirmitaḥ rathaḥ tamaḥ mayaḥ aṣṭa aśvaḥ mandasya āyasa nirmitaḥ svarbhānoḥ bhāskara areḥ ca tathā ṣaḍbhiḥ hayaiḥ vṛtaḥ ete mahā grahāṇām vai samākhyātāḥ rathāḥ nava sarve dhruve mahābhāgāḥ nibaddhāḥ vāta raśmibhiḥ graha ṛkṣa tārā dhiṣṇyāni dhruve baddhāni eśeṣatas iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca dhruvāt ūrdhvam mahar lokaḥ koṭi yojana vistṛtaḥ kalpa adhikāriṇaḥ tatra saṃsthitāḥ dvija puṃgavāḥ sanandana ādayaḥ tatra saṃsthitāḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ vairājāḥ tatra vai devāḥ sthitāḥ dāha vivarjitāḥ prājāpatyāt satyalokaḥ koṭi ṣaṭkena saṃyutaḥ atra lokaguruḥ brahmā viśvātmā viśvatomukhaḥ bhāste saḥ yogibhiḥ nityam pītvā yoga amṛtam param viśanti yatayaḥ śāntāḥ naiṣṭhikāḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ yoginaḥ tāpasāḥ siddhāḥ jāpakāḥ parameṣṭhinam dvāram tat yoginām ekam gacchatām paramam padam tatra gatvā na śocanti sa viṣṇuḥ saḥ ca śaṃkaraḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśam puram tasya durāsadam na me varṇayitum śakyam jvālā mālā samākulam tatra nārāyaṇasya api bhavanam brahmaṇaḥ pure śete tatra hariḥ śrīmān māyī māyā mayaḥ paraḥ sa viṣṇu lokaḥ kathitaḥ punarāvṛtti varjitaḥ devyā saha mahādevaḥ cintyamānaḥ manīṣibhiḥ yogibhiḥ śata sāhastraiḥ bhūtaiḥ rudraiḥ ca saṃvṛtaḥ tatra te yānti niyatāḥ dvijāḥ vai brahmacāriṇaḥ madādeva parāḥ śāntāḥ tāpasāḥ brahma vādinaḥ nirmamāḥ nirahaṅkārāḥ kāma krodha vivarjitāḥ drakṣyanti brahmanā yuktāḥ rudra lokaḥ saḥ vai smṛtaḥ ete sapta mahā lokāḥ pṛthivyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ mahātala ādayaḥ ca adhas pātālāḥ santi vai dvijāḥ mahātalam ca pātālam sarva ratna upaśobhitam nṛpeṇa balinā ca eva pātāla svarga vāsinā śailam rasātalam viprāḥ śārkaram hi talātalam suparṇena muni śreṣṭhāḥ tathā vāsukinā śubham rasātalam iti khyātam tathā anyaiḥ ca niṣevitam virocana hiraṇyākṣa takṣaka ādyaiḥ ca sevitam pūrvadevaiḥ samākīrṇam sutalam ca tathā aparaiḥ mahāntaka ādyaiḥ nāgaiḥ ca prahmādena asureṇa ca mahājambhena vīreṇa hayagrīveṇa vai tathā śaṅkukarṇena saṃbhinnam tathā namuci pūrvakaiḥ teṣām adhastāt narakāḥ māyā ādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ pāpinaḥ teṣu pacyante na te varṇayitum kṣamāḥ pātālānām adhas ca āste śeṣa ākhyā vaiṣṇavī tanuḥ kālāgni rudraḥ yoga ātmā nārasiṃhaḥ api mādhavaḥ yaḥ anantaḥ paṭhyete devaḥ nāga rūpī janārdanaḥ tad ādhāram idam sarvam sa kālāgnim apāśritaḥ tam āviśya mahā yogī kālaḥ tad vadana utthitaḥ sahastra māyaḥ apratimaḥ saṃhartā śaṃkara udbhavaḥ tāmasī śāmbhavī mūrtiḥ kālaḥ loka prakālanaḥ śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge dvicatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca etat brahmāṇḍam ākhyātam caturdaśavidham mahat atas param pravakṣyāmi bhūrlokasya asya nirṇayam jambudvīpaḥ pradhānaḥ ayam plakṣaḥ śālmalaḥ eva ca kuśaḥ krauñcaḥ ca śākaḥ ca puṣkaraḥ ca eva saptamaḥ ete sapta mahā dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ sapta vṛtāḥ dvīpāt dvīpaḥ mahān uktaḥ sāgarāt api sāgaraḥ kṣāroda ikṣurasodaḥ ca surodaḥ ca ghṛta udakaḥ dadhyodaḥ kṣīrasalilaḥ svādūdaḥ ca iti sāgarāḥ pañcāśat koṭi vistīrṇā sa samudrā dharā smṛtā dvīpaiḥ ca sapta yuktāḥ yojanānām samāsatas jambūdvīpaḥ samastānām dvīpānām madhyatas śubhaḥ praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśa adhastāt dvātriṃśat mūrdhani vistṛtaḥ mūle ṣoḍaśa sāhastraḥ vistāraḥ tasya sarvatas bhū padma āsya asya śailaḥ asau karṇikā tvena saṃsthitaḥ himavān hemakūṭaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ ca asya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaḥ ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ lakṣa pramāṇau dvau madhye daśa hīnāḥ tathā pare bhāratam dakṣiṇam varṣam tatas kiṃpuruṣam smṛtam harivarṣam tathā eva anyat meroḥ dakṣiṇatas dvijāḥ nava sāhastram ekaikam eteṣām dvijasattamāḥ ilāvṛtam mahābhāgāḥ cātvāraḥ tatra parvatāḥ viṣkambhāḥ racitāḥ meroḥ yojana ayutam ucchritāḥ pūrveṇa mandaraḥ nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ vipulaḥ paścime pārśve supārśvaḥ ca uttare smṛtaḥ jambūdvīpasya sā jambūḥ nāma hetuḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ mahā gaja pramāṇāni jambvaḥ tasyāḥ phalāni ca patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvatas rasena tasyāḥ prakhyātā tatra jambūnadī iti vai tad pānāt sustha manasām narāṇām tatra jāyate tīra mṛd tatra saṃprāpya vāyunā su viśoṣitā bhavati suvarṇam siddha bhūṣaṇam bhadrāśvaḥ pūrvatas meroḥ ketumālaḥ ca paścime tu muni śreṣṭhāḥ tayoḥ madhye ilāvṛtam sarāṃsi etāni catvāri deva yogyāni sarvadā sitāntaḥ ca kumudvant ca kururī mālyavant tathā vaikaṅkaḥ maṇiśailaḥ ca ṛkṣavant ca acala uttamāḥ veṇumant ca eva meghaḥ ca niṣadhaḥ deva parvataḥ iti ete deva racitāḥ siddha āvāsāḥ prakīrtitāḥ aruṇodasya sarasaḥ pūrvatas kesara acalaḥ trikūṭa śikharaḥ ca eva pataṅgaḥ rucakaḥ tathā niṣadhaḥ vasudhāraḥ ca kaliṅgaḥ triśikhaḥ śubhaḥ samūlaḥ vasudhāraḥ ca kuravaḥ ca eva sānumant tāmrātaḥ ca viśālaḥ ca kumudaḥ veṇuḥ vataḥ ekaśṛṅgaḥ mahāśailaḥ gajaśailaḥ piśācakaḥ pañcaśailaḥ atha kailāsaḥ himavant ca acala uttamaḥ iti ete deva caritāḥ utkaṭāḥ parvata uttamāḥ śikhivāsaḥ ca vaiḍūryaḥ kapilaḥ gandhamādanaḥ mārudhiḥ ca sugandhiḥ ca śrīśṛṅgaḥ ca acala uttamaḥ supārśvaḥ ca supakṣaḥ ca kaṅkaḥ kapilaḥ eva ca piñjaraḥ bhadraśailaḥ ca surasaḥ ca mahā balaḥ sahastra śikharaḥ ca eva pāṇḍuraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca suṣeṇaḥ puṇḍarīkaḥ ca mahāmeghaḥ tathā eva ca śaṅkhakūṭaḥ atha vṛṣabhaḥ haṃsaḥ nāgaḥ tathā paraḥ ca puṣpakaḥ ca sumeghaḥ ca vārāhaḥ virajāḥ tathā eteṣām śaila mukhyānām antareṣu yathākramam santi ca eva antara droṇyaḥ sarāṃsi ca vanāni ca prasannāḥ śānta rajasaḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām sahitāyām pūrva vibhāge tricatvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca yojanānām mahā purī tatra āste bhagavān brahmā viśvātmā viśvabhāvanaḥ upāsyamānaḥ yogi indraiḥ muni indra upendra śaṃkaraiḥ tatra deveśvara īśānam viśvātmānam prajāpatim samāste yoga yukta tmā pītvā tat parama amṛtam dīptam āyatanam śubhram purastāt brahmaṇaḥ sthitam mahā ṛṣi gaṇa saṃkīrṇam brahma niṣevitam devyā saha mahādevaḥ śaśāṅka arka agni locanaḥ tatra veda vidaḥ śāntāḥ munayaḥ brahmacāriṇaḥ pūjayanti mahādevam tāpasāḥ satya vādinaḥ teṣām sākṣāt mahādevaḥ munīnām brahma vādinām gṛhṇāti pūjām śirasā pārvatyā parameśvaraḥ nāmnā amarāvatī pūrve sarva śobhā samanvitā tam indram apsaraḥ saṅghāḥ gandharvāḥ gīta tatparāḥ upāsate sahastrākṣam devāḥ tatra sahastraśas ye dhārmikāḥ veda vidaḥ yāga homa parāyaṇāḥ teṣām tat paramam sthānam devānām api durlabham tejovatī nāma purī divya āścarya samanvitā japinām hominām sthānam dānavānām durāsadam nāmnā saṃyamanī divyā siddha gandharva sevitā tatra vaivasvatam devam deva ādyāḥ paryupāsate sthānam tat satya saṃdhānām loke puṇya kṛtām nṛṇām tasyāḥ tu paścime bhāge nirṛteḥ tu mahātmanaḥ rakṣovatī nāma purī rākṣasaiḥ sarvatas vṛtā tatra tam nirṛtim devam rākṣasāḥ paryupāsate nāmnā suddhavatī puṇyā sarva kāma ṛdhi saṃyutā tatra apsaraḥ gaṇaiḥ siddhaiḥ sevyamānaḥ amara adhipaḥ bhavati sa varuṇaḥ rājā tatra gacchanti ye ambudāḥ tīrtha yātrā parī nityam ye ca loke adhamarṣiṇaḥ nāmnā gandhavatī puṇyā tatra āste asau prabhañjanaḥ prāṇāyāma para amartya āsthānam tat yānti śāśvatam tasyāḥ pūrveṇa digbhāge somasya paramā purī nāmnā kāntimatī śubhrā tatra somaḥ virājate teṣām tat racitam sthānam nānā bhoga samanvitam tasyāḥ ca pūrva digbhāge śaṅkarasya mahā purī nāmnā yaśovatī puṇyā sarveṣām su durāsadā tatra īśānasya bhavanam rudra viṣṇu tanoḥ śubham tatra bhoga abhilipsūnām bhaktānām parameṣṭhinaḥ nivāsaḥ kalpitaḥ pūrvam devadevena śūlinā viṣṇu pādāt viniṣkrāntā plāvayitvā indu maṇḍalam samantāt brahmaṇaḥ puryām gaṅgā patati vai divaḥ sītā ca alakanandā ca sucakṣuḥ bhadra nāmakā pūrveṇa sītā śailāt tu śailam yāti antarikṣataḥ tatas ca pūrva varṣeṇa bhadrāśveṇa eti ca arṇavam tathā eva alakanandā ca dakṣiṇāt etya bhāratam prayāti sāgaram bhittvā sapta bhedāḥ dvijottamāḥ sucakṣuḥ paścima girīn atītya sakalān tathā paścimam ketumāla ākhyam varṣam gatvā eti ca arṇavam bhadrā tathā uttara girīn uttarān ca tathā kurūn gandhamādanaḥ bhāratāḥ ketumālāḥ ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravaḥ tathā pattrāṇi loka padmasya maryādā śaila bāhyatas jaṭharaḥ devakūṭaḥ ca maryādāparvatau ubhau dakṣiṇa uttara māyā amau ā nīla niṣadha āyatau aśīti yojana āyāmau arṇava antar vyavasthitau niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraḥ ca maryādāparvatau imau maryādāparvatāḥ proktāḥ aṣṭa iha mayā dvijāḥ jaṭhara ādyāḥ sthitāḥ meroḥ catur dikṣu mahā ṛṣayaḥ śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge catuścatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca ketumāle narāḥ kālāḥ sarve panasa bhojanāḥ bhadrāśve puruṣāḥ śuklāḥ striyaḥ candra aṃśu sannibhāḥ daśa varṣa sahastrāṇi jīvante āmra bhojanāḥ daśa varṣa sahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca hiraṇmaye hiraṇya ābhāḥ sarve ca lakuca aśanāḥ ekādaśa sahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca trayodaśa sahastrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca jīvanti kuru varṣe tu śyāma aṅgāḥ kṣīra bhojanāḥ sarve mithuna jātāḥ ca nityam sukha niṣevinaḥ tathā kiṃpuruṣe viprāḥ mānavāḥ hema sannibhāḥ daśa varṣa hastrāṇi jīvanti plakṣa bhojanāḥ dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya sa ādaram bhakti saṃyutāḥ daśa varṣa sahastrāṇi jīvanti ikṣu rasa āśinaḥ tatra nārāyaṇam devam viśvayonim sanātanam upāsate sadā viṣṇum mānavāḥ viṣṇu bhāvitāḥ mānam vāsudevasya pārijāta vana āśritam prākāraiḥ daśabhiḥ yuktam durādharṣam su durgamam sphāṭikaiḥ maṇḍapaiḥ yuktam deva rāja gṛha upamam hema sopāna saṃyuktam nānā ratna upaśobhitam sarobhiḥ svādu pānīyaiḥ nadībhiḥ ca upaśobhitam nārāyaṇa paraiḥ śuddhaiḥ veda adhyayana tatparaiḥ yogibhiḥ ca samākīrṇam dhyāyadbhiḥ puruṣam harim rājānaḥ sarvakālam tu mahimānam prakurvate striyaḥ yauvana śālinyaḥ sadā maṇḍana tatparāḥ ilāvṛte padma varṇāḥ jambu phala rasa āśinaḥ trayodaśa sahastrāṇi varṣāṇām vai sthira āyuṣaḥ bhārate tu striyaḥ puṃsaḥ nānā varṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ nānā deva arcane yuktāḥ nānā karmāṇi kurvate parama āyuḥ smṛtam teṣām śatam varṣāṇi suvratāḥ na anāhārāḥ ca jīvanti puṇya pāpa nimittatas karma bhūmiḥ iyam viprāḥ narāṇām adhikāriṇām mahendraḥ malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimant ṛkṣa parvataḥ vindhyaḥ ca pāriyātraḥ ca sapta atra kulaparvatāḥ indradyumnaḥ kaśerumant tāmravarṇaḥ gabhastimant ayam tu navamaḥ teṣām dvīpaḥ sāgara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahastram tu dvīpaḥ ayam dakṣiṇa uttaraḥ pūrve kirātāḥ tasya ante paśicame yavanāḥ tathā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśya madhye śūdrāḥ tathā eva ca stravante pāvanāḥ nadyaḥ parvatebhyaḥ viniḥ sṛtāḥ irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā devikā kuhūḥ gomatī dhūtapāpā ca bāhudā ca dṛṣadvatī kauśikī lohitā ca eva himavatpādaniḥ sṛtāḥ parṇāśā vandanā ca eva sadānīrā manoramā carmaṇvatī tathā dūryā vidiśā vetravatī api śigruḥ svaśilpā api tathā pāriyātra āśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ narmadā surasā śoṇa daśārṇā ca mahā nadī mandākinī citrakūṭā tāmasī ca piśācikā citrotpalā vipāśā ca mañjulā vāluvāhinī ṛkṣa vat pāda jāḥ nadyaḥ sarva pāpa harāḥ nṛṇām tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā śīghrodā ca mahā nadī veṇyā vaitaraṇī ca eva balākā ca kumudvatī toyā ca eva mahāgairī durgā ca antar śilā tathā vindhya pāda prasūtāḥ tāḥ nadyaḥ puṇya jalāḥ śubhāḥ sodāvarī bhīmarathā kṛṣṇā varṇā ca matsarī tuṅgabhdrā suprayogā kāverī ca dvijottamāḥ dakṣiṇāpatha gāḥ nadyaḥ sahya pāda viniḥ sṛtāḥ ṛtumālā tāmraparṇī puṣpavatī utpalāvatī malayāt niḥ sṛtāḥ nadyaḥ sarvāḥ śīta jalāḥ smṛtāḥ mandagā manda gāminī pālāsinī ca eva ṛṣikā vaṃśakāriṇī śuktimat pāda saṃjātāḥ sarva pāpa harāḥ nṛṇām bhāsām nadī upanadyaḥ ca śataśas dvija puṃgavāḥ sarva pāpa harāḥ puṇyāḥ snāna dāna ādi karmasu tāsu ime kuru pāñcālāḥ madhyadeśa ādayaḥ janāḥ pūrva deśa ādikāḥ ca eva kāmarūpa nivāsinaḥ puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅga amagadhāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca kṛtsnaśas tathā aparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūdra ābhīrāḥ tathā ar'budāḥ mālakāḥ mālavāḥ ca eva pāriyātra nivāsinaḥ sauvīrāḥ saindhavāḥ hūṇā śālvāḥ kalpa nivāsinaḥ madrāḥ rāmāḥ tathā ambaṣṭhāḥ pārasīkāḥ tathā eva ca māsām pibanti salilam vasanti saritām sadā kṛtam tretā dvāparam ca kaliḥ ca anyatra na kvacid yāni kiṃpuruṣa ādyāni varṣāṇi aṣṭau mahā ṛṣayaḥ na teṣu śokaḥ na āyāsaḥ na udvegaḥ kṣudh bhayam na ca svasthāḥ prajāḥ nirātaṅkāḥ sarva duḥkha vivarjitāḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge pañcacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca hemakūṭa gireḥ śṛṅge mahā kūṭaiḥ su śobhanam sphāṭikam devadevasya vimānam parameṣṭhinaḥ atha deva ādidevasya bhūteśasya triśūliṇaḥ devāḥ siddha gaṇāḥ yakṣāḥ pūjām nityam prakurvate sa devaḥ giriśaḥ sārdham mahādevyā maheśvaraḥ bhūtaiḥ parivṛtaḥ nityam bhāti tatra pinākadhṛk nivāsaḥ koṭi yakṣāṇām kuberasya ca dhīmataḥ nadī nānāvidhaiḥ padmaiḥ anekaiḥ samalaṅkṛtā deva dānava gandharva yakṣa rākṣasa kiṃnaraiḥ upaspṛṣṭa jalā nityam su puṇyā su manoramā anyāḥ ca nadyaḥ śataśas svarṇa padmaiḥ alaṅkṛtāḥ tāsām kūleṣu devasya sthānāni parameṣṭhinaḥ deva ṛṣi gaṇa juṣṭāni tathā nārāyaṇasya ca sitānta śikhare ca api pārijāta vanam śubham tatra atha devadevasya viṣṇoḥ viśva amara īśituḥ tatra nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān lakṣmyā saha jagatpatiḥ mad āste sarva amara śreṣṭhaḥ pūjyamānaḥ sanātanaḥ tathā ca vasudhāre tu vasūnām ratna maṇḍitam sthānānām aṣṭakam puṇyam durādharṣam suradviṣām ratnadhāre giri vare saptarṣīṇām mahātmanām sapta āśramāṇi puṇyāni siddha āvāsa yutāni tu tatra haimam catur dvāram vajra nīla ādi maṇḍitam bhāste hitāya lokānām śāntānām paramā gatiḥ atha ekaśṛṅga śikhare mahā padmaiḥ alaṅkṛtam su accha amṛta jalam puṇyam su gandham su mahat saraḥ jaigīṣavya āśramam tatra yogi indraiḥ upaśobhitam tatra asau bhagavān nityam āste śiṣyaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ śaṅkhaḥ manoharaḥ ca eva kauśikaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva ca sumanāḥ vedanādaḥ ca śiṣyāḥ tasya pradhānatas sarve yoga ratāḥ śāntāḥ bhasma uddhūlita vigrahāḥ upāsate mahā vīryāḥ brahma vidyā parāyaṇāḥ teṣām anugrihā arthāya yatīnām śānta cetasām sāṃnidhyam kurute bhūyas devyā saha maheśvaraḥ munīnām yukta manasām sarāṃsi saritaḥ tathā teṣu yoga ratāḥ viprāḥ jāpakāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ brahmaṇi āsakta manasaḥ ramante jñāna tatparāḥ ātmani ātmānam ādhāya śikhā anta antaram āsthitam dhāyāyanti devam īśānam yena sarvam idam tatam tatra āste bhagavān indraḥ śacyā saha sureśvaraḥ gajaśaile tu durgāyāḥ bhavanam maṇi tāraṇam bhagavatī durgā tatra sākṣāt maheśvarī upāsyamānāḥ vividhaiḥ śakti bhedaiḥ itas tatas pītvā yoga amṛtam labdhvā sākṣāt ānandam aiśvaram sunīlasya gireḥ śṛṅge nānā dhātu samujjvale rākṣasāṇām purāṇi syuḥ sarāṃsi śataśas dvijāḥ tathā pura śatam viprāḥ śataśṛṅge mahā acale sphāṭika stambha saṃyuktam yakṣāṇām amita ojasām śvetodara gireḥ śṛṅge suparṇasya mahātmanaḥ prākāra gopura upetam maṇi toraṇa maṇḍitam sa tatra garuḍaḥ śrīmān sākṣāt viṣṇuḥ iva aparaḥ dhyātvā āste tat param jyotiḥ ātmānam viṣṇum avyayam anyat ca bhavanam puṇyam śrīśṛṅge muni puṃgavāḥ śrī devyāḥ sarva ratna āḍhyam haimam su maṇi toraṇam tatra sā paramā śaktiḥ viṣṇoḥ ati manoramā sarāṃsi tatra catvāri vicitra kamala āśrayā tathā sahastraśikhare vidyādhara pura aṣṭakam nadyaḥ vimala pānīyāḥ citra nīlotpala ākarāḥ karṇikāravanam tatra āste śaṃkara umayā pāriyātre mahā śaile mahā lakṣmyāḥ puram śubham ramya prāsāda saṃyuktam ghaṇṭā cāmara bhūṣitam mṛdaṅga muraja udghuṣṭam vīṇā veṇu nināditam gandharva kiṃnara ākīrṇam saṃvṛtam siddha puṃgavaiḥ bhāsvat bhitti samākīrṇam mahā prāsāda saṃkulam gaṇeśvara aṅganā juṣṭam dhārmikāṇām su darśanam tatra sā vasate devī nityam yoga parāyaṇā mahā lakṣmīḥ mahādevī triśūla vara dhāriṇī trinetrā sarva śa saktībhiḥ saṃvṛtā sat asat mayā sarāṃsi siddha juṣṭāni deva bhogyāni sattamāḥ pāṇḍurasya gireḥ śṛṅge vicitra druma saṃkule sandharvāṇām pura śatam divya strībhiḥ samāvṛtam krīḍanti muditāḥ nityam vilāsaiḥ bhoga tatparāḥ añjanasya gireḥ śṛṅge nārīṇām puram uttamam vasanti tatra apsarasaḥ rambhā ādyāḥ rati lālasāḥ sā purī sarva ratna āḍhyā na eka prastravaṇaiḥ yutā anekāni purāṇi syuḥ kaumude ca api suvratāḥ rudrāṇām śānta rajasām īśvara arpita cetasām teṣu rudrāḥ mahā yogāḥ maheśa antara cāriṇaḥ samāsate param jyotiḥ ārūḍhāḥ sthānam uttamam piñjarasya gireḥ śṛṅge gaṇeśānām pura trayam nandīśvarasya kapile tatra āste suyaśāḥ yatiḥ tathā ca śṛṅge devadevasya dhīmataḥ dīptam āyatanam puṇyam bhāskarasya amita ojasaḥ sahastra yojana āyāmam suvarṇa maṇi toraṇam tatra āste bhagavān brahmā siddha saṅghaiḥ abhiṣṭutaḥ sāvitryā saha viśvātmā vāsudeva ādibhiḥ yutaḥ pañcaśailasya śikhare dānavānām pura trayam na ati dūreṇa tasya atha dhīmataḥ kardamasya āśramam puṇyam tatra āste bhagavān ṛṣiḥ tasya eva pūrva digbhāge kiñcid vai dakṣiṇa āśrite sarveṣu eteṣu śaileṣu tata anyeṣu muni īśvarāḥ sarāṃsi vimalāḥ nadyaḥ devānām ālayāni ca siddha liṅgāni puṇyāni munibhiḥ sthāpitāni tu vanyāni āśrama varyāṇi saṃkhyātum na eva śaknuyām eṣa saṃkṣepataḥ proktaḥ jambūdvīpasya vistaraḥ na śakyam vistarāt vaktum mayā varṣa śataiḥ api iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ṣaṭcatvāriśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca jambūdvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena samantataḥ saṃveṣṭayitvā kṣārodam plakṣadvīpaḥ vyavasthitaḥ plakṣadvīpe ca vipra indrāḥ sapta āsan kulaparvatāḥ bhṛju āyatāḥ su parvāṇaḥ siddha saṅgha niṣevitāḥ dundubhiḥ ca eva somaḥ ca ṛṣabhaḥ tathā upāsyate sa viśvātmā sākṣī sarvasya viśvasṛj teṣu puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ na ādhayaḥ vyādhayaḥ na ca na tatra pāpa kartāraḥ puruṣāḥ vā kathaṃcana teṣām nadyaḥ ca sapta eva varṣāṇām tu samudra gāḥ anutaptā śikhī ca eva vipāpā tridivā kṛtā amṛtā sukṛtā ca eva nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ kṣudra nadyaḥ tu asaṃkhyātāḥ sarāṃsi su bahūni api na ca eteṣu yuga avasthā puruṣāḥ vai cira āyuṣaḥ āryakāḥ kuravāḥ ca eva vidaśāḥ bhāvinaḥ tathā brahma kṣatriya viś śūdrāḥ tasmin dvīpe prakīrtitāḥ teṣām ca soma sāyujyam sārūpyam muni puṃgavāḥ sarve dharma pare nityam nityam mudita mānasāḥ pañca varṣa sahastrāṇi jīvanti ca nirāmayāḥ plakṣadvīpa pramāṇam tu dviguṇena samantataḥ saṃveṣṭya ikṣu rasa ambhodhim śālmaliḥ saṃvyavasthitaḥ sapta varṣāṇi tatra api sapta eva kulaparvatāḥ bṛju āyatāḥ su parvāṇaḥ sapta nadyaḥ ca suvratāḥ kumudaḥ ca unnataḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca balāhakaḥ droṇaḥ kaṅkaḥ tu mahiṣaḥ kakudvant sapta parvatāḥ yonī toyā vitṛṣṇā ca candrā śuklā vimocanī nivṛttiḥ ca eti tāḥ nadyaḥ smṛtāḥ pāpa harāḥ nṛṇām na ca eva asti yuga avasthā janāḥ jīvanti anāmayāḥ yajanti satatam tatra varṇāḥ vāyum sanātanam teṣām tasya atha sāyujyam sārūpyam ca salokatā kapilāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ proktāḥ rājānaḥ ca aruṇāḥ tathā pītāḥ vaiśyāḥ smṛtāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ dvīpe asmin vṛṣalāḥ dvijāḥ śālmalasya tu vistārāt dviguṇena samantataḥ saṃveṣṭya tu sura uda abdhim kuśadvīpaḥ vyavasthitaḥ vidrumaḥ ca eva hemaḥ ca dyutimant puṣpavant tathā kuśeśayaḥ hariḥ ca atha mandaraḥ sapta parvatāḥ dhutapāpā śivā ca eva pavitrā saṃmatā tathā anyāḥ ca śataśas viprāḥ nadyaḥ maṇi jalāḥ śubhāḥ tāsu brahmāṇam īśānam deva ādyāḥ paryupāsate brāhmaṇāḥ viprāḥ kṣatriyāḥ śuṣmiṇaḥ tathā vaiśyāḥ snehāḥ tu mandehāḥ śūdrāḥ tatra prakīrtitāḥ sarve vijñāna saṃpannāḥ maitra ādi guṇa saṃyutāḥ yathā ukta kāriṇaḥ sarve sarve bhūta hite ratāḥ teṣām ca brahma sāyujyam sārūpyam ca salokatā kuśadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena samantataḥ krauñcadvīpaḥ tatas viprāḥ veṣṭayitvā ghṛta udadhim krauñcaḥ vāmanakaḥ ca eva tṛtīyaḥ ca andhakārakaḥ devāvṛt ca vivindaḥ ca puṇḍarīkaḥ tathā eva ca ca eva saṃdhyā rātriḥ manojavā khyātiḥ ca puṇḍarīkā ca nadyaḥ prādhānyāt smṛtāḥ puṣkarāḥ puṣkalāḥ dhanyāḥ tiṣyāḥ tasya krameṇa vai brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca eva dvijottamāḥ arcayanti mahādevam yajña dāna samādhibhiḥ teṣām vai rudra sāyujyam sārūpyam ca ati durlabham salokatā ca sāmīpyam jāyate tad prasādataḥ śākadvīpaḥ sthitaḥ viprāḥ āveṣṭya dadhi sāgaram āmbikeyaḥ tathā ramyaḥ kesarī ca iti parvatāḥ sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī reṇukā tathā ikṣukā dhenukā ca eva gabhastiḥ ca iti nimnagāḥ mānavāḥ anāmayāḥ hi aśokāḥ ca rāga dveṣa vivarjitāḥ magāḥ ca magadhāḥ ca eva mānavāḥ mandagāḥ tathā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca atra krameṇa tu teṣām sūryeṇa sāyujyam sāmīpyam ca sarūpa tā śākadvīpam samāvṛtya kṣīrodaḥ sāgaraḥ sthitaḥ śvetadvīpaḥ ca tad madhye nārāyaṇa parāyaṇāḥ tatra puṇyāḥ janapadāḥ nānā āścarya samanvitāḥ śvetāḥ tatra narāḥ nityam jāyante viṣṇu tatparāḥ nitya puṣṭāḥ nirātaṅkāḥ nitya ānandāḥ ca bhoginaḥ nārāyaṇa pare sarve nārāyaṇa parāyaṇāḥ kecid dhyāna pare nityam yoginaḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ ekāntinaḥ nirālambāḥ mahā bhāgavatāḥ pare paśyanti paramam brahma viṣṇava ākhyam tamasaḥ param sarve caturbhuja ākārāḥ śaṅkha cakra gadā dharāḥ su pīta vāsasaḥ sarve śrīvatsa aṅkita vakṣasaḥ anye maheśvara pare tripuṇḍra aṅkita mastakāḥ sva yoga udbhūta kiraṇāḥ mahā garuḍa vāhanāḥ sarva śakti samāyuktāḥ nitya ānandāḥ ca nirmalāḥ vasanti tatra puruṣāḥ viṣṇoḥ antara cāriṇaḥ nārāyaṇam nāma puram vyāsa ādyaiḥ upaśobhitam hema prākāra saṃsuktam sphāṭikaiḥ maṇḍapaiḥ yutam harmya prākāra saṃyuktam aṭṭālaka samākulam śubhra āstaraṇa saṃyuktam vicitraiḥ samalaṅkṛtam nandanaiḥ vividha ākāraiḥ śobhitam sarobhiḥ sarvatas yuktam vīṇā veṇu nināditam patākābhiḥ vicitrābhiḥ anekābhiḥ ca śobhitam vīthibhiḥ sarvatas yuktam sopānaiḥ ratna bhūṣitaiḥ nārī śata sahastra āḍhyam haṃsa kāraṇḍava ākīrṇam cakravāka upaśobhitam nānā gīta vidhāna jñaiḥ devānām api durlabhaiḥ nānā vilāsa saṃpannaiḥ kāmukaiḥ ati komalaiḥ īṣat smitaiḥ su bimba uṣṭhaiḥ bāla mugdha mṛga īkṣaṇaiḥ saṃlāpa ālāpa kuśalaiḥ divya ābharaṇa bhūṣā etaiḥ nānā varṇa vicitra aṅgaiḥ nānā bhoga rati priyaiḥ asaṃkhyeya guṇam śuddham āgamyam tridaśaiḥ api śrīmat pavitram devasya śrīpateḥ amita ojasaḥ sthānam vaiṣṇavam divyam yoginām api durlabham tad madhye bhagavān ekaḥ puṇḍarīka dala dyutiḥ śete aśeṣa jagat sūtiḥ śeṣa ahi śayane hariḥ sva ātma ānanda amṛtam pītvā param tat tamasaḥ param kṣīroda kanyayā nityam gṛhīta caraṇa dvayaḥ sā ca devī jagat vandyā pāda mūle haripriyā samāste tad manāḥ nityam pītvā nārāyaṇa amṛtam na tatra adhārmikāḥ yānti na ca deva antara āśrayāḥ vaikuṇṭham nāma tat sthānam tridaśaiḥ api vanditam na me atra bhavati prajñā kṛtsnaśas tad nirūpaṇe etāvat śakyate vaktum nārāyaṇa puram hi tat śete nārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān māyayā mohayan jagant nārāyaṇāt idam jātam tasmin eva vyavasthitam iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhstryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge saptacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca śākadvīpasya vistārāt dviguṇena vyavasthitaḥ kṣīrārṇavam samāśritya dvīpaḥ puṣkara saṃvṛtaḥ yojanānām sahastrāṇi sārdham pañcāśat ucchritaḥ tāvat eva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvatas parimaṇḍalaḥ saḥ eva dvīpaḥ paśca ardhe mānasottara saṃjñitaḥ ekaḥ eva mahā sānuḥ saṃniveśāt dvidhā kṛtaḥ mahāvītam smṛtam varṣam dhātakīkhaṇḍam eva ca svādu udakena udadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ tasmin dvīpe mahā vṛkṣaḥ nyagrodhaḥ amara pūjitaḥ tasmin nivasati brahmā viśvātmā viśvabhāvanaḥ tatra eva muni śārdūlāḥ śiva nārāyaṇa ālayaḥ saṃpūjyamānaḥ brahma ādyaiḥ kumāra ādyaiḥ ca yogibhiḥ gandharvaiḥ kinnaraiḥ yakṣaiḥ īśvaraḥ kṛṣṇa piṅgalaḥ svasthāḥ tatra prajāḥ sarvāḥ brahmaṇā sadṛśa tviṣaḥ nirāmayāḥ viśokāḥ ca rāga dveṣa vivarjitāḥ satya anṛte na tatra āstām na uttama adhama madhyamāḥ na varṇa āśrama dharmāḥ ca na nadyaḥ na ca parvatāḥ pareṇa tasya mahatī dṛśyate loka saṃsthitiḥ kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvā ca eva śilā upamā tasyāḥ pareṇa śailaḥ tu maryādā ātmā ātma maṇḍalaḥ prakāśaḥ ca aprakāśaḥ ca lokālokaḥ saḥ ucyate yojanānām sahastrāṇi daśa tasya ucchrayaḥ smṛtaḥ tāvān eva ca vistāraḥ lokālokaḥ mahā giriḥ tamaḥ ca aṇḍa kaṭāhena samantāt pariveṣṭitam etaiḥ sapta mahā lokāḥ pātālāḥ sapta kīrtitāḥ brahmāṇḍasya eṣa vistāraḥ saṃkṣepeṇa mayā uditaḥ aṇḍānām īdṛśāṇām tu koṭayaḥ jñeyāḥ sahastraśas sarvaga tvāt pradhānasya kāraṇasya avyaya ātmanaḥ aṇḍeṣu eteṣu sarveṣu bhuvanāni caturdaśa tatra tatra catur vaktrāḥ rudrāḥ nārāyaṇa ādayaḥ samantāt saṃsthitam viprāḥ yatra yānti manīṣiṇaḥ anekadhā vibhakta aṅgaḥ krīḍate puruṣottamaḥ aṇḍāt brahmā samutpannaḥ tena sṛṣṭam idam jagat iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge aṣṭacatvāriṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ atīta anāgatāni iha yāni manvantarāṇi tu tāni tvam kathaya naḥ vyāsān ca dvāpare yuge veda śākhā praṇayanam devadevasya dhīmataḥ tathā avatārān dharma artham īśānasya kalau yuge uvāca manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvam tatas svārociṣaḥ manuḥ uttamaḥ tāmasaḥ ca eva raivataḥ cākṣuṣaḥ tathā ṣaṭ ete manavaḥ atītāḥ sāṃpratam tu raveḥ sutaḥ svāyaṃbhuvam tu kathitam kalpa ādau antaram mayā pārāvatāḥ ca tuṣitāḥ devāḥ svārociṣe antare vipaścit nāma devendraḥ babhūva asurasūdanaḥ ūrjastambhaḥ tathā prāṇaḥ dāntaḥ atha vṛṣabhaḥ tathā timiraḥ cārvarīvant ca sapta saptarṣayaḥ abhavan caitra kiṃpuruṣa ādyāḥ ca sutāḥ svārociṣasya tu dvitīyam a tad ākhyātam antaram śṛṇu ca uttaram suśāntiḥ tatra deva indraḥ babhūva amitra karṣaṇaḥ sudhāmānaḥ tathā satyāḥ śivāḥ ca atha pratardanāḥ mad vaśavartinaḥ ca pañca ete gaṇāḥ dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ tāmasasya antare devāḥ surāḥ satyāḥ ca sudhiyaḥ ca eva saptaviṃśatikāḥ gaṇāḥ śibiḥ indraḥ tathā eva āsīt śatayajña upalakṣaṇaḥ babhūva śaṃkare bhaktaḥ mahādeva arcane rataḥ pañcame ca api vipra indrāḥ raivataḥ nāma nāmataḥ amitābhāḥ bhūtarayāḥ vaikuṇṭhāḥ svacchamedhasaḥ hiraṇyaromā vedaśrī ūrdhvabāhuḥ tathā eva ca ca parjanyaḥ ca mahā muniḥ svārociṣaḥ ca uttamaḥ ca tāmasaḥ raivataḥ tathā priyavrata anvayāḥ hi ete catvāraḥ manavaḥ smṛtāḥ manvantare ca āsīt cākṣuṣaḥ tu manuḥ dvijāḥ ādyāḥ prasūtāḥ bhāvyāḥ ca pṛthugāḥ ca divaukasaḥ mahā anubhāvāḥ lekhyāḥ ca pañca ete hi aṣṭakāḥ gaṇāḥ sumedhāḥ virajāḥ ca eva haviṣmān uttamaḥ madhuḥ atināmā sahiṣṇuḥ ca sapta āsan ṛṣayaḥ śubhāḥ vivasvantaḥ sutaḥ viprāḥ śrāddhadevaḥ mahā dyutiḥ bhādityāḥ vasavaḥ rudrāḥ devāḥ tatra marut gaṇāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapaḥ ca atriḥ jamadagniḥ ca gautamaḥ tad aṃśa bhūtāḥ rājānaḥ sarve ca tridivaukasaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare pūrvam ākūtyām mānasaḥ sutaḥ ruceḥ prajāpateḥ yajñaḥ tad aṃśena abhavat dvijāḥ tuṣitāyām samutpannaḥ tuṣitaiḥ saha daivataiḥ satyāyām abhavat satyaḥ satya rūpaḥ janārdanaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ mānasaiḥ sārdham devaiḥ saha mahā dyutiḥ cākṣuṣe api antare ca eva vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ jajñe vāmanaḥ kaśyapāt viṣṇuḥ aditau saṃbabhūva ha tribhiḥ kramaiḥ imān lokān jitvā yena mahātmanā sapta ca eva abhavan viprāḥ yābhiḥ saṃrakṣitāḥ prajāḥ yasmāt viṣṭam idam kṛtsnam vāmanena mahātmanā tasmāt saḥ vai smṛtaḥ viṣṇuḥ viśyāḥ dhātoḥ praveśanāt eṣa sarvam sṛjati ādau pāti hanti ca keśavaḥ bhūta antarātmā bhagavān nārāyaṇaḥ iti śrutiḥ eka aṃśena jagat sarvam vyāpya nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ caturdhā saṃsthitaḥ vyāpī sa guṇaḥ nirguṇaḥ api ca ekā bhagavantaḥ mūrtiḥ jñāna rūpā śivā amalā vāsudeva abhidhānā sā guṇa atītā su niṣkalā dvitīyā kāla saṃjñā anyā tāmasī śeṣa saṃjñitā nihanti sakalam ca ante vaiṣṇavā paramā tanuḥ jagat sthāpayate sarvam sa viṣṇuḥ prakṛtiḥ dhruvā caturthaḥ vāsudevasya mūrtiḥ brāhmī iti saṃjñitā rājasā ca aniruddha ākhyā pradyumnaḥ sṛṣṭi kārakā nārāyaṇa ākhyaḥ brahmā asau karoti saḥ yā sā nārāyaṇa tanuḥ pradyumna ākhyā muni īśvarāḥ tayā saṃmohayet viśvam sa deva asura mānuṣam sā eva sarva jagat sūtiḥ prakṛtiḥ parikīrtitā ekam ca idam catuṣpādam caturdhā punar acyutaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ vyāsaḥ viṣṇuḥ nārāyaṇaḥ svayam pūrvam sva icchayā hi abhavat hariḥ anādi antam param brahma na devāḥ na ṛṣayaḥ viduḥ ekaḥ ayam veda bhagavān vyāsaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ iti etat viṣṇu māhātmyam uktam vaḥ muni puṃgavāḥ etat satyam punar satyam evam jñātvā na muhyati iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekonapañcāśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca dvitīye dvāpare ca eva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpatiḥ tṛtīye ca uśanāḥ vyāsaḥ caturthe syāt bṛhaspatiḥ savitā pañcame vyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ prakīrtitaḥ saptame ca tathā eva indraḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ ca aṣṭame mataḥ sārasvataḥ ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ ekādaśe tu trivṛṣaḥ śatatejāḥ tatas paras tryāruṇiḥ vai pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ kṛtañjayaḥ saptadaśe hi aṣṭādaśe ṛtañjayaḥ rājaśravāḥ ca ekaviṃśaḥ tasmāt śuṣmāyaṇaḥ paraḥ tṛṇabinduḥ trayoviṃśe vālmīkiḥ tad paraḥ smṛtaḥ pañcaviśe tathā śaktiḥ ṣaḍviṃśe tu parāśaraḥ saptaviṃśe tathā vyāsaḥ jātūkarṇaḥ mahā muniḥ aṣṭāviṃśe punar prāpte hi asmin vai dvāpare dvijāḥ parāśara sutaḥ vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ abhavat saḥ eva sarva vedānām purāṇānām pradarśakaḥ pārāśaryaḥ mahā yogī kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ hariḥ ārādhya devam īśānam dṛṣṭvā sa ambam trilocanam tad prasādāt asau vyāsam vedānām akarot prabhuḥ atha śiṣyān prijagrāha caturaḥ vedapāragān pailam teṣām caturtham ca pañcamam mām mahā muniḥ ṛgveda śrāvakam pailam jagrāha sa mahā muniḥ itihāsa purāṇāni pravaktum mām ayojayat prādhvaryavam yajurbhiḥ syāt ṛgbhiḥ hetram dvijottamāḥ tatas saḥ ṛcaḥ uddhṛtya ṛgvedam kṛtavan prabhuḥ yajūṃṣi ca yajurvedam sāmavedam ca sāmabhiḥ ekaviṃśati bhedena ṛgvedam kṛtavan purā śākhānām tu śatena eva yajurvedam atha akarot sāmavedam sahastreṇa śākhānām prabibheda saḥ bhedaiḥ aṣṭādaśaiḥ vyāsaḥ purāṇam kṛtavān prabhuḥ saḥ ayam ekaḥ catuṣpādaḥ vedaḥ pūrvam purātanāt oṃkāraḥ brahmaṇaḥ jātaḥ sarva doṣa viśodhanaḥ veda vākya uditam tattvam vāsudevaḥ param padam a vedam paramam vetti veda niṣṭhaḥ sadā īśvaraḥ a vedam ca vijānāti pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge pañcāśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca vedavyāsa avatārāṇi dvāpare kathitāni tu mahādeva avatārāṇi kalau śṛṇuta suvratāḥ nāmnā hitāya viprāṇām abhūt vaivasvate antare tasya śiṣyāḥ śikhā yuktāḥ vabhūvuḥ amita prabhāḥ śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaḥ ca eva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ catvāraḥ te mahātmānaḥ brāhmaṇāḥ vedapāragāḥ subhānaḥ damanaḥ ca atha suhotraḥ kaṅkaṇaḥ tathā aṣṭame dadhivāhaḥ syāt navame vṛṣabhaḥ prabhuḥ bhṛguḥ tu daśame proktaḥ tasmāt ugraḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ dvādaśe atriḥ samākhyātaḥ balī ca atha trayodaśe caturdaśe gautamaḥ tu vedaśīrṣā tatas param gokarṇaḥ ca abhavat tasmāt guhāvāsaḥ śikhaṇḍī atha baṭāmālī aṭṭahāsaḥ ca dārukaḥ lāṅgalī kramāt śvetaḥ tathā paraḥ śūlī ḍiṇḍī muṇḍī ca vai kramāt sahiṣṇuḥ somaśarmā ca nakulīśaḥ antime prabhuḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ ākhyātā hi ante kali yuge prabhoḥ tīrthe kāya avatāre syāt deveśaḥ nakulī īśvaraḥ śiṣyāḥ babhūvuḥ ca anyeṣām pratyekam muni puṃgavāḥ prasanna manasaḥ dāntāḥ aiśvarīm bhaktim āśritāḥ śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaḥ ca eva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ dundubhiḥ śatarūpaḥ ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumant tathā vikeśaḥ ca viśokaḥ ca viśāpaḥ śāpanāśanaḥ sanaḥ sanātanaḥ ca eva mukāraḥ ca sanandanaḥ dālabhyaḥ ca mahā yogī dharma ātmanaḥ mahā ojasaḥ sudhāmā virajāḥ ca eva śaṅkhapātrajaḥ eva ca sārasvataḥ tathā meghaḥ ghanavāhaḥ suvāhanaḥ kapilaḥ ca āsuriḥ ca eva voḍhuḥ pañcaśikhaḥ muniḥ parāśaraḥ ca gargaḥ ca bhārgavaḥ ca aṅgirāḥ tathā lambodaraḥ ca lambaḥ ca lāmbākṣaḥ lambakeśakaḥ kāśyapaḥ ca eva vasiṣṭhaḥ virajāḥ tathā atriḥ ugraḥ tathā ca eva śravaṇaḥ atha śraviṣṭhakaḥ kuṇiḥ ca kuṇibāhuḥ ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ utathyaḥ vāmadevaḥ ca mahākāyaḥ mahā anilaḥ vācaśravāḥ supīkaḥ ca śyāvāśvaḥ sapathīśvaraḥ hariṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyaḥ lokākṣiḥ kuthumiḥ tathā plakṣaḥ dārbhāyaṇiḥ ca eva ketumant gautamaḥ tathā śālihotraḥ agniveśyaḥ ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaḥ ca kumbhaḥ ca eva pravāhakaḥ ulūkaḥ vidyutaḥ ca eva śādvalaḥ hi āśvalāyanaḥ akṣapādaḥ kumāraḥ ca ulūkaḥ vatsaḥ eva ca śiṣyāḥ ete mahātmānaḥ yoginām vimalāḥ brahma bhūyiṣṭhāḥ jñāna yoga parāyaṇāḥ kurvanti ca avatārāṇi brāhmaṇānām hitāya hi yoga īśvarāṇām ādeśāt veda saṃsthāpanāya vai bhaviṣyati ca sāvarṇaḥ dakṣasāvarṇaḥ eva ca dvādaśaḥ rudrasāvarṇaḥ rocamānaḥ trayodaśaḥ bhautyaḥ caturdaśaḥ proktaḥ bhaviṣyāḥ manavaḥ kramāt ayam vaḥ kathitaḥ hi aṃśaḥ pūrvaḥ nārāyaṇa īritaḥ bhūta bhavyaiḥ vartamānaiḥ ākhyānaiḥ upabṛṃhitaḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api śrāvayet vā dvijottamān paṭhet devālaye snātvā nadī tīreṣu ca eva hi nārāyaṇam namaskṛtya bhāvena puruṣottamam namaḥ deva ādidevāya devānām paramātmane puruṣāya purāṇāya viṣṇave kūrma rūpiṇe iti śrī kūrmapurāṇe ṣaṭsāhastryām saṃhitāyām pūrva vibhāge ekapañcāśaḥ adhyāyaḥ
